# Project Rotation Log

Daily rotation across the 5 projects in this repo. Each day, one project
receives a "significant incremental move" вҖ” a coherent feature, polish pass,
or architectural step forward.

## Rotation order

1. Credicrew
2. LLM_Playground
3. SynapseOS
4. Titan
5. WaySafe

## Log

| Day | Date (UTC) | Project | Move |
|----:|---|---|---|
| 1 | 2026-04-19 | **WaySafe** | Built real Safety Intelligence engine (`safety.py`) вҖ” composite 0вҖ“100 score using geofences, recency- & severity-weighted incident proximity, late-night penalty, help-POI bonus. Added `pydeck` HeatmapLayer weighted by severityГ—recencyГ—verified. New `theme.py` with dark gradient, brand header, and animated score-ring card. Authority dashboard gained category & time-series breakdowns. README rewritten to match reality. |
| 2 | 2026-04-19 | **Credicrew** | Shipped the explainable match engine the architecture doc promised but nobody had built. New `frontend/src/lib/match.ts` parses free-text queries into skills/location/seniority, scores each candidate on weighted factors (skills 0.55 В· seniority 0.20 В· location 0.15 В· base 0.10), and returns a per-factor breakdown. Mirrored in `backend/app/services/match.py` with a new `POST /match` router so client and server always agree. Discover page now shows detected-plan chips, band counts, matched/missing skill chips, and a conic-gradient score ring per card. Added `MatchExplain` popover. Removed three stray duplicate files. README rewritten around the new feature. |
| 3 | 2026-04-22 | **LLM_Playground** | Turned a generic single-provider playground into a real evaluation studio. New `backend/src/pricing.py` holds published $/1M-token rates with prefix-matching so dated model ids still resolve. New `POST /api/compare` fan-outs one prompt to up to 6 provider/model candidates in parallel via `ThreadPoolExecutor`, catching per-candidate errors so a missing key never kills siblings, and computes winners (fastest, cheapest, most verbose). `GET /api/pricing` exposes the table; `/chat` now returns `cost_usd` too. Frontend gains an **Arena** mode alongside Universal/August: coloured candidate roster in the sidebar, parallel results grid with headline tiles (models В· succeeded В· wallвҖ‘time В· total $), per-card metric pills (latency/tokens/$), winner badges, one-click copy and JSON export. Fixed the mis-labeled "Deploy" header button (it was a download) вҶ’ "Export". README rewritten around Arena with a full API-surface table. |
| 4 | 2026-04-24 | **SynapseOS** | Greenfield rebuild from a 12-byte README. Stood up the whole product: a personal second-brain OS where notes auto-link via embedding-based synapses. **Backend** (FastAPI + SQLite): `embed.py` is a zero-dep 512-d hashing-trick embedder (char 4-grams + word uni/bi-grams, L2-normalized); `synapse.py` computes the graph on the fly with a cosine threshold П„ and top-K neighbor cap, plus Dijkstra-based path tracing over `1 вҲ’ strength`; `store.py` persists notes with packed-float embeddings in SQLite; `seed.py` ships a 16-note demo graph with deliberate cross-cluster bridges. Seven HTTP endpoints: `/graph`, `/neighbors`, `/search`, `/path`, plus CRUD. **Frontend** (Next.js 14 + Tailwind + react-force-graph-2d): neon dark UI with animated grain, glow halos, and gradient edges. Three-pane layout вҖ” NoteComposer / SearchBar / PathFinder on the left, canvas graph in the center with degree-scaled nodes + weight-hued glow + animated particles along highlighted paths, Inspector on the right with neighbor strength bars. Semantic search, live graph refresh on note create/delete, and path tracing that highlights the chain in amber. README rewritten from stub to full vision + architecture diagram + API table + formula. |
| 5 | 2026-04-25 | **Titan** | Tore out a leaked 124 MB `fintrace/__MACOSX` archive and replaced the AML stub with a real, deterministic, explainable engine. New `apps/ai-aml/risk.py` ships seven named detectors (structuring, velocity_spike, round_trip cycles via DFS depth вүӨ4, fan_in, fan_out, high_risk_geo on FATF-style codes, round_amount), each contributing weight Г— saturating-intensity to a 0вҖ“100 score. New `sar.py` renders a markdown SAR draft + structured payload with evidence harvested from the firing factors. Gateway gained `GET /attest/{docHash}` and `GET /attestations/recent` (event-log replay) plus an AML pass-through so the frontend has one origin. **Frontend rebuild**: dark gradient + glassmorphism Tailwind theme, brand SVG logo, custom `ScoreRing` (conic-gradient), `FactorBars`, and a deterministic-layout `TxGraph` (no charting libs). Four routes вҖ” `/` hero + flow diagram, `/aml` drag-drop CSV вҶ’ ranked accounts вҶ’ factor bars + transaction graph + one-click SAR, `/kyc` PDF dropzone with animated 3-stage pipeline + on-chain receipt, `/attestations` hash search + auto-refreshing live `Attested` feed. Untracked Hardhat build outputs and added them to `.gitignore`. READMEs rewritten вҖ” `Titan/README.md` from 8 bytes to full pitch, `titan-v2/README.md` rebuilt around the new API table, formula, and route map. |
| 6 | 2026-04-26 | **WaySafe** | Round 2 opener. The README always promised "smart navigation with safe routes" but no path planner existed вҖ” built one. New `routing.py`: pure-Python A* over a snapped lat/lon grid (~56 cells along the longest side, padded 1.5 km, 8-connected) with edge cost `haversine_km(u,v) * (1 + Оұ В· risk(midpoint))`; runs `Оұ=0` (fastest) and `Оұ=4.5` (safest) in parallel and reports length-weighted average safety, min-safety, and km of elevated-risk segments (вүҘ0.45). `to_gpx()` emits valid GPX 1.1 for any route. `safety.py` gained `point_risk()` reusing the existing safety physics, normalised to `[0,1]`, with the geofence component bumped to 38 of a 70-pt budget so detours actually fire on demo corridors. App: new "Plan Route" tab вҖ” POI dropdown / custom lat-lon, click-to-plan with parallel A*, dual `pydeck` PathLayer overlay (cyan = safest, amber = fastest), summary bar (detour %, safety gain, ETA delta, risk km avoided), two side-by-side route cards with mini conic-gradient rings + 4-stat grids + auto-generated trip notes, GPX downloads, Google Maps deeplink (down-sampled to вүӨ9 waypoints), and a "use safest as my next leg" jog. Theme: `ROUTE_ACCENT` palette (safest=#3DA9FC, fastest=#F9C440), `ws-route-grid` / card / stats / mini-ring / bar / summary helpers. Demo seed: six in-transit incidents along the AguadaвҖ“Panaji corridor вҖ” headline run produces +37% detour for +26 safety pts, dodging 2.4 km of elevated risk. |

| 8 | 2026-04-28 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-2 move: shipped the roadmap's headline item вҖ” **LLM-as-Judge auto-eval**. New `backend/src/judge.py` ships a five-criterion default rubric (Correctness 0.35 В· Completeness 0.20 В· Clarity В· Conciseness В· Format), an anti-flatter `JUDGE_SYSTEM` preamble, a strict JSON-shape prompt builder, and a paranoid `_extract_json` that tolerates ```json fences, prose preambles, and unbalanced text (depth-tracked balanced-block walk + first-fence + raw fallback). Scores are clamped to `[1,5]`, weights renormalised to sum 1, composite `ОЈ ((sвҲ’1)/4) В· wбөў` scaled to 0вҖ“100; missing verdicts get a sentinel that drops the candidate to the bottom of the leaderboard instead of crashing the UI. Two new routes: `GET /api/rubric` (default rubric for the editor) and `POST /api/judge` (orchestrates the judge call against any provider in the keychain, returns `verdicts[]`, `leaderboard[]`, `winner`, and judge-side `latency` + `cost_usd`). Frontend Arena gained: a header **Judge responses** button (gradient amberвҶ’orange) wired through `runJudge`, a collapsible rubric editor with per-row name/description/weight inputs and a live `ОЈ` chip that flips emerald when weights sum to 1, a leaderboard panel above the result grid (rank В· provider/model В· gradient bar В· composite В· rationale on hover), and a per-card score panel with a new conic-gradient `ScoreRing` (redвҶ’amberвҶ’emerald hue ramp В· trophy ribbon for the winner) plus a `ScoreBars` mini-chart of all five criteria and a quoted one-line rationale. The judge's #1 card gets a 2px amber ring + рҹҸ… *judge pick* badge alongside the existing fastest/cheapest/verbose chips. JSON export now bundles `judge: {rubric, verdicts, leaderboard, judge:{provider,model,latency,cost_usd,вҖҰ}}`. README rewritten around Judge mode with the composite formula and an updated API table; roadmap entry struck through. |
| 9 | 2026-04-29 | **SynapseOS** | Round-2 move: shipped the **cluster view** + **orphan rescue** roadmap entries. New `backend/app/community.py` ships a **greedy modularity** community detector (Newman-style agglomerative вҖ” chosen over plain LPA because synapse graphs have hub notes that collapse LPA into one giant label) and an auto-namer that scores each in-cluster term by `tf(t,c) В· (tf(t,c)/total_tf(t)) В· log(1+\|c\|)` вҖ” title tokens 3Г—, tags 2Г—, body 1Г— вҖ” so cluster names are *distinctive* rather than just frequent. Top-1 becomes the display name, top-3 are key-term chips. Same module ships `find_orphans` which scans the full embedding table per isolated note for the strongest below-threshold peer and returns the exact `nudged_П„ = max(0, sim вҲ’ 0.005)` that would attach them. Two new endpoints: `GET /communities?threshold&top_k` (`{id, name, color, size, terms[], member_ids[]}`) and `GET /orphans?threshold&top_k` (sorted by easiest-rescue first); `/graph` nodes now embed `community` + `community_color`, and stats grow a `communities` count. **Frontend**: new `TopicPalette` component (color-chipped cluster list with per-cluster name, size, three top-terms, and click-to-isolate); new `OrphanRescue` panel showing each orphan's title + suggested neighbor + similarity % + nudged П„; `Graph.tsx` rewired to paint nodes from `community_color`, draw intra-cluster edges in the cluster's own hue, fade everything outside the isolated community to 18% alpha, and add a thin white centrality ring on hub nodes. Header gains a `clusters` pill (synapse-pink). `page.tsx` parallelises `/graph + /communities + /orphans` on every refresh and clears stale isolation when a cluster vanishes. README rewritten around community discovery + orphan rescue with full Newman О”Q formula, naming formula, updated API table, and a refreshed architecture diagram; roadmap entries struck through. Frontend builds clean (`tsc --noEmit` + `next build` both green). |
| 10 | 2026-05-01 | **Titan** | Round-2 move: shipped the **sanctions screening** + **what-if simulator** roadmap entries. New `apps/ai-aml/sanctions.py` is a zero-dep fuzzy matcher вҖ” `similarity = 0.55В·token_set + 0.30В·char_3gram + 0.15В·containment` blend (each component вҲҲ [0,1]), token-set is "soft-prefix" aware so `volkov` matches `volkov-baranov` without overweighting legal-form stopwords (`Ltd / GmbH / JSC / FZE вҖҰ`), an optional `+0.05` jurisdiction prior nudges geo-aligned candidates. Walks canonical name + every alias and returns the strongest hit with the alias that produced it. Bundled watchlist `data/sanctions.json` ships 30 illustrative entries across OFAC-SDN / UN-1267 / UN-1718 / EU-CFSP / UK-OFSI; loader is path-overridable via `TITAN_WATCHLIST_PATH`. New AML factor `sanctions_hit` (weight 22) screens both subject and counterparty names against the watchlist, dedupes per entity, fires at вүҘ0.65 similarity (medium grade), intensity floor 0.55 + 0.10 per additional hit. `risk.py` now accepts `weights_override` (clamped to `[0, 60]`) and `sanctions_threshold` so callers can run what-if scenarios with full audit-trail; response echoes `effective_weights`. New endpoints: `POST /aml/sanctions/screen`, `GET /aml/sanctions/list`, both proxied through the gateway; `/aml/score` body now takes optional `weights` map. Engine version bumped to `titan-aml/1.1.0`. **Frontend**: new `/watchlist` route вҖ” paste names вҶ’ batch screen with jurisdiction prior + similarity floor sliders, per-query result cards with a hue-graded `SimilarityRing` (redвҶ’amberвҶ’teal) and component bars (token-set / char-3gram / contain / juris bonus / blended), plus a searchable browse view of the bundled list with per-entry id/aliases/list/jurisdiction/added-date. New `SimilarityRing` component (conic-gradient hue ramp by grade). AML console rebuilt: header gains a **What-if simulator** toggle that opens a per-detector slider panel (8 sliders, override pills, debounced 250ms re-score, reset button); summary tiles add a `sanctions` count; account-list rows show a sanctions chip + display name; detail panel grows a **Sanctions hits** section (per-hit ring + grade badge + list/jurisdiction/role chips + matched-alias quote + reason); sample CSV widened with `subject_name` / `counterparty_name` columns and a 12-row demo that exercises 3 sanctions matches alongside structuring / round-trip / high-risk-geo. Layout NAV grew a Watchlist tab; home page bumped to 4 cards (added Watchlist) and updated stats (8 detectors В· 30 watchlist entries). FactorBars labels include `sanctions_hit`. Fixed a pre-existing CSS build break (`border-white/12` вҶ’ `border-white/10`); added `tsconfig.tsbuildinfo` to `.gitignore`. `next build` ships clean. README rewritten around the new feature: full similarity formula, grade table, updated detector table with rebalanced weights (sanctions=22, structuring=26, velocity=16, round-trip=20), curl examples for screen + weights override, layout diagram refresh, Phase-2 sanctions roadmap entry struck through. |
| 12 | 2026-05-03 | **Credicrew** | Round-3 move: shipped the **Interview Kit** + **CSV shortlist export** roadmap items so the hiring loop now spans JD вҶ’ match вҶ’ outreach вҶ’ **interview** вҶ’ ATS handoff. New `frontend/src/lib/interview.ts` is a pure-TS engine that turns a Role's `QueryPlan` into a deterministic 4-stage interview plan. **Question bank**: 13-skill bank (React, Next.js, TypeScript, FastAPI, Python, Postgres, MongoDB, Redis, AWS, Docker, Kubernetes, PyTorch, LLM) at 1вҖ“4 prompts each (вүӨ3 used per skill, capped to dodge one-skill bloat), each prompt tagged with `signal` (which rubric dim it probes), `difficulty` (1=warm-up В· 4=stretch), and `followups`. Skill prompts route to natural stages via `SKILL_TO_STAGES` (frontend/backend/data вҶ’ technical+system_design, infra вҶ’ system_design, language вҶ’ technical), interleaved across stages so a single skill never piles up in one stage. Universal prompts cover phone-screen (3) / technical (2) / system-design (3) / behavioral (4). **Rubric** (4вҖ“7 dims): skill dims collapse duplicates (`react` + `next.js` вҶ’ one *Frontend depth* row, weighted `1.0 + 0.25В·(countвҲ’1)` so ОЈ-weight scales with depth-of-skill), plus `system_design_skill` (1.0), `communication` (0.7), `ownership` (0.7), `collaboration` (0.6), and a `scope_influence` (1.0) bonus dim for senior+ roles; trimmed to top-7, weights renormalised to sum 1.0. **Scorecard**: latest-rating-per-dim across all stages wins; composite = `ОЈ ((ratingвҲ’1)/4) В· (weight / ОЈ-rated-weight) В· 100` вҖ” half-finished interviews still produce a meaningful number because weights renormalise across rated dims. Bands: вүҘ80 strong-hire В· вүҘ65 lean-yes В· вүҘ50 mixed В· вүҘ35 lean-no В· else no-hire. `localStorage` persistence keyed `credicrew:interviews:v1`; CRUD helpers (`ensureInterview`, `setRating`, `setStageStatus`, `setStageNotes`, `addSignal`, `removeSignal`, `summarise`). Backend mirror in `backend/app/services/interview.py` ships the same banks/dims/formula; new `routers/interview.py` exposes `POST /interview/plan` (JD or pre-parsed plan вҶ’ rubric + questions + empty stages) and `POST /interview/score` (rubric + stages вҶ’ composite + recommendation + per-dim breakdown). Engine version bumped to `0.4.0`. **Frontend workspace** at `/roles/[id]/interview/[candidateId]`: full-bleed dark canvas with stage stepper (per-stage status pill + question count + rated/total chip + per-stage tone), recommendation ring (124 px conic-gradient hue-ramped redвҶ’amberвҶ’skyвҶ’indigoвҶ’emerald with composite + recommendation chip + rated-count caption + striped state when empty), per-stage panel with stage-tone-coloured numeric badge + status segmented control + collapsible question cards (difficulty/signal/source pills + amber follow-up disclosure) + per-stage rubric panel with `RubricSlider` rows (1вҖ“5 buttons coloured by rating, weight chip, on-bar/above-bar semantics, click-again to clear) + per-stage signal log (strength/concern toggles + quick-add + per-row delete) + composite breakdown bar chart (indigoвҶ’emerald gradient, weight chips, rated/unrated dim distinction). Markdown report export (`Export report (.md)`) writes a structured debrief with rubric В· strengths В· concerns В· per-stage notes. **Role-detail integration**: every shortlist row now carries an `iv В· <composite>` chip in the candidate's recommendation tone the moment any rating exists, plus an *Open / Start interview* violet-tone button next to Outreach/Remove; new `Export CSV` action in the title row writes `shortlist_<role>.csv` with id/name/role/location/status/note/match-score/matched-skills/missing-skills/interview-composite/interview-recommendation/interview-rated/interview-total вҖ” closing the *CSV export for ATS handoff* roadmap item. New components: `InterviewStepper`, `QuestionCard`, `RubricSlider`, `RecommendationRing`. Tiny `lib/csv.ts` (RFC-4180 quoting + Blob downloader). README rewritten around the new feature with formula, stage table, and the two new endpoints in the API map; both interview-kit and CSV-export roadmap entries struck through. `tsc --noEmit` + `next build` both green (interview workspace = 5.16 kB / 113 kB First Load); end-to-end backend round-trip validated against a pre-parsed plan, a JD-driven plan, and an empty-payload scorecard. |
| 14 | 2026-05-05 | **SynapseOS** | Round-3 move: shipped the roadmap's flagship AI item вҖ” **Chat with your graph**, a graph-aware RAG that uses the synapse network itself as the retriever and shows the user the exact synapses that contributed. New `backend/app/chat.py` runs a four-stage retriever: (1) **seed** = top-`k_seed` cosine hits against the query; (2) **expand** = up to 2 hops along the *same* synapses the canvas renders, capped at `top_k` fan-out per node, gated by an `EXPANSION_FLOOR=0.10` strength floor and a `0.85^hop` decay; (3) **anchor** = the highest-weight note in each seed's auto-detected community as a topic anchor (skipped when redundant with seed/synapse hits); (4) **answer** with strict inline `[#N]` citations. Composite score for synapse hits: `(s В· s_seed В· 0.85^hop) + 0.4 В· cosine(q, neighbour)`. `_query_terms` splits hyphenated tokens (e.g. `retrieval-augmented` вҶ’ `retrieval`, `augmented`) so multi-word concepts still match body prose. Returns a `Traversal` carrying the original semantic seeds + the exact `(src, dst, strength, kind)` expansions, filtered to citations that survived MAX_CITATIONS=12 ranking. **Default extractive answerer** (zero new deps) scores every sentence in the citations by `(query-hits В· 1.4) / length_norm + 0.6 / (rank+1)` and bullet-lists up to 5, one per citation when possible; if nothing matches lexically, falls back to a "your strongest matches wereвҖҰ" summary so the answer never claims more than the data supports. **Optional LLM mode** via stdlib-only `app/llm.py` (`urllib.request` only вҖ” no `anthropic`/`openai` SDK pulled in) supports both Anthropic Messages and OpenAI-compatible Chat Completions; sniffed from `SYNAPSE_LLM_PROVIDER` / `SYNAPSE_LLM_KEY` / `SYNAPSE_LLM_MODEL`; defaults to `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`. System prompt enforces "answer ONLY from these notes, cite inline as `[#N]`, say so plainly if missing"; on any 5xx / network / decode failure we silently fall back to extractive with a UI notice. Two new endpoints: `GET /chat/status` (probe LLM availability) and `POST /chat` (the RAG itself); engine version bumped to `0.2.0`. **Frontend**: new `ChatPanel.tsx` lives above the Inspector вҖ” transcript with per-turn user-bubble + answer-body + per-citation row (role-tinted icon: в—Һ match / вҶқ synapse / вҳ… anchor + role pill + "via #N В· X%" provenance line + 2-line snippet + score), inline `[#N]` markers rendered as clickable chips that jump the Inspector to the note, mode chips (auto / extractive / LLM вҖ” last disabled when no key), 0/1/2 hops segmented control, mini-`**bold**` renderer for the extractive fallback's title-emphasis, "thinkingвҖҰ" shimmer bar (`@keyframes ws-shimmer`), suggestion chips on empty state, transcript auto-scroll, and a "replay" button per turn that re-projects that turn's traversal onto the canvas. **Graph**: gained a second highlight set (`chatTraversalEdges` + `chatTraversalNodes`) вҖ” synapse expansions paint cyan with 3-particle animation (vs. the path tracer's amber 4-particle), participating nodes get a thin cyan halo just outside the core (suppressed when selection ring fires); existing path-tracer highlights still win z-order so the two annotations never blur. **Header**: new "traversal active" pulse pill. Page wires the chat traversal into the canvas, clears highlights on note delete, and re-uses citation clicks вҶ’ Inspector. Frontend `tsc --noEmit` + `next build` both green (12.4 kB / 99.7 kB First Load, +5.5 kB for the panel). Backend FastAPI test-client smoke validated all paths: `/health`, `/chat/status`, `POST /chat` extractive (seeds + 5 synapse expansions), 2-hop expansion (7 expansions), forced-LLM fallback with notice, 422 on empty query / bad mode. README rewritten around the new feature: composite-score formula, four-stage retrieval diagram, env-var table, full API table updated, layout diagram refreshed to add chat.py + llm.py + ChatPanel, roadmap entry struck through; quick-start gained an LLM-mode block. |
| 13 | 2026-05-04 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-3 move: shipped the README's flagged "next move" вҖ” **Persisted runs as a queryable history**, plus a side-by-side **diff** view that wasn't on the roadmap but completes the loop. New `backend/src/history.py` is a pure-`sqlite3` store (SQLAlchemy-free вҖ” judge.py/pricing.py are zero-dep too, didn't want to drag a session pattern in for one table). Schema: payload JSON column for the heavyweight (`results`, `verdicts`, `leaderboard`, `winners`) + 14 indexed scalar mirrors for everything we filter/sort on (`created_at`, `prompt_hash`, `models` CSV fingerprint, `n_candidates`, `n_success`, `total_cost_usd`, `wall_latency`, `fastest_model`, `cheapest_model`, `judged`, `judge_provider`, `judge_model`, `judge_winner`, `judge_top_score`, `tag`, `note`, `starred`) вҖ” fast under thousands of rows without paying the JSON1 indexing tax. Public API: `save_run`, `update_judge`, `list_runs` (8 composable AND filters: `q` substring across prompt+system+models, `model`/`provider`, `judged_only`, `starred_only`, `tag`, `since`/`before` epoch, `limit`/`offset`), `get_run`, `set_meta`, `delete_run`, `stats`, `diff`. Per-call sqlite connection with a process-wide `threading.Lock`; init runs at import time and is idempotent. **Wiring**: `/api/compare` now writes a row at the end of every fan-out (best-effort вҖ” a save error is logged but never 500s the run); `/api/judge` accepts an optional `run_id` and retro-attaches its verdict to the persisted row, so judging is a non-destructive append. Six new endpoints: `GET /api/history` (paginated list), `GET /api/history/<run_id>` (full payload), `POST /api/history/<run_id>/meta` (tag/note/starred), `DELETE /api/history/<run_id>`, `GET /api/history/stats` (total runs В· total $ В· judged count В· avg top score В· top-8 winners + top-8 appearances), `POST /api/history/diff` (side-by-side comparator that indexes both runs by `provider:model`, returns shared/a-only/b-only model lists + per-model deltas; `b - a` everywhere with a `safe_delta` that returns None on type mismatch). End-to-end Flask test-client smoke validated (list/get/meta/stats/delete/diff/404/400 all green). **Frontend**: new `components/HistoryPanel.jsx` is a self-contained 4-zone surface вҖ” stats banner (5 gradient tiles + Top judge winners ribbon with appearance counts), filter row (search input with leading icon, 3 provider toggle pills with provider-coloured dots, judged/starred Switches, reset chip; debounced 250ms refetch), 12-col grid with run list (left) and detail/diff pane (right). Run rows: per-row 0-100 conic `MiniRing` (judge composite if scored, neutral Bot icon otherwise) + provider-coloured dot strip + prompt preview line-clamped to 2 + meta strip (rel time В· n_candidates В· success ratio В· total $ В· judge winner with ribbon В· tag pill) + star toggle. **Cmd/Ctrl + click** pins a second row as the diff partner; primary click selects for inspection. Detail pane: title bar (large ring В· prompt В· abs time В· winner ribbon) + 3 action buttons (**Re-run** loads prompt+system+candidate roster back into Arena and toasts; **Compare withвҖҰ** + clear; **Delete**) + tag/note row with save-on-button + replays the Arena cards (`ResultMiniCard` matches Arena visual language: provider chip В· score ring + rationale В· response body В· 3-metric footer В· winner badges) + judge leaderboard with hue-graded gradient bars. **Diff view** (drops in when both A and B are pinned): violet headline banner with prompt previews + 4 `DiffStat` tiles (`wall_latency`, `total_cost`, `n_success`, `judge_top_score` вҖ” each with A вҶ’ B values + colour-flipped `Delta` chip where lower-is-better metrics show emerald-up/rose-down correctly: green up-arrow always means "B improved over A") + shared/a-only/b-only chips + per-shared-model `DiffMetric` row (latency В· cost В· response chars В· composite). | 11 | 2026-05-02 | **WaySafe** | Round-3 opener. Closed a silently-broken promise вҖ” Day 6's "Plan Route" tab was committed in *name* only: `routing.py`, `safety.point_risk`, and the route-compare theme helpers all shipped but `app.py` was never wired, so the README's headline feature didn't exist in the running app вҖ” **and** delivered the README's last big roadmap item: **incident prediction**, without an XGBoost dep. New `forecast.py` is a pure-Python empirical-Bayes spatiotemporal hazard model. Historical hazards are binned by ВҪ-km cell Г— DOW Г— hour with weight `severity Г— verified_bump Г— recency_decay(14-day half-life)`; a separable triangular kernel (0.45В·1.0В·0.45 over hour, 0.35В·1.0В·0.35 over DOW) smooths counts across the 3Г—3 (DOW, hour) neighbourhood so a single Saturday 22:00 incident bleeds softly into Friday/Sunday and 21:00/23:00. Empirical-Bayes posterior `О»МӮ(c,t) = (k_{c,t} + ОұВ·ПҖ_t) / (kernel_mass + Оұ)` against a per-bucket city prior `ПҖ_t = ОЈ_c k_{c,t} / N_cells` вҖ” sparse cells shrink toward the city-wide rate at that hour instead of getting a coin-flip estimate. Risk is Poisson-saturated: `risk = 1 вҲ’ exp(вҲ’Оә В· О»МӮ)`, Оә=0.85, Оұ=3.0. Public API: `risk_at`, `forecast` (with confidence + cell-conditional category mix smoothed toward the global prior + WHY explainer lines), `risk_curve` (24 hourly), `risk_grid` (HeatmapLayer-ready), `hotspots`, `find_best_window`, `summary`. **Routing**: new `plan_forecast_route` reuses the existing A\* but the edge cost folds in expected risk at the time the traveler will reach each midpoint вҖ” `t_arrive = depart + cum_km / 32 km/h` вҖ” blended 65/35 with current-time `point_risk` so geofences and *currently active* incidents still count even when the historical model is sparse for that bucket. `_astar` was generalised to accept either a `risk_fn(lat, lon)` (current-time) or a `risk_fn_t(lat, lon, km_at_u)` (forecast-time) hook, with a parallel `g_km` table for cumulative ETA tracking. New `find_best_departure` sweeps Вұ2 h at 30-min resolution and ranks candidates by `0.7В·avg_safety + 0.3В·min_safety`. `RouteResult` grew `depart_at`, `arrive_at`, and `eta_at_node`. **App** got a major restructure: 7-tab Tourist layout (Map В· **Plan Route** В· **Forecast** В· Report В· Alerts В· SOS В· Trip). The Plan Route tab is the long-promised one finally wired in вҖ” POI dropdown / custom lat-lon, depart-at picker, parallel A\* + optional forecast-aware run, summary bar (detour %, safety gain, time cost, risk km avoided), dual route cards with mini conic-gradient rings, dual-route map overlay (cyan safest / amber fastest / purple forecast-aware), GPX downloads, Google-Maps deeplinks (down-sampled to вүӨ9 waypoints), and a "Find best departure window" expander. The Forecast tab pairs a Now / Custom hour-slider with a headline forecast card (conic-gradient risk ring coloured by 4-stop ramp + confidence pill + О»МӮ + cell-obs metric + category chips + WHY explainer), a 24-h bar curve coloured per-bar by ramp with peak-hour glow + lightweight axis, an expected-category bar list (top-3, 0вҖ“100%), a forecast HeatmapLayer at user-centred bbox (~7 km radius, 48Г—48 lattice) with custom 6-stop colour ramp greenвҶ’amberвҶ’coralвҶ’pinkвҶ’purple, and a top-5 hotspots row with rank chips and per-row top-hazard. Authority dashboard gained a "next-24 hours" forecast curve at the top-cell-per-hour + likely hotspots at the predicted peak. **Theme**: `ROUTE_ACCENT['forecast-safest']` purple `#A78BFA`, `FORECAST_RAMP` 4-stop palette (`#53E3A6 вҶ’ #F9C440 вҶ’ #FF6A3D вҶ’ #FF3D60`), `forecast_color()` helper, full new CSS surface вҖ” `ws-fc-card` (purpleвҶ’teal gradient + side-by-side ring + chips), `ws-fc-ring`, `ws-fc-pill` (high/medium/low/cat variants), `ws-fc-bars` + `ws-fc-bar.peak`, `ws-fc-cat` rows, `ws-fc-window` recommendation card with delta-vs-your-time row builder, `ws-hotspot-row` ranked grid. | 19 | 2026-05-11 | **SynapseOS** | Round-4 move: shipped the **Daily Brief** вҖ” a spaced-revisit engine that fights the PKM failure mode every other tool ignores (notes get written once, never re-read). New `backend/app/revisit.py` is a pure-stdlib composite scorer: `score = 0.55В·staleness + 0.25В·centrality + 0.30В·orphan_bonus вҲ’ 0.20В·same_cluster_picks + jitter(note_id Г— YYYY-MM-DD вҲҲ Вұ0.05)`. **Staleness** is a piecewise curve вҖ” 0 below a day, linear ramp 0вҶ’1 across days 1вҖ“14, holds at 1.0 through day 60, decays linearly to a 0.65 floor by day 180 (very-old notes still surface, just less urgently). **Centrality** = `0.55В·degree_norm + 0.45В·weight` (reuses the synapse graph's existing hub signal so the brief doesn't compute a parallel PageRank). **Orphan bonus** is flat additive at 0.30 вҖ” isolated notes need attention before П„ drifts and they become invisible. **Diversity** is greedy: at each pick we subtract `0.20 Г— same_cluster_picks_so_far` before re-comparing, so a hot topic can't monopolize the K=5 budget; surface stats report `clusters_touched`. **Jitter** is keyed by SHA256(`note_id|YYYY-MM-DD`) вҶ’ uint64 вҶ’ centered into Вұ0.05, so the brief is *idempotent within a day* (page reload = same picks) and reshuffles tie-breaks across days without dragging the scoring physics into randomness. Each pick carries a **journal prompt** templated against the note's cluster name + top distinctive term ("How does *X* connect to *Y* in the *embeddings* cluster?"; orphans get "Where does *X* belong?"; very-old notes get "You wrote this N days ago вҖ” what would you change today?") and up to **2 cross-cluster bridge suggestions** вҖ” notes from *other* communities with cosine вүҘ 0.20 (same-cluster needs вүҘ 0.30 since those already light up in the synapse view); diversification dedupes per cluster so we never show two suggestions from the same neighborhood. **Store**: SQLite gained a nullable `last_seen_at` column with an idempotent `PRAGMA table_info`-gated `ALTER TABLE` for old DBs; two new helpers (`touch_note(id, when=None)` returns False on 404, `last_seen_map()` for batch reads). Reasons strip is ordered by contribution-weight descending so the dominant cause reads first; staleness reasons humanise ("3 days since touched" / "2 weeks since touched" / "4 months since touched"). Two new endpoints: `GET /brief?k=&date=&threshold=&top_k=` (defaults to today UTC, k=5; returns date В· picks[note_id/title/snippet/tags/score/reasons[]/prompt/connections[]/cluster_*/days_since_seen/is_orphan] В· stats; 422 on kвҲү[1,12]) and `POST /notes/{id}/touch` (refreshes `last_seen_at` to now, returns new timestamp, 404 on missing note). `NoteOut` schema gained optional `last_seen_at`. **Frontend**: new `DailyBrief.tsx` (~430 lines) вҖ” full-screen modal with backdrop blur + grid-fade overlay, header strip carrying date + cluster-touched stat + esc-to-close hint, single-card carousel (one pick at a time keeps the experience focused вҖ” the brief is meant to *replace* scrolling not add another scroll surface), `ScoreВӯRing` conic-gradient ring painted in the pick's cluster colour, cluster + orphan + seen pills, title + snippet + tag chips, weight-ordered reason chips (в—· amber stale В· вңҰ violet central В· в—Ӣ pink orphan В· вӨ¬ cyan diverse), violet-rimmed **journal prompt** card with blurred radial corner accent, **bridges to consider** list with cross-cluster cosine % chips and per-row click to inspect, dual CTAs (`open in graph вҶ’` selects the note and closes the modal; `mark seen` updates `last_seen_at` and flips the pill to вң“ seen), footer with prev/next + per-pick dots (cyan = current В· lime = touched В· slate = untouched) + `mark all seen` (parallelised `Promise.all` over remaining picks), keyboard nav (`вҶҗ` / `вҶ’` between picks, `Esc` to close). | 18 | 2026-05-10 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-4 opener: shipped the README's flagged "Blind A/B voting вҶ’ ELO leaderboard across saved runs" вҖ” turning the playground into a personal LMSYS-style arena fed by your own runs. New `backend/src/vote_arena.py` is a pure-`sqlite3` module sharing the existing `history.db` file (the `votes` table slides in alongside `runs`, single-backup captures everything). Schema: 14 indexed scalar columns (`id`, `created_at`, `run_id`, `prompt_hash`, `prompt_preview`, `model_a`, `model_b`, `winner вҲҲ {a,b,tie,both_bad}`, `voter`, `judge_winner`, `latency_a/b`, `cost_a/b`). **ELO replay is the single source of truth** вҖ” every leaderboard call walks `votes ORDER BY created_at` and reapplies one update per vote, so deleting a misclick rewinds it cleanly and changing K reshapes the ranking without losing data. Math: `expected_a = 1 / (1 + 10^((rating_b вҲ’ rating_a) / 400))`, `rating_a' = rating_a + K В· (score_a вҲ’ expected_a)`; K=24 (FIDE-blitz default, env `LLM_ELO_K`), prior=1500 (env `LLM_ELO_PRIOR`), tie вҶ’ 0.5/0.5, **both-bad вҶ’ no rating change** (no information either way). Pair sampler walks the 60 newest runs newest-first, enumerates every cross-pair, scores each by play-count (lowest first вҶ’ bias towards under-played match-ups so a power-voter doesn't see the same pair twice), shortcuts to any 0-play pair found. Anonymisation is server-side: provider/model are stripped from the response sides and the truth lives under `_truth` until the vote POST. Engine surface: `record_vote`, `delete_vote`, `pick_pair`, `pick_pair_from_run`, `leaderboard` (returns rank В· rating В· games В· W/L/T В· win_rate В· avg_opp_rating В· last_played В· 8-char `recent_form` of `WLTB`), `pair_matrix` (top-NГ—N head-to-head with proper canonical-pair flipping), `recent_votes`, `agreement` (judge vs human вҖ” for every decisive vote on a judged run, did the human's pick match the judge's #1?), `stats`. Two further panels: a 12-col **leaderboard** with `RankRibbon` (рҹҘҮ/рҹҘҲ/рҹҘү for top-3, `#N` after), per-row mini gradient bar showing rating relative to prior (anchored 0% at priorвҲ’50, 100% at prior+250), `FormStrip` (last 8 results as colour-coded W/L/T/B chips), per-row hue-graded win-rate; and an 8Г—8 **head-to-head matrix** (`Matrix` component) with hue-graded cells via `hsl(0вҶ’120, 75%, 45%)`, proper canonical-pair flipping (A/B order at vote-time isn't what the row/col order necessarily matches, so the lookup mirrors via `100 вҲ’ wr`), per-cell win-rate% + games count + tooltip. | 20 | 2026-05-12 | **Titan** | Round-4 move: shipped **Network Intelligence** вҖ” turning the per-account AML scorer into a networked one that catches the patterns single-account scoring misses. New `apps/ai-aml/network.py` (~620 lines, pure stdlib) does three things. (1) **Entity resolution** via Union-Find: two parties are merged if **either** their names blend вүҘ 0.78 on the watchlist matcher's own building blocks (token-set 0.55 В· char-3gram 0.30 В· containment 0.15, with the same legal-form `STOPWORDS` strip so `Ltd`/`GmbH`/`JSC` don't inflate Jaccard, and single-token names need an exact normalised match) **OR** their counterparty-fingerprint Jaccard вүҘ 0.55 (both parties must have вүҘ3 counterparties and share вүҘ3, so a single shared payee doesn't collapse the graph). The transitive closure runs Union-Find with iterative path compression. (2) **Biased PageRank propagation**: `r вҶҗ (1вҲ’Оұ)В·s + ОұВ·WбөҖВ·r` with Оұ=0.7, where `s` is the L1-normalised seed-risk vector (per-cluster max of contained-account `risk_score`) and `W[i,j] = amount(iвҶ’j) / ОЈ amount(iвҶ’*)`. Dangling-row mass teleports back to the seed per iteration (standard dead-end fix). Converges in вүӨ20 iter on demo data; cap=30, tol=1e-5. Final per-entity `network_risk = 0.55В·risk_score + 0.45В·100В·(r/max r)` вҖ” the 55/45 blend keeps per-account signal visible while letting peer-tainted "clean by themselves" nodes lift visibly, which is the *inversion* this layer is meant to expose. (3) **Counterfactual + attribution**: `counterfactual(ablate)` drops every transaction touching any party in the ablated cluster set, reruns the full pipeline, and returns per-entity {risk_before, risk_after, network_before, network_after, deltas} sorted by network_delta. `attribution(account)` runs leave-one-counterparty-out вҖ” for each partner, drop every transaction between the two, rescore, report the drop in `risk_score`. Simplest possible SHAP-style explanation: marginal contribution under a leave-one-out coalition, fully auditable. Layout uses a deterministic Fruchterman-Reingold variant computed server-side (SHA-seeded golden-ratio spiral init вҶ’ 80 iter of repulsion `kВІ/dВІ` + edge attraction `dВІ/k В· (0.4 + 0.6В·w/maxW)` + 0.04 centre-gravity + linear cooling), so the frontend renders to the returned `(x,y)` immediately вҖ” no client-side simulation, no flicker. Truncation caps at 80 nodes / 200 edges ranked by sanctioned вҶ’ risk вҶ’ activity, so a clipped view never silently drops the most important signal. Four new endpoints exposed on both ai-aml and the gateway: `GET /aml/network/rules`, `POST /aml/network/analyze`, `POST /aml/network/counterfactual`, `POST /aml/network/attribution`; engine bumped to `titan-aml/1.3.0`. **Frontend**: new `/network` route (~570 lines) with full input zone (drag-drop CSV, paste textarea, reset-to-sample), 5-tile stats banner (resolved entities / aggregate clusters / avg network lift / components + density / top-lift entity), main 1.55:1 split (large `RiskGraph` left, sortable entity sidebar right). New `RiskGraph.tsx` is a pure-SVG force-graph that consumes pre-laid coordinates: nodes hue-coded by band, sized 8 + 18В·(network_risk/100), aggregate clusters get a 2.2px ring, sanctioned ones get a radial rose halo, the focus/hover node gets a teal aura that highlights direct neighbours (everything outside fades to 28% alpha), edge widths scale 0.7 + 3.6В·(amount/maxAmt), curved Q-paths so two-way flows don't overlap, focused edges flip to the brand tealвҶ’violet gradient and surface `вӮ№amount` labels mid-arc, ablated edges fade to 18% with a 4-4 dasharray, plus a 4-tone legend pinned to the bottom-right. New `EntityCard.tsx` is the sidebar row: 44px conic-gradient mini-ring (network_risk%В·3.6deg) with band-coloured core, name + member-count pill + sanctions pill, flag chips (truncated to 4), per-row ablation toggle (`вҲ’` button flips to `вң“` on click, rose-tinted background when active). New `DeltaBar.tsx` is a diverging-bar (centered on a 50/50 midline, fills outward toward teal for negative deltas / amber for positive). Sort dropdown supports network/risk/lift/flow. Below the graph sits the **Counterfactual** panel вҖ” a violetвҶ’teal gradient banner with the network avg before/after, the alerted-count flip, the txs_removed count, and a per-entity delta table (12 rows, with DeltaBar + signed О” in matching tone). Selecting any entity opens a 1:1.4 split: detail card (84px `ScoreRing`, member list for aggregates, 3 stat tiles, flag chips, net flow, plus a violet "in current counterfactual" callout when the selection appears in the active counterfactual response) and **Attribution** card (baseline score, per-counterparty `ws-net-attrib-row` with `ws-net-attrib-bar` gradient amberвҶ’orange, signed lift). `useSearchParams()` reads `?focus=вҖҰ` so the AML console can deep-link to the network with a selected account. The AML console's `selectedReport` actions gained a `Network вҶ’` button next to `Copy JSON`, and the header gained a top-level `Network view вҶ’` link. Layout NAV grew a `Network` tab between AML Console and Cases. Home page bumped to 6 feature cards on a 3-col xl grid (added Network Intelligence with a cyanвҶ’violet accent and "Open graph" CTA) and 5 stats tiles (added `Graph propagation Оұ 0.7`). 9 new CSS selectors in globals.css (`ws-net-stat` + 3 colour variants with radial corner blurs, `ws-net-row` + `-sel` + `-ablated` (the ablated state gets a repeating 135deg dashed background), `ws-net-ring` + `-core`, `ws-net-pill-agg` violet + `-san` rose, `ws-net-flag` mono chip, `ws-net-ablate` toggle with rose hover ramp, `ws-net-attrib-row` 1:4:1 grid with bottom-border separators, `ws-net-attrib-bar` gradient amberвҶ’orange, `ws-net-cf-banner` with a violetвҶ’teal gradient and a blurred radial corner spot). New `lib/api.ts` types: `NetEntity`, `NetEdge`, `NetworkAnalyze`, `NetworkDelta`, `NetworkCounterfactual`, `AttributionContribution`, `NetworkAttribution`; three new methods: `analyzeNetwork`, `counterfactualNetwork`, `attributionNetwork`. **Validation**: end-to-end FastAPI `TestClient` smoke validated 11 scenarios вҖ” `/aml/network/rules` 200 with the entity_resolution + propagation + layout + caps blocks; empty `transactions` 422 from pydantic; `/aml/network/analyze` against the AML console's named sample correctly produces 7 entities + 5 edges with **1 aggregate cluster merging M1/M2/M3 into 'Trident Exports'** (display_name resolved from the counterparty_name field); top_lift_entity_id=A2 (round-trip pulls A2 up the most); `/aml/network/counterfactual` rejecting empty ablate, ablating A3 removes 1 tx and surfaces correct deltas, **ablating B (the round-trip middle node) drops alerted from 3вҶ’1** вҖ” exactly the inversion the feature exists to demonstrate; `/aml/network/attribution` for unknown account returns 200 with `note='account not found in baseline'` (graceful), and for A2 correctly identifies counterparty B as the single biggest lift (14.7) and C as second (8.3) вҖ” exactly the cycle structure. `/healthz` reports `titan-aml/1.3.0`. | 21 | 2026-05-13 | **WaySafe** | Round-4 move: shipped the **Multi-Stop Itinerary Planner** вҖ” the next-up roadmap entry that turns the previously single-destination app into the "one tourist day, many stops, one safe schedule" tool tourists actually need. New `itinerary.py` (~360 lines, pure stdlib + reuse) is the engine: `Stop` (name/lat/lon/dwell_min), `Leg` (route + depart/arrive), and `ItineraryPlan` (legs + roll-up properties вҖ” `total_km`, `total_travel_min`, `total_dwell_min`, `total_minutes`, `arrive_at`, `avg_safety` km-weighted, `min_safety` worst-leg, `danger_km`, `danger_legs` count, `composite_score`). **Order solver** is an open-path TSP variant вҖ” start fixed (the user), tail free, no return-to-origin: greedy nearest-neighbour over the haversine distance matrix seeds the order, then a clean **2-opt** refinement reverses every sub-tour `best[i:j]` (including the tail, `j == n`) until no improvement, capped at 12 stops to keep latency snappy. (For вүҘ13 stops we keep NN only, still useful.) The 2-opt was carefully reviewed: dead `a/b/c/d` edge variables stripped, tail-reversal branch made reachable, single `_tour_length` cached per candidate. **Per-leg planning** routes each segment through the existing `plan_safest_route` / `plan_fastest_route` / `plan_forecast_route` so the same risk-aware A* with the same Оұ=4.5 prices the chain вҖ” and crucially the forecast-aware variant cascades the depart time: `leg_k.depart = leg_{kвҲ’1}.arrive + dwell_{kвҲ’1}`, so every midpoint is timed correctly along the day. **Composite score** is `clip(ОЈ(km_i В· avg_safety_i)/ОЈ km_i вҲ’ 6В·#(legs with min_safety<35), 0, 100)` вҖ” a km-weighted average with a 6-point penalty per danger spike, so a single bad leg can't get hidden behind 4 safe ones. **`find_best_start_window(stops, around, mode, span_h=2, step_min=30)`** sweeps Вұ2 h at 30-min resolution, re-plans the *full* itinerary at each candidate (9 total), ranks by composite, returns the sorted list. **Exports**: `to_combined_gpx` (one `<trk>` per leg + `<wpt>` per stop), and a proper **RFC-5545 `to_ics`** вҖ” VCALENDAR with one VEVENT per leg (`SUMMARY: рҹҡ— From вҶ’ To`, mode/km/ETA/safety in DESCRIPTION, `GEO:lat;lon` for calendar deep-link, `CATEGORIES:TRAVEL`) and one VEVENT per dwell (`CATEGORIES:DWELL`), CRLF-folded at 75 chars, comma/semicolon/backslash/newline escaped per spec, floating local times so Apple/Google/Outlook show the events at the planned hour regardless of device TZ. **UI** (new tab between *Plan Route* and *Live Trip*; | 22 | 2026-05-14 | **Credicrew** | Round-5 opener: shipped the **Offer Studio** вҖ” closes the JD вҶ’ match вҶ’ outreach вҶ’ interview вҶ’ decision вҶ’ *offer* loop with the missing money + math layer. New `frontend/src/lib/offer.ts` is a pure-TS engine with three concerns: (1) **deterministic compensation benchmark** вҖ” P25/P50/P75/P90 base bands derived from a Bengaluru-normalised seniority anchor (intern 6 В· junior 14 В· mid 26 В· senior 48 В· staff 82 В· principal 135 В· lead 70 LPA) Г— a city multiplier (Bengaluru 1.00 В· Mumbai 1.05 В· Pune 0.92 В· Kochi 0.78 В· Remote 0.95 вҖҰ) Г— `(1 + skill_premium)`. Premium = +4% per rare matched skill (Rust / Kubernetes / Terraform / PyTorch / Kafka / LLM / gRPC / Pulsar / Wasm), +1.5% per modern-stack signal (TS / FastAPI / Next.js / Postgres / React / Go / GraphQL вҖҰ), capped at 20%. Spread P25 = P50Г—0.82, P75 = P50Г—1.18, P90 = P50Г—1.36. Equity bands by seniority (intern 0% В· senior 0.10вҖ“0.30% В· staff 0.25вҖ“0.65% В· principal 0.50вҖ“1.40% вҖҰ), target-bonus % by seniority (intern 0 вҶ’ principal 18), and a suggested sign-on = `min(P50Г—0.12, (P75вҲ’P50)Г—0.5)` so the auto-fill covers half the P50вҶ’P75 gap. (2) **Win-probability logistic** вҖ” `logit = -0.6 + 3.5В·(base/P50 вҲ’ 1) + 0.8В·(equity/P50 вҲ’ 1) + 1.8В·(signOn/base) + 1.2В·(bonusвҲ’market)/100 вҲ’ 0.18В·rare_skills вҲ’ 0.45В·top_tier вҲ’ 0.2В·(daysвҲ’7)/7 вҲ’ 0.5В·thin_data вҲ’ 0.25В·low_confidence + 0.4В·(compositeвҲ’60)/100 + (matchвҲ’60)/200`. Пғ(logit) вҶ’ probability, banded `long_shot/<25 В· uphill/25-45 В· coin_flip/45-65 В· likely/65-85 В· lock/вүҘ85`. Every term reported with its delta so the UI can render signed contribution bars. (3) **Markdown offer-letter composer** вҖ” headline, candidate salutation, two-column comp table (base В· target bonus % В· sign-on В· equity В· vesting `Ny + Nmo cliff` В· start date), benchmarking note (band position + full P25/P50/P75/P90 line in Indian numbering вҖ” `вӮ№51 LPA` format with proper thousand separators via `_inr_fmt`), optional notes, sign-off. Auto-save persists drafts to localStorage `credicrew:offers:v1` keyed `${roleId}:${candidateId}`. **Backend mirror** in `app/services/offer.py` (333 LOC, pure stdlib `math`+dataclasses, no extra deps) is byte-for-byte parity with the TS engine вҖ” confirmed by side-by-side smoke for the senior/Bengaluru/(fastapi+postgres+kubernetes) case: both compute anchor 48 В· mult 1.0 В· premium 0.07 В· P50 51. New `app/routers/offer.py` exposes 4 endpoints (`POST /offer/benchmark В· /simulate В· /compose В· /full`), each accepting both `snake_case` (curl-style) and `camelCase` (TS-engine `as_dict`) draft fields via `Field(alias=вҖҰ)` + `ConfigDict(populate_by_name=True)`. API version bumped 0.5.0 вҶ’ 0.6.0; root payload extended with the four new endpoint advertisements. **Frontend Offer Studio** at `/roles/[id]/offer/[candidateId]` (12.1 kB В· 119 kB First Load): gradient title row + 4 headline tiles (accept-probability В· base salary В· total comp P50 В· equity grant), then a 12-col grid вҖ” left 5 cols hold the new **CompLadder** component (vertical gradient track with tick lines at P25/P50/P75/P90, an offer marker that slides to its band position with a violet glow, three pill chips for equity-P50 + target-bonus + sign-on hint, and the rationale bullets) above the **counterfactual controls** (4 sliders with custom Tailwind range thumbs styled in `globals.css`, market-anchor tick labels at P25/P50/P75/P90, date/number inputs for start / expiry / vesting / cliff, company name + hiring manager + notes textarea, `Reset to suggested` chip). Right 7 cols hold the new **WinProbabilityDial** (220В° SVG arc with `linearGradient` roseвҶ’indigoвҶ’emerald, hue-coded centre value, band tick lines at 25/45/65/85, drop-shadow glow on the value arc, band badge underneath) paired with the new **FactorBars** (symmetric bar chart centred on 0 вҖ” positives grow right in emerald, negatives left in rose, label В· bar В· signed delta), plus a **candidate-signals card** (composite chip, matched/missing skill chips, 3-up small-stat row вҖ” match В· interview rated В· days since shortlist вҖ” and an amber callout linking to the interview workspace when no composite yet). Below sits the new **OfferLetterPreview** component вҖ” a custom Markdown renderer (parses h1/h2/p/list/single-pipe table without pulling in a markdown lib, escapes only `**bold**` and `` `code` ``) styled as a print-ready document with a soft violet halo, light table headers, and `@media print` rules in `globals.css` that flip the whole page to light-on-white, hide chrome + nav + buttons, and let the user `cmd-P` straight to a clean PDF. | 23 | 2026-05-15 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-5 move: shipped **Multi-Judge Consensus** вҖ” the explicit roadmap-tagged "run K judges, average scores, surface disagreement" item. A single LLM judge has known biases (self-preference, format prejudice, "longer = better"); a panel doesn't, and the playground now lets you stand one up in three clicks. Three new helpers in `judge.py` (`_stddev`, `_fleiss_kappa`, `_aggregate_verdicts`, `_compute_agreement`) plus `judge_consensus_compare()` (~120 LOC) fan the *same* judge prompt out to вүӨ 6 judges in a `ThreadPoolExecutor` вҖ” wall time is the slowest judge, not the sum вҖ” and per-judge errors (missing key, upstream 5xx) are caught and surfaced under `judges_failed` so a flaky panelist never kills the run. Aggregator returns per-candidate `composite_mean`, sample `composite_std` (n-1), `composite_min`/`max`, `composite_values`, full `per_criterion` cell `{mean, std, votes:[1..5]}` for every rubric criterion, all `rationales` tagged by judge, and a `winner_votes` count of how many judges put this candidate at #1. Agreement layer computes **Fleiss' Оә per criterion** over the 1вҖ“5 categorical buckets (matrix `N_candidates Г— 5`, formula `(PМ„ вҲ’ P_e)/(1 вҲ’ P_e)` with `P_i = (ОЈcВІ вҲ’ n)/(n(nвҲ’1))`, returns `None` when `P_e==1`), an overall Оә (mean of per-criterion), `mean_composite_std` as a fast "panel disagreement" signal, and a per-judge `agrees_with_panel` flag (their argmax-composite == panel-mean-argmax). **History persistence**: new `history.update_consensus()` stores the full block at `payload.consensus` *and* synthesizes a back-compat `payload.judge` view from panel means (rounded per-criterion means as int scores, mean composites) so the History list/detail keeps rendering with zero awareness of consensus runs вҖ” indexed columns get a `consensus(K)` sentinel + the panel-mean top score. **New endpoint** `POST /api/judge/consensus` accepts `{prompt, system_prompt, candidates, judges:[{provider,model}], rubric, run_id?}`, de-dupes the judges list on `${provider}:${model}` while preserving order, requires вүҘ 2 distinct judges, and best-effort attaches to the persisted run. **Frontend** (App.jsx + api.js): new `judgeConsensus()` client method; new `judgePanel` array state for additional judges beyond the primary; new `consensusResults` state with parallel render path. The "Judge responses" button morphs based on roster size: amber gradient + `Judge responses` for 1 judge, fuchsiaвҶ’orangeвҶ’amber gradient + `Run consensus В· K judges` (or `Re-judge В· panel of K` on re-run) for вүҘ 2. | 26 | 2026-05-18 | **WaySafe** | Round-5 move: shipped **Sentinel вҖ” Live Cluster Intel** вҖ” the missing "what's escalating right now" layer that turns the static heatmap into actionable situational awareness. New `sentinel.py` (~330 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `utils.haversine_km`) is the engine: (1) **`dbscan_haversine(points, eps_km, min_samples)`** вҖ” textbook DBSCAN over haversine distance with the noise/border-point rules done by the book (unvisited point вҶ’ Оө-neighbour count, вүҘ min_samples вҮ’ core, transitively grow via a worklist `seen` set so cycles don't loop; -1 = noise). (2) **`cluster_incidents(...)`** вҖ” coerces raw incident rows (filters unparseable lat/lon/timestamps, normalises category lowercase, stamps severity from the project-wide `CATEGORY_SEVERITY` table), runs DBSCAN, then for every cluster produces a `Cluster` dataclass with **severity Г— recency weighted centroid** (`ОЈ w_iВ·lat_i / ОЈ w_i`, `w_i = sev Г— 0.5^(age_h / 72h)`; falls back to plain mean when all weights vanish on ancient incidents), bounding **radius_km** (max member distance from centroid), full **category mix** (sorted (cat, count) tuples, used both for the dominant tag and for the UI tag bar), **severity_mean**, **verified_frac**, **last_seen**, **days_since_last**, **peak_hour** (argmax over a 24-bin histogram), and a **30-day daily-counts array** (oldestвҶ’newest, for the per-cluster sparkline). (3) **Velocity grading**: `velocity = (recent_rate + Оө) / (baseline_rate + Оө)` with `Оө=0.005` rate-floor вҖ” `recent_rate = recent_count / recent_days`, `baseline_rate = baseline_count / baseline_days`, recent window is `[now вҲ’ recent_days, now)`, baseline window is `[now вҲ’ recent_days вҲ’ baseline_days, now вҲ’ recent_days)` so the two windows are disjoint and contiguous. Status thresholds chosen to match human intuition: `вүҘ 2.5Г—` Critical, `1.3 вүӨ v < 2.5` Emerging, `0.6 вүӨ v < 1.3` Steady, `< 0.6` Cooling вҖ” with a hard override that any cluster with `recent_count == 0` is forced to Cooling regardless of the velocity ratio (so a long-quiet cluster doesn't read as Critical just because its baseline is also 0). A previously-dormant cluster that fires N recent incidents reads as `(N/recent_days + Оө)/Оө` Г— velocity, which lands firmly in Critical вҖ” exactly what you want for emergent-pattern detection without a per-cluster cold-start hack. (4) **`compute_risk_pulse(...)`** вҖ” global Risk Pulse rolling every cluster into one of four states: `n_critical вүҘ 1` вҶ’ **Critical**, `n_emerging вүҘ 2` вҶ’ **Active**, `n_emerging вүҘ 1 or n_steady вүҘ 3` вҶ’ **Watch**, else **Calm**. Reports per-status cluster counts, last-24h & last-72h totals, recent-window vs prior-window incident counts (global), an aggregate velocity, and the dominant category across emerging/critical clusters (falls back to the recent-window mix when no clusters trip). (5) **`nearest_cluster(clusters, lat, lon)`** returns the cluster whose *edge* (max(0, dist_to_center вҲ’ radius)) is closest to the user вҖ” answers "how far am I from the nearest hotspot" honestly. (6) **`recommended_action(cluster, lat, lon)`** branches on inside / within 1.5 km / far away Г— status to produce a one-line tip that's actionable rather than alarmist. (7) **`cluster_polygon(c)`** вҖ” 32-vertex approximate circle (lat/km = 1/110.574, lon/km = 1/(111.320В·cos lat)) with a min-radius floor of 0.18 km so single-point or tightly-packed clusters still render as a visible halo on the pydeck `PolygonLayer`. Stable display order: status priority (Critical вҶ’ Cooling) then recent-count desc then total-count desc, then renumber `id` 1..n so the UI reads tidily. **UI** вҖ” new `Sentinel` tab between *Forecast* and *Report Hazard* (10-tab total; existing tabs 5вҖ“8 shifted +1). The shared cluster computation is hoisted to the top of the Tourist App view so the Map tab's **Watch banner** and the Sentinel tab's full intel surface always see the same numbers. Tab layout: **Risk-Pulse hero** вҖ” band-coloured card (`#FF3D60`/`#FF7F50`/`#F9C440`/`#53E3A6` for Critical/Active/Watch/Calm) with a radial-gradient glow, an animated **pulse-dot** (radial-gradient core inside a 50% mask, two `::before`/`::after` rings expanding via `@keyframes ws-sent-pulse` on a staggered 2.4 s loop with `animation-delay: 1.2s` on the second so the rings interleave), the status word at 1.85 rem, headline below, and a right-anchored 4-stat strip (clusters В· last-N days В· prior-N days В· velocity); a chip ribbon underneath breaks out Critical/Emerging/Steady/Cooling counters each with a band-coloured dot plus a "Mostly В· рҹҡ§ accident"-style dominant-category chip. Below the hero: a **collapsible parameter expander** with 4 number inputs (`Оө km` 0.10вҖ“3.00 step 0.05, `min_samples` 2вҖ“15, `recent_days` 1вҖ“120, `baseline_days` 7вҖ“365); any change diff triggers `st.session_state.sentinel_params` write + `st.rerun()` so the whole surface re-clusters live. Then a **pydeck cluster map** вҖ” one `PolygonLayer` per cluster (32-vertex halo, alpha-40 fill + alpha-230 outline, both in the cluster's status hue), white centre `ScatterplotLayer` sized by recent count (radius_min_pixels=8 floor), faint incident dots underneath, view-state re-centred on the cluster centroid at zoom 11.3 вҖ” plus a legend caption. Then the **per-cluster intel cards** (one per cluster, sorted by status priority): card has a 3-px left-accent border in the status hue, top row with category icon (рҹҡ§/рҹҡҰ/вӣ°пёҸ/рҹҢҠ/вҡ пёҸ), title (`Cluster #N В· Category В· count`), centroid + radius + last-seen + peak-hour subtitle, and a right-anchored status pill (background + border alpha-derived from the accent hue); a **velocity bar** with a `1.0Г—` baseline tick at exactly 25% width (visual cap = 4Г—) so the user reads "how far above baseline" at a glance вҖ” current velocity printed in the accent colour underneath, recent rate and baseline rate captioned on the left; a 4-cell **stat grid** (recent count В· prior count В· severity mean / 5 В· verified %); a tag-bar **category mix** showing every category with its count; a 30-day **sparkline** (one bar per day, normalised to peak, accent-hue fill, empty days shown as faint placeholders to preserve the time axis), and a recommended-action callout вҖ” *"You are inside a critical accident hotspot вҖ” leave the area вҖҰ"* when the user is within the cluster, *"You're 0.92 km from a critical hotspot вҖ” reroute via Plan Route (safest)"* when within 1.5 km, otherwise a status-appropriate sentinel tip. Below the cards: a **nearest-cluster mini-callout** that reads either `inside cluster #X` or `nearest cluster #X В· N km from its edge`. **Watch banner on the Map tab** вҖ” always-on top-strip that fires whenever the pulse is anything other than Calm (`рҹҡЁ CRITICAL` / `вҡ пёҸ ACTIVE` / `рҹ‘Җ WATCH`), gradient-tinted in the pulse hue with a left accent rail, links the reader to the Sentinel tab, and shows `N incidents В· K-day window` on the right. **Theme additions** (~210 lines of fresh CSS in `theme.py`): `.ws-sent-hero` shell with radial-gradient glow + flex layout + `--pulse-hue` custom property; `@keyframes ws-sent-pulse` (0% вҶ’ 70% вҶ’ 100%, scale .85вҶ’1.9 + opacity .8вҶ’0) for the dual-ring animation; `.ws-sent-pulse-dot`/`-core` with the layered gradient + 18-px box-shadow glow; `.ws-sent-status-block`/`-kicker`/`-label`/`-headline` typography stack; `.ws-sent-stats`/`-stat`/`-stat-val`/`-stat-lbl` tabular-numeric stat grid; `.ws-sent-counters`/`-chip`/`-chip-dot` chip ribbon; `.ws-sent-cluster` card with left-accent and CSS-var-driven status colouring; `.ws-sent-cluster-head`/`-icon`/`-title`/`-sub`/`-status` header row + pill; `.ws-sent-velbar-wrap`/`-velbar`/`-velbar-fill`/`-velbar-baseline`/`-velbar-baseline-lbl`/`-vel-meta`/`-vel-current` velocity-bar block with the absolutely-positioned baseline tick + `1.0Г—` label; `.ws-sent-statgrid`/`-cell`/`-val`/`-lbl` 4-up grid; `.ws-sent-mix`/`-mix-tag` tag bar; `.ws-sent-spark-wrap`/`-kicker`/`-sparkline`/`-spark-bar`/`-spark-bar.empty`/`-spark-axis` sparkline + axis; `.ws-sent-action` callout with accent-tinted background; `.ws-sent-empty`/`-empty-title` dashed-border idle state; and `.ws-sent-banner`/`-icon`/`-text`/`-meta` Watch banner with status-driven `--banner-hue`/`-bg`/`-bd` CSS vars. | 27 | 2026-05-19 | **Credicrew** | Round-6 opener: shipped **Peer Parity** вҖ” closes the open roadmap line ("per-role team peer parity check вҖ” flag offers that drift too far from the team's existing accepted offers at similar interview composite") with a real fairness audit that bridges Decision Studio (interview composite) and Offer Studio (comp dims). New `frontend/src/lib/peer_parity.ts` (~430 LOC) is the engine: (1) `regress(xs, ys)` вҖ” closed-form 1-D OLS returning `(a, b, rВІ, Пғ_residual)`; degenerate denoms (n<2 or zero composite variance) fall back to a flat mean-of-y predictor so a homogeneous team still reports a verdict; (2) `computePeerParity({composite, base, equityPct, signOn, targetBonusPct, candidateName}, peers)` fits the regression across 5 dimensions (`base`, `equity`, `sign_on`, `target_bonus`, `total_cash = base + signOn + baseВ·bonus%`), z-scores the proposal as `z = (proposed вҲ’ expected)/Пғ_residual` with `Пғ_floor = 5%В·mean(y)` (so a tight team isn't infinitely strict), bands each dim `in_band`/`stretch`/`severe` at |z| thresholds 1.5 / 3.0, and computes inversions = any peer with `composite > proposed.composite + 1` whose total cash is > 2 % less than the proposal's; (3) overall verdict is `inversion` (any inversion) вҶ’ `drift` (any severe dim or вүҘ 3 OOB) вҶ’ `stretch` (вүҘ 1 OOB) вҶ’ `fair`; suppresses to `fair` when peers < 2 so a near-empty pool can't lie; (4) `suggestions[]` includes the smallest single-axis move on the worst dim to land back inside Вұ1.5Пғ (signed, formatted in `вӮ№X LPA` / `Y pp` / `Z%`), plus an explicit "cut total cash by ~вӮ№N LPA to clear the inversion against {peer}" line per inversion; (5) localStorage namespace `credicrew:peers:v1` is keyed per-roleId so deletions don't leak across roles; `ensureSeeded(roleId, buildSeed)` auto-seeds 8 realistic India-engineering offers (Aarav/Priya/Karan/Riya/Vivaan/Ishaan/Nayantara/Mihir, composite 65вҖ“89, base вӮ№28вҖ“вӮ№138 LPA, Bengaluru/Mumbai/Pune, juniorвҶ’principal) for a fresh role so the audit lights up on first open. **Mirrored byte-for-byte** in `backend/app/services/peer_parity.py` (~380 LOC, same dataclasses + camelCase `as_dict()` for parity) and exposed via `backend/app/routers/peer_parity.py` (~150 LOC) with 4 endpoints вҖ” `POST /peer-parity/check` (caller-supplied peers, both snake and camel payloads via Pydantic aliases), `GET/POST/DELETE /peer-parity/peers?team=ID` (in-memory team pool CRUD, thread-safe `RLock`), and `POST /peer-parity/check_team?team=ID` (audit against the pooled peers); `main.py` `version` bumped `0.6.0 вҶ’ 0.7.0` and root index lists the new routes. **Frontend UI**: new `PeerParityPanel.tsx` (~420 LOC) mounts under the win-prob dial вҖ” hue-driven `--parity-hue` CSS custom property tints the whole shell, 4 hero stat tiles (verdict / drift score / out-of-band / inversions), an inline-SVG **composite-vs-base scatter** at 520Г—260 with peers as dim grey dots, a translucent Вұ1Пғ band as a `<polygon>`, a dashed violet regression line, and the proposed offer as a 5-point gradient-glowing `<polygon>` star (zero new chart deps), 5 **per-dim parity bars** with violetвҶ’sky gradient bands and a pulsing status-tinted proposed marker (`@keyframes cc-parity-pulse`), an **Inversion alert** card with an `inv-glow` animation and a "Snap to peer band" button that recomputes a base-only cut to bring total cash to `peer_total Г— 0.98`, a Suggestions list, a Nearest-peers table (5 closest by |О” composite| with coloured base/composite deltas), and right-aligned `Publish to peer pool` + `Manage peers` controls. New `PeerPoolDrawer.tsx` (~210 LOC) is a right-side drawer (220 ms `cc-parity-slide` slide-in) with per-peer cards (3Г—2 stat grid + Remove button) and a 10-field add form (name / role / seniority dropdown / location / composite / base / equity / sign-on / bonus / accepted-on) wired straight to `addPeer()` in the engine. Offer Studio page integrates the panel + drawer: a new `peers` state + `peerSeedRef` guards a one-shot seed on role load; `parity` is `useMemo`-derived off `(draft, interviewSummary, peers, candidate)` so dragging the base/equity/sign-on sliders re-renders the audit live; `onPublishPeer` snapshots the current proposal back into the pool as an "observed" peer; `onClearInversion` runs the snap-to-band math (`newBase = (draft.baseВ·factor вҲ’ drop)/factor`) and updates the draft, after which the existing win-prob dial, factor bars, comp ladder, and letter all re-render off the same state. **Theme**: ~65 lines of new CSS in `globals.css` covering `.cc-parity-shell` with dual radial-gradient glows + a top accent rail painted via `linear-gradient` + `color-mix(in srgb, вҖҰ)`, the verdict dot, hover lift on `.cc-parity-stat`, the SVG drop-shadow, `.cc-parity-marker` pulse, the `.cc-parity-inv` ring-glow, peer-card hover, and the drawer slide-in. **Validation**: backend `pytest`-style smoke against `TestClient` covered 11 scenarios вҖ” empty pool returns `fair` + the "No peer offers in the pool yet" note; | 28 | 2026-05-20 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-6 move: shipped the roadmap-tagged **Prompt Library with diff'd versions** вҖ” closing the loop that's been dangling since Round 1. Playground had every measurement (Arena fan-out, Judge, Multi-judge consensus, History, Vote/ELO) but no way to tie *a specific prompt revision* to the runs it produced вҖ” so "did my edit actually help?" was unanswerable without manual JSON diffing. The new `backend/src/prompts.py` (~530 LOC) is a pure-`sqlite3` versioned-prompt store sharing `history.db` (single backup still captures everything): two new tables вҖ” `prompts` (id, name, created_at, updated_at, current_version_id, starred, tag, note) and `prompt_versions` (id, prompt_id, version_num, system_prompt, user_template, created_at, parent_version_id, note) вҖ” plus an **idempotent ALTER on boot** that adds `runs.prompt_version_id` (nullable FK, indexed) via a `PRAGMA table_info(runs)` introspection so the migration is safe on every cold start without dragging Alembic in. Public engine: `create_prompt` (auto-creates v1), `list_prompts` (returns per-prompt rolls вҖ” n_versions, n_runs, n_judged, avg_composite, last_run_at, plus a **score-progression sparkline** array `[{v: n, s: judge_top_score_or_null}, вҖҰ]` ordered v1вҶ’vN with `None` for un-judged versions so the UI shows real gaps instead of linearly interpolated lies), `get_prompt` (full prompt + every version + per-version `stats` derived from the linked runs), `add_version` (**idempotent on identical content** вҖ” same system+template returns the existing head verbatim, no sibling-version litter from double-clicks), `set_prompt_meta`, `delete_prompt` (cascades versions but **preserves runs** вҖ” their `prompt_version_id` becomes a dangling pointer, deliberate so the audit trail of "which prompt produced this answer" survives prompt cleanup), `link_run` (called from `/compare` when the request carries a `prompt_version_id`, also bumps the prompt's `updated_at` so the library re-sorts), `runs_for_version`, `diff_versions`, and `stats`. **Diff engine** uses stdlib `difflib.unified_diff` over a joined `## SYSTEM\nвҖҰ\n## USER\nвҖҰ` blob (single diff covers both fields with a sentinel that tells the reader where the change landed); the unified-diff output is parsed server-side into structured hunks (`{header, lines:[{type:add|del|ctx, text}]}`) so the frontend doesn't re-parse strings, and `SequenceMatcher.get_opcodes()` also emits per-field add/del counts + similarity ratio. The diff response carries a `score_delta = avg_composite(b) вҲ’ avg_composite(a)` computed from each version's judged runs (None on either side stays None) вҖ” the headline answer to "did my edit help?". **`/api/compare` modified** to accept an optional `prompt_version_id` in the payload and best-effort `prompts.link_run(run_id, version_id)` after `history.save_run` вҖ” a missing/dangling version logs a warning but never 500s the run. **9 new endpoints** under `/api/prompts/*`: `GET /` (list with q/starred/tag/limit/offset filters), `POST /` (create), `GET /:id` (detail), `DELETE /:id`, `POST /:id/meta` (name/star/tag/note), `POST /:id/versions` (append), `GET /:id/versions/:vid/runs` (linked-run listing), `POST /diff` (unified diff + score О”), `GET /stats` (library-level dashboard banner вҖ” n_prompts, n_versions, n_linked_runs, avg_composite, top-5 most-iterated). **Frontend**: new `components/PromptLibrary.jsx` (~760 LOC) вҖ” stats banner (4 gradient tiles + most-iterated pill row), filter row (search input + `Starred only` switch + reset chip), create-prompt form (name + system + user template + tag), two-column grid with prompt list (left) and detail (right). Detail card: large head-version score ring + inline rename (Enter saves, Esc cancels) + tag chip + star/new-version/delete buttons; collapsible **new-version editor** with system + template textareas + change-note input and a "v{n+1} will be created if content differs from head" subline. Version timeline (latest first) вҖ” each row's ring is clickable to set the diff endpoint (1st click вҶ’ A, 2nd вҶ’ B, 3rd resets); HEAD badged violet, A indigo, B fuchsia; per-row chips (n_runs В· `{score}/100` В· рҹҸҶ best-model В· cost). When both A+B are picked, the diff banner replaces the version-detail body with a **DiffPanel**: header chips (+adds / вҲ’removes / similarity % / **Score О”** with direction-aware emerald-up/rose-down arrows), two side-by-side `VersionStatTile`s (A indigo / B fuchsia В· n_runs В· judged score В· best-model В· change note), and a **slate-900 unified-diff surface** (max-h 280px scrollable) with hunk headers in `bg-slate-800` and per-line `+`/`вҲ’`/ctx coloring (emerald-300/rose-300/slate-300) and `+`/`вҲ’`/space prefix. **App.jsx integration**: 6th radio mode **Library** (violetвҶ’fuchsia `new` badge), new state `activePromptLink` (`{prompt_id, prompt_name, version_id, version_num}`) + `libSelectedPromptId` + `libPendingDraft`; when Library's "Run" button fires `onRunInArena`, the app hops to Arena mode, pre-loads system+template into the existing fields, sets `activePromptLink`, and the next `/compare` call auto-injects `prompt_version_id`. Arena header gained three context-aware buttons: a **violet `BookOpenText` chip** showing the linked prompt name + version (click вҶ’ Library), a **"Save as new version"** button when linked (appends a version via `addPromptVersion` and updates the link in-place to the new vN), and a **"Save to Library"** button for any *unlinked* Arena prompt (opens Library in create-from-draft mode with name/system/template pre-filled). `services/api.js` extended with 8 prompt methods (`listPrompts`, `createPrompt`, `getPrompt`, `deletePrompt`, `setPromptMeta`, `addPromptVersion`, `diffPromptVersions`, `promptStats`, `runsForVersion`). **Validation**: `ast.parse` clean on both modified files; standalone-module smoke tested 12 scenarios вҖ” `create_prompt` + first version, `add_version` chain, **idempotency** on identical content (same id returned, no sibling row), `list_prompts` rolls + filters (q/starred/tag), `link_run` + `update_judge` integration (avg_composite = 85.0, best_model = "OpenAI:gpt-4o"), `diff_versions` (added=2, similarity=0.667 between v1 and a v2 with one tightened line), edge cases (diff with bogus id вҶ’ None, diff same-id blocked at route layer), `delete_prompt` cascades versions but preserves runs (audit trail), library stats roll-up.
