| 29 | 2026-05-21 | **SynapseOS** | Round-6 move: shipped **Distill** вҖ” the empty-graph killer. PKM has one persistent cold-start problem (you install a graph-based note system, stare at an empty canvas, and never come back); Distill closes it by taking *any* paste вҖ” article, transcript, Slack thread, braindump вҖ” and exploding it into atomic-note previews that already pre-show their synapse landings before any save fires. New `backend/app/atomize.py` (~430 LOC) is a pure-stdlib pipeline with six concerns wired tight: (1) **segment** вҖ” `_split_paragraphs` hard-splits on blank lines, markdown headings (always their own atom вҖ” without this rule a paste like `# A / short body / # B / short body` would fuse into one giant atom because each paragraph is below `MIN_ATOM_CHARS=80`), and bullet runs (gathered into a single coherent list atom, not one-line orphans), with Windows/Mac line endings normalized and BOM stripped first; `_merge_to_atoms` then glues short fragments forward, sentence-repacks any paragraph exceeding `MAX_ATOM_CHARS=900` into `~TARGET_ATOM_CHARS=480` chunks, and folds a tiny final atom backwards *unless* it's heading-led (so `## Conclusion / Ship it.` ships as its own atom); (2) **title** вҖ” `_pick_title` lifts the heading verbatim when present, else picks the first sentence via a forced-`always=True` sentence splitter (regular splitter short-circuits paragraphs вүӨ 480 chars to keep the segmenter cheap; the title-picker overrides because the headline IS the first sentence, not the first paragraph), and on long openers tries break-points in priority `": " > " вҖ” " > " вҖ“ " > "; " > ", "` before falling back to a word-bounded trim at 80 chars; trailing markdown emphasis / quotes / hard punctuation are stripped; (3) **tags** вҖ” `_tag_candidates` yields 1- and 2-grams skipping stops, sub-4-char unigrams, sub-3-char bigram halves, and pure-digit tokens; `_score_tags` runs a TF-IDF flavored distinctiveness `tf В· log(1 + n_atoms / df)` (bigrams Г—1.15 вҖ” multi-word tags are more informative than the unigrams they decompose into), takes вүӨ1 top bigram + вүӨ2 top unigrams, slugifies (lowercase, `[^a-z0-9]+` collapses, 24-char cap), and dedupes; (4) **cluster prediction** вҖ” `_community_centroids` averages and L2-renormalizes member embeddings per cluster (skipping clusters whose members all lack embeddings), `_predict_cluster` cosine-matches the atom's embedding against each centroid and accepts the best only above `CLUSTER_HINT_TAU=0.18` (deliberately above the synapse default `П„=0.14` so we only flag a real cluster landing, not a weak peripheral one); (5) **neighbor preview** вҖ” `_neighbor_preview` returns top-3 existing notes at `cosine вүҘ П„` with per-neighbor `note_id / title / strength / cluster_id / cluster_color` so the UI can paint the synapse chip with the destination's cluster tint; `_all_neighbors_count` reports the full above-П„ count as `expected_synapses` (drives the "N synapses predicted" / "will be an orphan" badge); (6) **optional LLM refine** вҖ” `llm_refine_title` reuses the existing `app/llm.py` stdlib HTTP client (Anthropic Messages + OpenAI-compatible Chat Completions; no SDK adds) under a strict JSON-output system prompt ("write tight 3вҖ“9-word titles and 2вҖ“3 lowercase slug tags; output only `{title, tags}`"), tolerates markdown code-fences around the JSON, slug-normalizes returned tags through the same `_slugify` as heuristic mode, and dedupes against the heuristic tags (heuristic+LLM merged, cap 4). Any 5xx / network / decode failure silently keeps the heuristic output for that atom вҖ” the product is fully usable without an LLM key. **Two new endpoints** in `main.py`: `POST /atomize?threshold&top_k` (preview-only, no DB writes вҖ” body `{text, mode}` with 422 on empty / >120k chars; runs the pipeline + LLM-refine pass when `mode='llm'` or `mode='auto' + key_set`, surfaces a `notice` when the user asked for LLM and we couldn't deliver, returns `{atoms[], total_chars, mode_used, llm_available, llm_provider, notice}`) and `POST /atomize/commit?threshold&top_k` (bulk insert of user-edited atoms, 1вҖ“64 cap; each atom goes through `store.add_note` so the embedding cache + `last_seen_at` handling stays identical to single-note creation; recomputes the graph once and attributes new edges back to each atom via a single pass вҖ” endpoints where one side is newly-created bump that atom's counter and the global total вҖ” so the post-commit flash reports a faithful "M synapses formed" instead of guessing; tags are defensively dedup+lowercased; 422 on empty list). **Frontend**: new `Distill.tsx` (~635 LOC) is a 3-stage modal вҖ” **input** (full-width textarea on a glass card, char counter, mode toggle `auto / fast / llm` with the llm chip disabled + tooltip when no key, a "try a sample" button preloading a 3-paragraph article so first-time users see the demo immediately, footer hints `В· headings start new atoms В· short paragraphs glue forward В· monster paragraphs sentence-split В· nothing saves until you confirm`), **preview** (one card per atom вҖ” left-edge cluster-color accent stripe with linear-gradient fade-out, editable title `<input>` and editable body `<textarea>` inline, per-card status row with `char_count В· expected_synapses` (cyan "N synapses predicted" or pink "will be an orphan") + `will join {cluster} ({%} match)` + an `вңЁ llm-refined` badge when the atom went through the LLM, tag chips that delete on click and a `+ tag` dashed-ring input that enters on Enter or comma, predicted-neighbor chips with cluster-tinted dot + truncated title + cosine % вҖ” click pipes the existing note up to the page's Inspector so you can verify the landing *before* committing, drop / restore toggle so you can prune without retyping), **committing** (pulse-ring shimmer + "committing N atomsвҖҰ"), **done** (gradient-blurred green checkmark + count + `synapses_formed` honest summary + "distill more" / "back to graph" CTAs); sticky bottom bar in preview keeps `вҶҗ back` / atom-count subtext / `commit N atoms вҶ’` reachable without scrolling. New `nodes` prop lets the modal enrich neighbor chips against the live graph (full GraphNode handed to `onPreviewNeighbor` so the Inspector gets degree + weight, not just title). `lib/api.ts` gained `atomize({text, mode})` + `atomizeCommit(atoms)`; `lib/types.ts` gained 6 new types (`AtomNeighbor / AtomPreview / AtomizeMode / AtomizeResponse / AtomCommit / AtomizeCommitResponse`). Header gained a violetвҶ’cyan gradient `вңЁ distill` button between the existing pills and `daily brief`. Page wires the modal in: `distillOpen` / `distillFlash` state; on commit, refreshes `/graph + /communities + /orphans` in parallel (reusing the existing `refreshGraph`) and shows a fixed bottom-center pill `{N} atom(s) added В· {M} synapse(s) formed` (auto-dismisses in 5.5 s) so the user *sees* the graph re-render and gets a verbal confirmation. **Validation**: backend `TestClient` smoke validated 16 scenarios end-to-end against a freshly-seeded 16-note demo graph вҖ” full regression on `/health`, `/notes`, `/graph`, `/communities`, `/orphans`, `/brief`, `/chat/status`, `/trails`, `/search`, `/path`, `/neighbors/1`, `POST /chat` (all 200); `POST /atomize` with a 4-paragraph article returns 4 atoms with sensible titles ('Hashing trick embeddings', 'Why not a real model', 'Trade-off: it misses synonymy', 'The trick lives in app/embed.py'), distinctive tag picks (`['hashing-trick', 'hashing', 'embeddings']`, no overlap with `['real-model', 'real', 'model']`), cluster predictions matching existing communities at 0.27вҖ“0.34 cosine, and per-atom neighbor previews referencing real seed notes; `POST /atomize/commit` lands all 4 atoms (graph grows 16 вҶ’ 20 nodes, 23 synapses formed); 422 paths validated (empty text, whitespace-only text, >120k chars, empty commit list, >64-atom commit cap); LLM-mode-without-key returns a clear `notice` and falls back to heuristic; the headed-atom segmentation test confirms `# My deep thought\n\nbody\n\n## And another\n\nbody` correctly splits into 2 atoms rather than fusing (regression coverage for the heading-boundary rule); unit tests cover the segmentation primitives directly (`_split_paragraphs` produces 5 paragraphs from a mixed heading/body/bullet input, `_merge_to_atoms` keeps bullet runs as one atom, oversized 1800-char paragraph repacks into 4 вүӨ480-char chunks, tiny final atom folds backward unless heading-led). Frontend `npx tsc --noEmit` exits 0; `next build` ships clean (`/` 26.7 kB / 114 kB First Load, +4.4 kB / +4 kB First Load for the modal). **Schema**: 7 new pydantic models (`AtomizeRequest / AtomNeighborOut / AtomPreviewOut / AtomizeOut / AtomCommitIn / AtomizeCommitRequest / AtomCommitResult / AtomizeCommitOut`); zero net store / migration changes since atoms persist through the existing `store.add_note` path. | 30 | 2026-05-22 | **Titan** | Round-6 move: shipped **Typology Classifier** вҖ” the analyst-facing answer to the "which playbook does that add up to?" question that the eight-detector engine has always left dangling. New `apps/ai-aml/typology.py` (~520 LOC, pure stdlib) ships six FATF / Wolfsberg laundering typologies (`SMURF` smurfing/structuring В· `LAYER` round-trip layering В· `TBML` trade-based ML В· `MULE` pass-through mule network В· `SANCEV` sanctions evasion В· `INTEG` integration) each declared as a frozen `TypologyDef` of `_Contributor` rows; each contributor is either a detector key (`structuring`, `fan_in`, `round_trip`, `sanctions_hit`, `high_risk_geo`, `round_amount`, `velocity_spike`, `fan_out`) recovered as `intensity = points/weight вҲҲ [0,1]`, or a derived structural signal (`__retention__` = `(1вҲ’|inвҲ’out|/max(in,out))ВІ` for MULE's pass-through symmetry detection, `__sanctions_strength__` = `(best_similarityвҲ’0.65)/0.35` clipped for additive SANCEV severity, `__low_counterparty_density__` = `max(0, 1вҲ’cp_count/6)` for INTEG's concentrated-source pattern). **Confidence** = `ОЈ(signal Г— weight) / ОЈ(weight)` so a perfect match scores 1.00; matches below `CONFIDENCE_FLOOR=0.35` are dropped (keeps SAR narratives honest); top `MAX_REPORTED=3` returned ranked descending. Every match carries `severity_floor` (low/medium/high/critical), ranked `evidence` chips with per-contributor signal % and detector detail strings lifted off the firing factor, an **auto-generated narrative** (interpolates `{flow_total / counterparty_count / struct_detail / cycle_detail / geo_detail / sanction_detail / integ_detail}` against the live account stats using `_format_inr` for Indian-numbering вӮ№), and a **recommended_action** sentence that pre-fills SAR В§5. `risk.py` `score_accounts()` now calls `typology.classify()` per account and embeds the ranked list on the `AccountReport` payload; `rules_version` bumped `1.1.0 вҶ’ 1.2.0`; `get_rules()` exposes the full library under a new `typologies` block for auditors. `cases.py` got two **idempotent migrations** via `PRAGMA table_info` introspection (`ALTER TABLE cases ADD COLUMN typology_code TEXT` / `вҖҰ typology_confidence REAL`) so older DBs pick up the columns at first boot with no table rewrite; | 31 | 2026-05-23 | **WaySafe** | Round-7 opener: shipped the **Travel Advisory brief** вҖ” a single-page, share-and-print safety briefing that fuses every engine in the repo (Safety Intelligence + Sentinel + Forecast + geofences + POIs) into the *one screen* a tourist actually wants before walking out the door. New `advisory.py` (~540 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of the project's modules; reportlab only imported lazily inside `brief_to_pdf`) is the engine: (1) **`build_brief(target_lat, target_lon, target_label, *, inc_df, poi_df, geofences, forecaster, sentinel_clusters, risk_pulse, now=вҖҰ, radius_km=2.0, lookback_days=7)`** is the single entrypoint вҖ” pandas DataFrames or list-of-dicts both go through `_as_records()`, `compute_safety` runs identical-to-the-Map-tab physics so the score never disagrees, geofence membership is point-in-polygon-checked against every ring, recent incidents within the scan disc are coerced + ranked `(age_hours asc, severity desc)` with each row stamped with a human-readable `age` ("3h ago"), a `category_severity` lookup, status badge, and a 160-char note snippet; categories aggregated, a 7-day daily-counts trend built oldestвҶ’newest with `bucket = min((now-ts).days, lookback_days-1)` so boundary incidents never silently drop; help POIs filtered to the `safety.HELP_POI_TYPES` set, ranked by distance, top-5 kept; Sentinel clusters with disc overlap (`d вүӨ radius_km + c.radius_km`) projected to **edge distance** `max(0, d вҲ’ c.radius_km)` so an overlapping cluster reads as "0.0 km" not "centroid 0.6 km"; forecast windows pulled by sweeping the next 12 h hourly through `forecaster.hotspots(t, k=1)` and surfacing the **3 lowest-risk hours**. (2) **Advisory level** is computed in two stages вҖ” base level from safety score (`0вҖ“34 Critical В· 35вҖ“59 Elevated В· 60вҖ“79 Caution В· 80+ All clear`) then *force-bumped* by Sentinel: `вүҘ2 severe clusters (Critical/Emerging вҲ§ severity_meanвүҘ3.5) вҶ’ Critical`, `вүҘ1 severe and base==All clear вҶ’ Elevated`, because a static score can't see "things are moving in this neighbourhood" without bringing the velocity signal across. (3) **Recommendations** are built by a small priority-ordered ruleset: Critical/Elevated вҶ’ postpone + share location; in-zone вҶ’ name the geofence; escalating cluster nearby вҶ’ cite its velocity status + distance + category; help POI вҶ’ pin the nearest by type; late-night + non-All-clear вҶ’ prefer well-lit busy streets; non-All-clear with windows вҶ’ name the best depart label + top-cell risk %; All-clear and clean вҶ’ standard precautions fallback so the list never goes empty. (4) Three exports are first-class: **`brief_to_json`** emits a stable `waysafe.advisory.v1` schema (target, advisory{level/color/headline/is_safe_to_go}, safety{score/band/factors/nearest_help_km/incidents_nearby}, scan{radius_km/lookback_days/trend_daily_counts}, incidents[], incidents_by_category, active_geofences, help_pois[], nearby_clusters[], best_windows[], risk_pulse{status/headline/severe_cluster_count}, recommendations[]) so two briefs can be diff'd, stored in a CRM, or piped into a downstream chatbot; **`brief_to_markdown`** is the WhatsApp/email/Notion-paste format with severity dots + verified-tick + nested note quotes; **`brief_to_pdf`** uses reportlab to render a polished single-page A4 вҖ” colour-stripe header band lifted from the advisory hue (`_hex_to_rgb01` for clean fractional RGB), wide score-bar with band-coloured fill behind a white "Safety N / 100 В· band" label, two-column layout (left: "Why this score" factor rows + Risk-zone names В· right: "Nearest help" POIs + Safer depart windows), incident table with verified вң“ markers + italicised notes underneath each row, live-clusters row with edge-distance + radius + days-since-last, numbered recommendations checklist (markdown bold stripped, 95-char wrap), footer disclaimer about deferring to local authorities. **New theme component**: `theme.render_advisory_brief(brief)` вҖ” a ~200-line render that emits the full card stack: glass **hero** card with radial-gradient glow keyed to the advisory hue + 6 px left-border + uppercase advisory stripe + conic-ring score (`--pct` driven via the same `.ws-ring` primitives `render_score_card` uses) + level headline; four **KPI tiles** (incidents nearby В· live clusters / N escalating В· safer depart window В· nearest help name+km); **two-column section row** with recent-incident pills (per-severity color dot via `_SEVERITY_HUE`, category icon, distance, age, verified/pending pill, italic note) + the 7-day trend sparkline (weekday labels aligned via `_adv_timedelta` so the labels match `now - lookback_days + 1 + i`), and on the right the cluster pill list (status pill colored by `_cluster_status_hue`, "overlapping" label when edge distance вүӨ 50 m) + safer-depart-windows rows (greenвҶ’amberвҶ’red gradient bar, hour label, percentage right-aligned); **nearest help** list with per-type emoji (`рҹҸҘ рҹҡ“ вһ• рҹҡ’ в„№пёҸ`); **numbered, accent-tinted recommendations** with lightweight `**bold**` markdown rendering. CSS lives inside `inject_theme` (additive вҖ” 6 new selector groups under `.ws-adv-*` totalling ~140 lines: `ws-adv-hero / ws-adv-stripe / ws-adv-tiles / ws-adv-section / ws-adv-inc-row / ws-adv-spark / ws-adv-cluster / ws-adv-window / ws-adv-poi / ws-adv-rec` plus their state variants) so the new tab inherits the same dark glassmorphism every other panel uses. **App wiring**: tab labels grow from 10 to 11 (`Advisory` inserted between `Forecast` and `Sentinel` вҖ” Sentinel/Report/Alerts/SOS/Trip-Log indices shifted down by 1 in lockstep); | 32 | 2026-05-24 | **Credicrew** | Round-7 move: shipped the **Command Center** (`/hq`) вҖ” the portfolio layer the whole product had been missing. Every other surface is single-role/single-candidate; a recruiter running ten reqs had no bird's-eye view. New `frontend/src/lib/portfolio.ts` (~470 LOC, pure functions, no I/O) is the aggregation engine: it takes a flattened snapshot of every role + shortlist (each candidate carrying match score, interview composite, confidence, recommendation, an optional offer draft, and an optional accept-probability) and rolls it up into one `PortfolioSummary`. Six concerns: (1) **hire-signal parity** вҖ” re-derives `round(compositeВ·вҲҡconfidence)` exactly as `decision.ts` so the two never disagree; (2) **aggregate funnel** вҖ” current-status histogram across the 5-stage progression (`newвҶ’outreachвҶ’screeningвҶ’interviewвҶ’offer`, `passed` bucketed separately), reached-at-least computed by summing from the deepest stage backwards, adjacent-stage conversion = `reached(this)/reached(prev)`; (3) **comp forecast** вҖ” `total_cash = base + signOn + baseВ·bonus%` (mirrors peer-parity's definition) summed over every drafted offer into **committed** (all sign) vs **expected** (risk-weighted by each offer's live win-probability), plus avg base / avg accept / top-spend role; (4) **per-role health** вҖ” a renormalised weighted blend of momentum (`1 вҲ’ stale/active`, 0.30), interview coverage (`interviewed/reached-interview`, 0.25), decision quality (`mean hireSignal/100`, 0.25), and offer confidence (`mean winProb`, 0.20) where **absent signals drop out and remaining weights renormalise** (same philosophy as the interview rubric вҖ” a role with no offers isn't punished), plus a top-candidate pick, best composite, and a bottleneck stage (the progression stage holding the most active, вүҘ2 to qualify); (5) **cross-role talent leaderboard** вҖ” the 8 strongest interviewed candidates across *all* roles by hire signal; (6) **attention feed** вҖ” a priority-sorted action list: stale candidates (вүҘ14d medium / вүҘ21d high), offers tracking <45% accept (`<30%` high), signal-вүҘ75 candidates still parked in new/outreach (fast-track), roles with a shortlist but zero interviews, and empty roles вҖ” capped at 10, highвҶ’low. Portfolio health weights each role by its active count. **Backend mirror** in `backend/app/services/portfolio.py` (~360 LOC, pure stdlib) is byte-for-byte parity with the TS engine вҖ” confirmed by transpiling `portfolio.ts` standalone and running an identical fixed-`NOW` 3-role / 5-candidate fixture through both: every number, ordering, funnel cell, comp total (committed 90.16 / expected 52.23 LPA), health score (rA 68 В· rB 79 В· portfolio 74), talent ranking (Dev 86 В· Asha 82 В· Esha 61 В· Chitra 28), and attention kind matched exactly (the only JSON delta is TS-omits-`undefined` vs Python-emits-`null`, the same convention every other mirror uses). New `backend/app/routers/portfolio.py` exposes `POST /portfolio/summary` accepting both `camelCase` and `snake_case` via Pydantic `Field(alias=вҖҰ)` + `ConfigDict(populate_by_name=True)`; `main.py` version bumped `0.7.0 вҶ’ 0.8.0` and root index advertises the route. **Frontend Command Center** at `/hq` (13.3 kB / 120 kB First Load): `gatherInput()` resolves every role's shortlist through the *existing* match/interview/offer engines (so the dashboard never disagrees with the per-role pages вҖ” composite via `summarise()`, accept-probability via `benchmarkComp()` + `winProbability()`), then `buildPortfolio()` drives the render. Layout вҖ” gradient title row with **Copy brief / Export brief.md** (a Markdown portfolio digest built inline: health, comp, funnel, top talent, attention); a hero row pairing a 120 px conic health ring (hue-ramped roseвҶ’amberвҶ’indigoвҶ’emerald via `HEALTH_HUE`) with a 6-tile KPI grid (open roles В· in-flight В· interviews run В· offers out В· committed comp В· stale); a full-width **funnel card** (per-stage gradient bars sized by reached/total-active with reached+here counts overlaid and a colour-graded conversion % on the right); a **role leaderboard** (sortable by health / in-flight / days-open вҖ” each row a 48 px health ring + proportional `StageBar` segmented by `STATUS_TONE` + stale/bottleneck chips + top-candidate caption, deep-linking to the role); a **comp-forecast aside** (committed vs expected gradient bars + avg-base / avg-accept stat tiles) above a **recommendation-mix** bar reusing `TIER_HUE`; and a 2-up **talent leaderboard** (signal rings deep-linking to each scorecard) + **attention feed** (severity-toned, deep-linked cards вҖ” offer-risk items route to Offer Studio, others to the scorecard/role; empty state reads "Nothing on fire вң“"). New `.cc-hq-*` CSS in `globals.css` (ring hover glow, hero/comp radial-gradient surface accents, attention-row translate-x hover). Nav links added to Discover / Roles / Navbar. Empty-state CTA when no roles exist. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `next build` ships clean across 14 routes (`/hq` 13.3 kB / 120 kB First Load, every other route unchanged, shared chunks steady at 87.1 kB); `next dev` serves `GET /hq` 200 with `вң“ Compiled` and no runtime errors; backend `TestClient` smoke green across unit checks (hire-signal/total-cash), the 3-role fixture (totals, funnel reached/here, comp committed+expected, attention kinds, talent order, role+portfolio health), `/portfolio/summary` round-trips in both camelCase and snake_case, and the empty-portfolio guard returns `portfolioHealth=null` + `bottleneck=null`. README: opening blurb extended, new **"What's new вҖ” Command Center (Day 32)"** section (health-score formula, funnel, comp forecast, leaderboards, attention feed, brief export, backend mirror), `POST /portfolio/summary` curl example + endpoint-map row, project-structure tree extended with `portfolio.py` (router + service) + `portfolio.ts` + `hq/page.tsx`. |

| 33 | 2026-05-25 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-7 move: shipped **Studio Insights** вҖ” the analytics layer the whole product had been missing. The playground could *measure* everything (Arena latency & cost, single + multi-judge composites, blind-vote ELO) and *persist* it all into `history.db`, but it never answered the one question an LLM-eval tool exists for: **which model gives the best quality per dollar?** New `backend/src/insights.py` (~430 LOC, pure stdlib + a single `from src import vote_arena` for the ELO join) is a **read-only** roll-up вҖ” it invents no tables and writes nothing, so it's the *same numbers* History/Judge/Vote already produced, just aggregated, and can never disagree with them. `_aggregate()` walks every run once, building a per-`Provider:model` accumulator (`_Acc`, `__slots__`-only so the file's non-stdlib import surface is literally one line): appearances, success/error counts, latency/cost/token/char samples, judge composites (pulled from `payload.judge.verdicts` вҖ” works for single-judge *and* consensus runs since `history.update_consensus` writes a back-compat `payload.judge`), and judge wins. `model_scorecards()` derives per-model `avg_cost`, `avg_composite`, `quality_per_dollar = avg_composite / avg_cost`, success rate, and an `efficiency_index` (min-max-normalised q/$ to 0-100), then joins each row to its `vote_arena.leaderboard()` ELO rating + games + win-rate. `efficiency_frontier()` computes the **Pareto frontier of maximise-quality / minimise-cost**: a model is *dominated* iff some other eligible model has `composite вүҘ mine AND avg_cost вүӨ mine` with at least one strict вҖ” the non-dominated set is the frontier, and dominated points carry their `dominated_by` list; only models with a judge score **and** positive cost are placed (the two axes), everything else lands in `unplaced` with a `no_judge_score`/`no_cost` reason. `cost_timeline()` buckets runs to UTC-day (spend В· runs В· judged В· avg-top-score), `provider_rollup()` aggregates to provider level (spend share + mean quality), and `build_insights()` stitches it all into one payload with a headline `summary` (total spend, best-value/top-quality/cheapest/fastest/top-ELO picks, and a 7-day spend trend anchored on the *latest run's* timestamp so it's deterministic). **One new endpoint** `GET /api/insights?min_appearances=N` returns the whole bundle in a single read. **Frontend**: new `components/InsightsPanel.jsx` (~640 LOC) is a 7th sidebar mode (**Insights**, indigoвҶ’emerald `new` badge, `Gauge` icon). Headline is a **custom-SVG efficiency-frontier scatter** вҖ” x = cost/response on a **log scale** (costs span orders of magnitude), y = judge composite 0-100, each model a provider-coloured bubble (radius вҲқ вҲҡappearances), frontier points joined by a line over a gradient fill and ringed while dominated ones fade to 32% opacity; hovering a bubble pins a detail card (quality В· cost В· q/$ В· runs В· frontier/dominated-by status). A **Copy brief** button emits a Markdown digest of the whole dashboard. `App.jsx` gains the radio option + a panel branch (the Library "new" badge moves to Insights); `services/api.js` gains `insights({minAppearances})`. **Validation**: deterministic engine smoke test against a seeded temp DB (3 runs, 4 models, 1 vote) asserts every number вҖ” avg composites (gpt-4o 89.0 from [90,88], haiku 82.0), q/$ (flash 71000, haiku 41000), the dominated `o-mini` (0.012/65) correctly excluded from the frontier with `dominated_by=["OpenAI:gpt-4o"]` while gpt-4o/haiku/flash all sit on it, frontier sorted cost-ascending, ELO joined (gpt-4o games=1, judge_wins=2), timeline = 3 days with avg-top-score 90.0 on day 0, provider spend-share summing to 100.0%, summary best-value=flash / top-quality=gpt-4o / cheapest=flash, and an empty-DB guard returning `scorecards=[]` + `frontier=[]`. | 34 | 2026-05-26 | **SynapseOS** | Round-7 move: shipped **Synthesis** вҖ” auto-written, cited topic briefings per cluster. Day 9 made clusters *visible* (greedy-modularity communities) and *named* (distinctive-term TF-IDF), but a violet blob labelled "embeddings" still isn't knowledge вҖ” you had to open every member note to learn what the topic actually *said*. Synthesis closes that gap. New `backend/app/synthesis.py` (~430 LOC, pure stdlib + the existing `embed`/`community`/`store`/`llm` modules вҖ” no new deps) builds a brief straight from a cluster's members: (1) **centroid** = mean of member embeddings, L2-normalized so plain dot-product is cosine; (2) **cohesion** = mean `cosine(member, centroid)` вҲҲ [0,1] вҖ” a real "how tight is this topic" signal that doubles as a split-me-up hint when low; (3) **harvest** splits every member body into sentences and scores each by `cosine(sentence, centroid) + 0.04В·key_term_hits + 0.02В·source_centrality`; (4) **select** runs MMR-style dedup (drop any candidate whose cosine to an already-picked sentence > 0.86) with a two-pass diversifier that prefers one sentence per distinct note before backfilling вҖ” top 3 вҶ’ **overview**, next 5 вҶ’ **key claims**; (5) **compose** orders the overview sentences by their source note's centrality and stitches them into prose, every sentence carrying an inline `[#N]` citation into a Sources list numbered by centrality (so `[#N]` is stable + clickable); (6) **open threads** = member notes phrased as questions (title or a body sentence ends in `?`) plus *under-developed* members (body < 140 chars, or zero intra-cluster synapses computed from edges with both endpoints inside the cluster); (7) **bridges** = notes in *other* clusters with `cosine(note, centroid) вүҘ 0.16` that the synapse graph hasn't linked to any member вҖ” cross-pollination the graph is one П„-nudge from drawing, each carrying its own cluster id/name/colour. Degenerate cases handled: a stub-only cluster falls back its most-central note's opening line; a singleton cluster reports cohesion 1.0 and skips bridges/threads. **Optional LLM mode** (`SYNAPSE_LLM_KEY`) rewrites the overview under a strict contract (use ONLY numbered sources, every sentence ends `[#N]`, 2вҖ“3 sentences вүӨ80 words) вҖ” and we *reject* any LLM answer that drops its citations, falling back to extractive so synthesis never loses its receipts. `to_markdown()` renders a self-contained portable brief; `serialize()` ships the dataclasses as JSON. **Two new endpoints** in `main.py`: `GET /digest?cluster_id=&threshold&top_k&mode` (404s cleanly when the id doesn't exist at the given params) and `GET /digest/export.md?cluster_id=вҖҰ` (Content-Disposition attachment, slugified filename). `schemas.py` gains `ClusterDigestOut` + 4 nested models. **Frontend**: new `components/Synthesis.tsx` (~430 LOC) вҖ” a centered modal tinted with the cluster's own colour, a **cohesion ring** (conic-gradient, same idiom as the brief's score ring), the synthesis paragraph with `[#N]` markers parsed into **clickable superscript citation chips** (`ref` renamed off the reserved React prop name so the click handler actually fires), key-claim bullets, an **open-threads** list (`?` amber for questions, `в—Ӣ` pink for stubs, each opening the source note), a **bridges** list (target-cluster chip + cosine %), a numbered **sources** list, an **extractive/вңЁ llm** mode pill, and a **вӨ“ md** export anchor. `TopicPalette.tsx` grew a per-row вқҚ **synthesize** button (appears on hover, tinted the cluster colour) wired through a new `onSynthesize` prop; `page.tsx` mounts the modal with fallback name/colour from the loaded communities and resolves citation/source/bridge clicks back to the canvas inspector; `lib/types.ts` + `lib/api.ts` gain the `ClusterDigest` types, `api.digest()`, and `api.digestExportUrl()`. **Validation**: backend exercised against the seeded 16-note graph вҖ” all 4 clusters produce coherent, correctly-cited overviews (e.g. *Design* cohesion 0.57, *Hashing* surfaces a *Graph view вҶ’ Design* bridge at 21%), citation refs map 1-to-1 to sources, the singleton *Folder* cluster degrades gracefully, `GET /digest?cluster_id=99` вҶ’ 404, and `mode=llm` with no key returns the extractive fallback + honest notice. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `next build` ships clean (29.2 kB page, 116 kB first-load); dev server serves `/` 200 with no compile errors. README: new **Synthesis** entry in "What's in the box", a methodology block (7-step pipeline + cohesion/bridge definitions + LLM contract), architecture diagram + API table extended, roadmap item ticked. A `verdict` block grades the model (strong/fair/marginal/poor) and writes plain-English notes ("lowering the cut to 7 lifts recall 75%вҶ’100%"; "N known-bad accounts slip under the current cut"). Crucially it honours a candidate `weights` override, so a what-if hypothesis from the day-1 simulator is *validated*, not just admired вҖ” boosting the under-weighted fan detectors recovers the mule at higher precision than blindly dropping the threshold, and the headline tiles show the О”-vs-canonical to prove it. Endpoints `POST /aml/backtest` + `GET /aml/backtest/sample` (43-tx labelled set: 8 confirmed-bad across five typologies + two hard cases вҖ” an under-detected smurf = recall miss, a benign payroll account that trips the weak round-amount rule = false-positive trap). Pure function of `(transactions, labels, weights)` вҶ’ identical report every time = admissible model evidence. | 37 | 2026-05-29 | **Credicrew** | Round-8 opener: shipped the **Calibration Studio** (`/roles/[id]/calibration`) вҖ” the panel-fairness layer every interview surface had been missing. Until now every scorecard assumed a *single* rater (one composite, one verdict); real hiring runs panels, and the loudest hidden source of unfair decisions is uncalibrated interviewers вҖ” lenient vs. severe, flat/central-tendency, or simply off-consensus вҖ” so a candidate's fate turns on *who* happened to interview them. New `frontend/src/lib/calibration.ts` (~560 LOC, pure functions) models interviewers Г— candidates Г— rubric-dimensions and computes: (1) **per-rater bias** вҖ” *leniency* = mean deviation from the per-cell panel consensus (signed +lenient/вҲ’severe), *spread* = population stdev of their ratings (near-zero вҮ’ central-tendency "flat"), and *consensus correlation* = Pearson r against the cell means (low вҮ’ off-consensus), each auto-flagged `lenient`/`severe`/`flat`/`contrarian`; (2) **panel reliability** вҖ” a variance-based **consensus index** (`mean(1 вҲ’ cellVar/4)` over multi-rated cells) for cell-level agreement *plus* **ICC(1)**, an *unbalanced one-way* intraclass correlation over the candidateГ—dim cells (handles panels where different candidates were seen by different interviewers, which a balanced targetsГ—raters matrix can't) measuring how much rating variance is real candidate signal vs. rater noise; (3) the same ICC recomputed on **de-biased** ratings (each rater's leniency subtracted) вҖ” the headline insight: on a biased panel the lift is dramatic (the seed lands **ICC 0.00 вҶ’ 0.34**), proving calibration restores the panel's power to discriminate; (4) **raw vs. calibrated composites + rank shifts** вҖ” each candidate gets a raw consensus composite and a de-biased one (rater offsets removed before averaging), revealing that when the lenient EM only saw juniors and the severe staffer only saw seniors, the raw ranking *compresses* the real gap and calibration reorders the boundary candidates; (5) **disagreement hot-cells**, per-candidate flags (`single_rater`/`high_disagreement`/`thin`), an overall verdict (`calibrated`/`minor_drift`/`needs_calibration`/`unreliable`), suggestions and a Markdown report. New `frontend/src/lib/panel_seed.ts` builds a deterministic, deliberately **unbalanced** 4-person seed panel (Meera NairВ·lenient EM В· Arjun VermaВ·severe staff В· Sana KhanВ·calibrated senior В· Dev MenonВ·flat lead) hashed from role+candidate+dim so it's idempotent and lights the studio up on first open; Sana+Dev anchor the consensus while Meera sees only the lower-scoring half and Arjun only the upper half, manufacturing exactly the bias calibration then corrects. **Backend mirror** in `backend/app/services/calibration.py` (~430 LOC, stdlib only вҖ” `math`+dataclasses) is **byte-for-byte parity** with the TS engine, *verified* by transpiling `calibration.ts` standalone via the TypeScript compiler API and diffing a fixed 6-candidate / 90-rating fixture through both engines (every rater stat, cell, composite, rank, consensus index, raw+calibrated ICC and verdict matched exactly ex-timestamp); new `backend/app/routers/calibration.py` exposes `POST /calibration/summary` accepting `camelCase` (TS-engine `as_dict`) and `snake_case` (curl) via Pydantic `Field(alias=вҖҰ)` + `ConfigDict(populate_by_name=True)`. API version bumped `0.8.0 вҶ’ 0.9.0`; root index advertises the new route. **Frontend Calibration Studio** at `/roles/[id]/calibration` (14.2 kB / 121 kB First Load): gradient fuchsiaвҶ’sky title row with Manage-panel / Copy-report / Export-report.md; a 5-tile headline (verdict В· consensus index В· ICC with `вҶ’ de-biased` delta В· rank shifts В· biased-rater count); new `CalibrationBias` component (diverging severeвҶҗвҶ’lenient bars per interviewer with spread/consensus-r chips + flag pills); new `RankShiftChart` (an SVG **bump chart** connecting each candidate's raw rank вҶ’ calibrated rank, climbs in emerald / drops in rose, with composite + О” labels); new `AgreementGrid` (candidate Г— dimension heatmap tinted by agreement via a roseвҶ’amberвҶ’emerald `agreementHue`, hot-cells ringed, **click any cell to inspect every rater's rating and edit it inline 1вҖ“5** вҖ” bias, ranking and reliability all recompute live off a `useMemo`); new `PanelDrawer` (add/remove interviewers вҖ” new ones auto-scored on the whole shortlist via a chosen archetype вҖ” + reset-to-seed); a hot-cell list and an actions/notes panel. Theme: ~10 new `.cc-cal-*` selectors in `globals.css` (verdict/ bias/ bump radial-gradient accents, cell hover scale, inspector glow, drawer slide reusing the existing `cc-parity-slide` keyframe). Role-detail header gained a `Calibration вҶ’` button (fuchsiaвҶ’sky gradient, disabled until the shortlist is non-empty), beside Decision Studio. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `next build` clean across 12 routes (`/roles/[id]/calibration` 14.2 kB, every other route unchanged, shared chunks steady at 87.1 kB); `next dev` serves `GET /roles/test-id/calibration` 200 with no runtime errors; FastAPI `TestClient` smoke green (camel + snake payloads agree on verdict, empty-panel guard returns `verdict=unreliable` + `icc=null`, seed fixture returns 4 rank shifts + 2 biased raters + ICC 0.00вҶ’0.34); cross-engine fixture diff = exact match. README rewritten: opening blurb extended, new **"What's new вҖ” Calibration Studio (Day 37)"** section (bias metrics, consensus + ICC, de-bias recovery, rank shifts, heatmap, panel CRUD, backend mirror), `POST /calibration/summary` curl example + endpoint-map row, structure tree extended with `calibration.py` (router + service) + `calibration.ts` + `panel_seed.ts` + `calibration/page.tsx` + the four new components, roadmap entry ticked. (No headless browser was available in this environment for pixel-level UI verification вҖ” the studio was validated via tsc + next build + dev-server 200 + the cross-engine fixture diff and router smoke; the `.cc-cal-*` CSS reuses the established dark glass / ring / grid primitives the Decision & Peer-Parity surfaces already render.) |

| 38 | 2026-05-30 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-8 move: shipped **Eval Suites** вҖ” the regression-test layer every prior surface in the playground had been missing. Arena measures *one* prompt Г— N models, Judge scores it, Consensus debiases it, Vote ELOs it, History persists it, Library versions it, Insights aggregates it вҖ” but nothing in the studio let you run the **same fixed battery of cases** against every candidate model and watch for *regressions* when you change a prompt or swap a model. That's what real LLM-ops needs and what every commercial tool (Braintrust, Langfuse, PromptLayer) builds first; the playground now has it natively. New `backend/src/evals.py` (~720 LOC, pure-stdlib + `ThreadPoolExecutor`) models *suites* (named, ordered case lists with tag/star/desc), *cases* (a user prompt + AND-combined pass criteria: `expected_contains`, `expected_not_contains`, `expected_regex` via `re.search`, `expect_json` that strips ```json fences before `json.loads`, `judge_min` composite threshold), *runs* (one execution against a provider+model with optional judge), and *case_results* (response, status, latency, cost, judge composite + rationale, pass bool, and a per-criterion `reasons[]` array вҖ” every rule's `{kind, expected, ok, detail?}` so the UI never has to guess *why* a case failed). The engine fan-outs cases through a 6-worker pool вҖ” a 12-case suite finishes in ~2Г— the slowest call, not 12Г— вҖ” then runs a parallel judging pass that reuses the existing `judge_compare` path so the math is provably identical to the Arena's `/judge` endpoint. **Schema** lives in the same `history.db` (single backup captures everything): `eval_suites` + `eval_cases` (with re-packed `idx` on delete so the UI stays gap-free) + `eval_runs` + `eval_case_results`, all guarded with `CREATE IF NOT EXISTS` and bulletproof child-row cleanup on `delete_suite` regardless of `PRAGMA foreign_keys` state. Aggregates: `pass_rate`, `avg_composite`, `total_cost`, `wall_latency` (max-parallel) vs `total_latency` (serial-sum) so the UI can show **the parallelism dividend**. **`compare_runs(a, b)`** joins cases by `case_id` first, falling back to `case_idx` (so a renamed case still pairs), and produces per-case `delta.composite` + a `delta.passed` of **+1 = fixed**, **вҲ’1 = regressed**, **0 = same** вҖ” a single column tells you whether the new model fixed cases or broke them. **`seed_smoke_suite()`** is idempotent and seeds a 6-case starter battery (factual recall В· refusal В· JSON formatting В· arithmetic В· summarisation `judge_min: 70` В· code synthesis regex) so a brand-new user presses *Run* in 10 seconds and sees every column populate. **16 new routes** in `routes/llm.py` (`POST/GET/DELETE /api/suites`, `/seed`, `/stats`, `/<id>/meta`, `/<id>/cases` + `/<id>/cases/<cid>` (POST=update, DELETE=delete), `/<id>/cases/reorder`, `/<id>/runs` (POST=execute, GET=list), `/runs/<rid>` (GET=detail, DELETE), `/runs/compare`) all wired into `api.js` with a matching narrow client. **Frontend Eval Suites panel** (`components/EvalSuites.jsx`, ~1100 LOC): a gradient indigoвҶ’violetвҶ’fuchsia hero header; a 5-tile **stats banner** (suites В· cases В· runs+avg-pass В· spend В· best-model crown by avg pass-rate across all its runs); a left-rail **suite list** with per-row stats (case count В· run count В· last-run-relative В· model:provider chip + pass-rate bar pinned to the latest run) and a starred-only toggle; a right-pane that swaps between an empty state (with a "**Seed Smoke Test**" CTA + blank-suite alternative вҖ” first-click delight) and a full **suite workspace** stacking *Suite header / Run Config panel / Case list editor / Recent runs / Run report / Compare drawer*. The **Run Config panel** (`Provider` + `Model` selects auto-populated via `/api/models/<provider>`, an optional system prompt that's applied to every case, and a `judge` switch that reveals judge provider+model selects with the same wiring) issues one `/runs` call and toasts the pass-rate verdict on return. The **Case editor** is a single grid with `Must contain` / `Must NOT contain` / `Regex match` / `Response must parse as JSON` switch / `Judge min (0-100)` / note, validates the prompt is non-empty, and saves to either `/cases` (new) or `/cases/<cid>` (edit). The **Case row** renders a chip-row of every criterion with a 1-char glyph (`+ вҲ’ / {} вүҘ вң“`) so the suite's *intent* is readable in two seconds; **smoke-only** cases (no criteria) get a single `вң“ non-empty response` chip вҖ” the engine and the UI agree on what "no criteria means pass". The **Run report** is four gradient KPI tiles (Pass-rate ring + breakdown В· Avg-composite + judged-share В· Total cost + per-case В· Wall-time + serial-sum), a **criteria breakdown** card that pivots every AND-combined rule across all cases ("`regex` passed 4/5 В· `judge_min` passed 3/5") with mini pass-rate bars per kind, and an accordion of per-case rows whose collapsed state shows pass chip + composite + cost + latency + the per-criterion reason chips and whose expanded state lays out *prompt | response | judge rationale* side-by-side. The **Compare drawer** picks two runs of the same suite (UI: a `vs` button per run row that cycles AвҶ’B), fetches `/runs/compare`, and renders a 3-column summary (A В· B В· BвҲ’A delta вҖ” pass-rate / composite / cost / wall-time, with **invert=true** on cost+latency so cheaper/faster reads green), then a per-case table with PassChip-per-side В· О”-composite В· and a **"fixed | regressed | same"** column with up/down/minus icons. App wiring: a new **"Suites"** radio at the bottom of the sidebar (FlaskConical icon, `new` gradient ribbon) + a render branch at the top of the main-column switch (`selectedMode === 'suites' вҶ’ <EvalSuites />`). **Validation**: `pnpm build` clean (1729 modules вҶ’ 606 kB gzip:171 kB); a Flask `test_client` walked all 10 user-paths end-to-end against a monkey-patched `FakeProvider` (seed вҶ’ list вҶ’ detail вҶ’ create вҶ’ add case вҶ’ run вҶ’ stats вҶ’ update case вҶ’ second run вҶ’ compare вҶ’ delete) вҖ” every status code 200/201, the seed run reported `pass=5/6 rate=83.33%` with the 5th case correctly failing on `judge_min: 70` without judging enabled and the per-criterion reason `"judge_min:N В· no judge run for this case"` proving the engine surfaces *why* every case fails. README rewritten with a new top-of-page **"What's new вҖ” Eval Suites"** section (criteria table, pass-criteria philosophy, full 16-endpoint API surface, `/runs` request schema, `/runs/compare` response schema with the `delta.passed = +1/вҲ’1/0` callout), Studio Insights demoted to a sub-section. | 39 | 2026-05-31 | **SynapseOS** | Round-8 move: shipped **Tensions вҖ” where your second brain disagrees with itself** вҖ” the contradiction-surfacing layer no PKM tool has. Every prior surface reveals what *agrees* (synapses link, clusters bind, Synthesis paraphrases the consensus); none surface where the graph *contradicts itself*, and that's the highest-value PKM signal вҖ” a note that says "boring tech wins" sitting next to "that framework was a mistake" is an *unreconciled belief*, exactly the thing a thinking partner should flag. New `backend/app/tensions.py` (~600 LOC, pure stdlib, zero new deps) is the engine. For every pair `(a, b)` with `cosine(a, b) вүҘ floor` (default `0.18`, tuned slightly above П„ so tensions are pulled from the *connected* graph not random buzzword collisions), it runs four detectors and emits a `Tension` when any fire with non-trivial weight: (1) **polarity** вҖ” hand-tuned valence lexicons (POSITIVE `good В· best В· ship В· wins В· works В· scale В· вҖҰ`, NEGATIVE `bad В· worst В· breaks В· fails В· overrated В· slow В· вҖҰ`) plus a one-content-word negation window that flips local valence ("not bad" вҶ’ positive, "not great" вҶ’ negative) so the naive bag-of-words doesn't get reversed by hedging; fires when `sign(pol_a) вү  sign(pol_b)` *and* `min(|pol_a|, |pol_b|) вүҘ 1` so a single polar word per side doesn't trip the rule, weight = `min(1, span/6)`; (2) **antonym** вҖ” a 28-pair lexicon (simple/complex, fast/slow, overrated/underrated, robust/brittle, durable/fragile, вҖҰ) checked against each side's word set, weight saturates at two pairs because contradictions aren't additive; (3) **contrast** вҖ” both-sided contrast cues (but, however, although, instead, rather, actually, вҖҰ); a "but" on *one* side is just writing, a "but" on *both* means each is qualifying the other's frame, weight = `min(1, 0.3 + 0.15В·(min(ca,cb)вҲ’1))`; (4) **title-clash** вҖ” explicit "Against X" vs "Why X works" with light singular/plural stemming (`folder вүҲ folders`, the most common plural that originally broke obvious pairs) and stopword filter (so "the" doesn't crown a false match), *plus* opposite-polarity titles with a shared non-polar topic token. The **title-clash bypass** lets unambiguous title contention surface even *below* the cosine floor вҖ” the hashing-trick embedder is what it is, and a deterministic linguistic signal shouldn't be overridden by `cosine = 0.04`. `magnitude = clip(cosine В· (1 + ОЈ weights), 0, 1)` so cosine sets the ceiling and signals scale within it. Each emitted `Tension` carries: `kind вҲҲ {internal, cross}` (same-cluster вҖ” where you expected agreement and got conflict вҖ” vs philosophical disagreement across topics), the firing `signals[]` with per-signal `(kind, weight, detail)`, two `evidence` quotes (one per side, the **most-polarized sentence in each note in the direction of that note's own stance** вҖ” picked via per-note pre-pass over sentence-split bodies, fallback to opening sentence for neutral framings), and a `bridge_title + bridge_prompt + bridge_tags` triple auto-generated from the firing signal kinds ("When X applies vs when Y" for antonym pairs, "Reconciling: X вҶ” Y" for polarity, "Bridge: X & Y" otherwise) so **Reconcile** is one click. **Two new endpoints**: `GET /tensions?floor=&limit=&threshold=&top_k=` returns the full report (threshold В· floor В· total_pairs_scanned В· candidate_count В· tension_count В· tensions[] В· stats with internal/cross counts and top_magnitude), `GET /tensions/export.md` ships the same report as a portable artifact (sectioned by Inside-a-cluster / Across-clusters, both quotes with `вҶ‘/вҶ“` arrows, signal line, **Reconcile:** prompt) вҖ” paste into Notion / journal / anywhere. New Pydantic schemas (`TensionSignalOut`, `TensionEvidenceOut`, `TensionOut`, `TensionReportOut`); API version bumped `0.2.0 вҶ’ 0.3.0`. **Frontend Tensions modal** (`components/Tensions.tsx`, ~530 LOC): roseвҶ’violet header strip (rose because contradiction, not violet because not just-another-cluster), a custom logo glyph (two circles connected by a jagged disagreement line), **3 filter chips** with live counts (all / inside a cluster / across clusters) and an `вӨ“ md` export link; per-tension **card** with a magnitude meter bar at the top (roseвҶ’pink gradient with `box-shadow: 0 0 12px {accent}55` to read as "alive"), a 3-column headline grid (`title A | вҹ· | title B`) where each title is clickable to inspect the note and shows its cluster color-dot + name, a `kind` micro-label and `magnitude% В· cos N%` readout in the middle column, **signal chips** with a one-char glyph (`вҶ• вҮ„ вү  вҖј`) + label (`stance / antonyms / but-cues / title clash`) + the engine's `detail` string, a **2-column evidence grid** (one quote per side, italic with `border-left: 2px solid {accent}66`, `вҶ‘/вҶ“/В·` polarity arrow in lime/rose/grey), and a **suggested bridge** panel with the title/prompt and a gradient cyanвҶ’violet **вӨҙ Reconcile** button that fires `onReconcile(draft)`. The composer is extended to accept an optional `draft` prop: on receive it pre-fills `(title, body, tags)`, **scrolls itself into view with `requestAnimationFrame` + `scrollIntoView`** so the user lands on the form, **focuses the body textarea** with `setSelectionRange(0,0)` so typing immediately appends to the prompt, and shows a 2.2s pulse вҖ” a rose ring + shadow + `вӨҙ reconciling` floating chip вҖ” to confirm what just happened. **Header trigger** is a rose-bordered pill (`вҹ· tensions`) with a live count badge (the page does a cheap `api.tensions({ limit: 50 })` probe after every graph refresh and renders `N` or `99+`) вҖ” *your second brain has N unresolved contradictions* is now a glanceable header stat. **Seed extended** with two notes that manufacture a tension on first run ("Unit tests are underrated" vs the existing "The test pyramid is overrated", and "Why folders work" vs the existing "Against the folder") so the modal isn't empty on cold start; the seed graph now contains 18 notes and surfaces **5 tensions** (3 internal В· 2 cross В· top magnitude 0.44) at default settings вҖ” covering all four signal types (antonym, polarity, contrast, title-clash). **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean across the new component + every existing one; `next build` clean (Route `/` 32.6 kB В· First Load JS 120 kB В· 4 static pages); FastAPI `TestClient` smoke green (`/health 200`, `/graph 200`, `/communities 200`, `/orphans 200`, `/search 200`, `/brief 200`, `/tensions 200`, `/chat 200` вҖ” every pre-existing endpoint still works); a full schema-shape test asserts all 14 required keys per tension, polarity arrows present in markdown, floor sweep is monotonic (`{0.05 вҶ’ 15, 0.10 вҶ’ 12, 0.18 вҶ’ 5, 0.25 вҶ’ 2, 0.4 вҶ’ 1}`), empty-DB and single-note edge cases return `tension_count = 0` cleanly. README extended with a top-of-features **Tensions** bullet, a new in-depth **"Tensions"** section (signal table В· magnitude formula В· title-clash bypass rationale В· per-tension shape В· markdown export), two new API-table rows (`/tensions`, `/tensions/export.md`), modal listed in the architecture diagram, and `tensions.py` added to the backend module tree. | 40 | 2026-06-01 | **Titan** | Round-8 move: shipped **Behavioral Drift** вҖ” the *account-vs-self* anomaly layer that complements every prior surface. The eight rule detectors catch **threshold breaches** вҖ” a transaction crossed a line. They cannot catch the inverse failure mode: **accounts whose recent behavior no longer matches their own historical baseline** вҖ” sleeper takeovers, mule recruitments, slow operator shifts where the line itself moved, no single transaction crossed it. New `apps/ai-aml/drift.py` (~720 LOC, pure stdlib, zero new deps) is the engine. For each account it splits transactions into a **baseline** + **current** window (configurable: `baseline_fraction` 0.2вҖ“0.9 or an explicit ISO `split_at`; the latter lets an analyst test their own "I think it started here" hypothesis against the data) and computes a fingerprint across **ten distribution-distance axes**: (1) **`amount`** вҖ” two-sample Kolmogorov-Smirnov on tx amounts, weight `0.18`; (2) **`hour`** вҖ” Jensen-Shannon divergence on a 24-bucket hour-of-day histogram (normalised by ln 2), weight `0.14`; (3) **`dow`** вҖ” same JS on a 7-bucket day-of-week histogram, weight `0.10`; (4) **`direction`** вҖ” abs delta in inflow/total ratio scaled so a 50pp swing saturates, weight `0.10`; (5) **`velocity`** вҖ” abs log-ratio of tx-per-active-day scaled by log 5 (a 5Г— spike saturates), weight `0.08`; (6) **`cparty_diversity`** вҖ” abs delta in Herfindahl-Hirschman of counterparty share, weight `0.08`; (7) **`cparty_novelty`** вҖ” share of current counterparties **never seen** in the baseline window (the single most-predictive axis in real laundering вҖ” clean accounts don't suddenly grow new payee lists), weight `0.12`; (8) **`geo`** вҖ” total-variation distance between baseline-mix and current-mix geo vectors, weight `0.08`; (9) **`round_rate`** вҖ” abs delta in % of round-amount transfers (` >= 1k and amt % 1k == 0`), weight `0.05`; (10) **`median_shift`** вҖ” abs logвӮӮ shift of median amount scaled by 3 (an 8Г— change saturates), weight `0.07`. Weights sum to exactly 1.0 (`assert` on import). Composite `overall = clip(ОЈ wбөў В· scoreбөў, 0, 1)` mapped to five verdict bands: `stable <0.18 В· mild <0.35 В· drifting <0.55 В· erratic <0.75 В· transformed вүҘ0.75`. The engine also derives: **drivers** (axes whose contribution clears `DRIVER_FLOOR В· overall`, top 3), an auto-generated **narrative** that strings together the top-driver `detail` + new-counterparty list + median-shift line + inflow/outflow flip + change-point onset, a **suggested_action** keyed off verdict ("escalate вҖ” promote to a case at high priority and confirm account-holder identity" at the top end), a **counterparty contribution table** (top 8 sorted with brand-new entrants first, each row with `baseline_count/current_count/baseline_volume/current_volume/is_new/activity_lift/volume_lift`), and a **change-point estimate**: walks the current window day by day, computes KS of the trailing 7-day slice against the *full baseline*, reports the earliest day above `CHANGE_POINT_KS_FLOOR = 0.30` (with `n >= 3` in the slice) as `onset_iso + days_ago`. The full rolling-KS series ships with the response so the frontend draws a curve with a dashed-floor guide and a pulsing onset dot. **Three new endpoints** in `apps/ai-aml/main.py`: `GET /aml/drift/rules` (auditor view of weights, bands, dim labels, every tunable), `GET /aml/drift/sample` (a deterministic three-account demo вҖ” `ACC-STABLE` routine vendor pattern, `ACC-MILD` gentle growth, `ACC-DRIFT` 18-week sleeper that wakes up into a 9-day round-amount burst вҖ” plus a `recommended_split_at` ISO timestamp so the demo teaches the tool), `POST /aml/drift` (`{ transactions, account_id?, baseline_fraction?, split_at? }` вҶ’ portfolio-ranked report or single-account detail; portfolio mode skips accounts with `< MIN_BASELINE_TXS(6) + MIN_CURRENT_TXS(3)` on either side and surfaces them in `skipped[]`). Engine version bumped `titan-aml/1.6.0 вҶ’ 1.7.0`. **Gateway**: three pass-through routes in `apps/api/main.py` (10 s timeout for the cheap `rules`/`sample` GETs, 30 s for the `/aml/drift` POST since portfolio mode over a large book can run the engine 20Г— in one call). **API client**: ~150 LOC of new TS types in `apps/frontend/lib/api.ts` covering `DriftVerdict В· DriftDimensionKey В· DriftDimension В· DriftCounterparty В· DriftChangePoint В· DriftWindow В· DriftReport В· DriftPortfolioSummary В· DriftResponse В· DriftRules В· DriftSample` plus `getDriftRules() В· getDriftSample() В· runDrift()`. **Frontend `/drift` console** (`app/drift/page.tsx`, ~620 LOC; **page bundle 8.91 kB В· First Load JS 96 kB**): a glass-strong **hero strip** (round-8 В· day-40 ribbon, gradient headline, Load-demo + Run-analysis buttons, auto-loaded demo with the recommended split pre-set so the page is *never* empty on first visit); a controls section with a CSV textarea (live row count) + scope toggle (Portfolio В· Single-account) + a window-split control that flips between a fraction slider (`0.2вҖ“0.9`, step `0.05`) and an explicit ISO timestamp; a **6-tile portfolio summary** (accounts В· drifters В· per-verdict counts) tinted with the verdict hex; a **ranked left-rail** (per-row verdict pill + gradient bar + composite %, click to swap the active report); and the showpiece вҖ” the **active report**: a verdict-tinted **hero ring** (132px conic-gradient on `var(--drift-accent)`, glowing via `ws-drift-ring-glow` for `drifting/erratic/transformed`, the headline + plain-English narrative + recommended-action block beside it), the **`DriftRadar`** (`components/DriftRadar.tsx`, 10-axis polar SVG вҖ” baseline silhouette pinned to the outer rim as a dashed teal reference, current silhouette plotted **inwards** by `1 - score` so a perfectly-matching axis lands on the rim and a fully-drifted axis collapses to the center; | 41 | 2026-06-02 | **WaySafe** | Round-9 opener: shipped **StaySafe вҖ” Accommodation Safety Picker**, the *bookable* counterpart to Compass. Compass answers "where should I *go* tonight?" вҖ” a single-point-in-time visit. StaySafe answers "where should I *sleep*?" вҖ” a fundamentally different question because you spend 16+ hours/day at a stay across the sleep / evening-return / morning-depart windows. New `stays.py` (~580 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `safety` + `forecast`, zero new deps) is the engine. **Six 0..1 sub-dimensions** scored per candidate, composite = weighted sum Г— 100: (1) **`sleep`** вҖ” mean blended risk 22:00вҶ’06:00 on check-in date (weight 0.30); (2) **`evening`** вҖ” mean 19:00вҶ’22:00 (0.20); (3) **`morning`** вҖ” mean 06:00вҶ’09:00 (0.10). Each window is a **45/55 blend** of `forecaster.risk_at(when)` (DOWГ—hour patterns) and `safety.point_risk(when)` (static incident proximity + geofence + late-night + help-POI physics) so a stay surrounded by recent verified incidents is *always* downgraded even when the forecaster has no late-night history for that cell. (4) **`walkability`** (0.18) вҖ” mean goodness over (hospital / police / clinic) walk legs with ceilings 4 / 2 / 1.5 km; **gracefully degrades to 2-of-3** when the dataset has no clinic POIs (the project's POI set has only hospitals + police, so this matters in practice). (5) **`quiet`** (0.12) вҖ” inverse Sentinel cluster pressure within 0.8 km of the property, with night-active clusters (peak_hour вҲҲ [20..3]) carrying a **1.6Г— multiplier** so loud-by-night hotspots can't hide behind quiet-by-day. (6) **`reach`** (0.10) вҖ” **U-shaped** distance to the trip's own centre of gravity (mean of the candidate stays' coords; falls back to attraction POIs, then any POI); sweet spot 1.5 km, full penalty under 0.2 km (too central / crowded) or beyond 6 km (too isolated). **Geofence floor**: if the property sits inside a risk-zone polygon the composite is forced to вүӨ 59 (Elevated) regardless of the per-window math. **Four traveller profiles** rebalance the dimension weights вҖ” Solo (sleep 0.32, evening 0.24, morning 0.08, walk 0.18, quiet 0.10, reach 0.08), Couple (default), Family-with-kids (walk 0.22 + quiet 0.16), Business/solo-F (sleep 0.34) вҖ” and `compare_stays(profile=...)` plugs them in. Verdict layer: ranks 2..8 candidates (compass score desc В· then better worst-window В· then closer hospital), names the winner with margin ("Recommend Vivanta Goa Panaji вҖ” 14 pts clear of Lemon Tree Amarante Candolim"), surfaces the **deciding factor** via the largest *weight-multiplied* goodness gap in the winner's favour, and produces a one-line plain-English **why_pick** per stay assembled from the actual numbers (e.g. "Hospital 1.2 km away; calm sleep window."). **JSON** (`waysafe.staysafe.v1`) and **markdown** exports for WhatsApp / email / Notion paste. **Frontend**: new `StaySafe` tab between Compass and Sentinel (existing tab indices 7..11 shifted to 8..12). The render stack вҖ” `theme.render_staysafe` (~180 LOC theme additions, ~250 LOC of `.ws-stay-*` CSS) вҖ” opens with a **hero card** (winner's 0вҖ“100 ring, level chip, profile chip, check-in/nights/N-stays meta, `+pts ahead` margin), a **podium row** of stay cards (rank chip В· kind chip В· level chip В· score bar В· sleep/evening/morning tri-cell В· **24-hour risk sparkline** with one bar per hour hue-coded greenвҶ”red by risk В· headline blurb В· `why_pick` rationale below a dashed divider), a **three-column walk-to-help** card for the winner only (hospital / police / clinic each as name + distance + walk-time at 4.8 km/h + goodness bar), and a **heat-mapped factor matrix** (stays as columns, factors as rows, every cell hue-coded greenвҶ”red by goodness with a sub-cell showing the **weighted points contribution** so users see *which* dimension is driving the score). Below the matrix: a per-stay text breakdown in an expander + JSON/markdown download buttons. **Demo data**: new `data/stays.csv` ships 15 curated Goa stays (premium resorts ITC Grand Goa / Hyatt / Taj Holiday Village / Park Hyatt / Radisson Blu / Vivanta / Lemon Tree / Mayfair В· mid-tier The Park Calangute / Whispering Palms / Anjuna Beach Resort В· hostels Mantra Anjuna + The Hosteller Vagator + Old Quarter Hostel В· homestay Casa Britona). On the bundled incidents.csv with the corridor seed + Family-with-kids profile + Tue 15:00 check-in, the engine ranks Vivanta Goa Panaji (urban, GMC 1.2 km / police 0.4 km) at **88/100 All-clear** vs Lemon Tree Amarante Candolim at 79 vs The Park Calangute at 59 Elevated (forced floor вҖ” inside the demo corridor geofence) вҖ” a clear, defensible verdict that exercises every dimension. **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` clean on all three modified files (`app.py`, `theme.py`, `stays.py`); end-to-end engine test (load 15 stays вҶ’ compare 6 across two profiles вҶ’ JSON round-trip + markdown render) produces meaningful differentiation (88 vs 79 vs 76 across profiles, reach goodness varying 0.0..0.84 once the centroid is the candidate-mean); `render_staysafe` exercised with a captured-stdout mock streamlit and produces 27 K of HTML across 6 markdown blocks with every expected CSS marker present (`ws-stay-hero В· ws-stay-podium В· ws-stay-matrix В· ws-stay-card В· ws-stay-spark В· ws-stay-legs`); `streamlit run app.py --headless` boots clean (HTTP 200 on `/_stcore/health`, no init-time exceptions). README rewritten with a new top-of-features StaySafe bullet, a dedicated **"StaySafe вҖ” Accommodation Safety Picker (Day 41)"** section (six-dimension table with formulas + defaults, profile re-weighting table, verdict surface walkthrough, exports). |

| 42 | 2026-06-03 | **Credicrew** | Round-9 move: shipped **Channel Studio вҖ” Sourcing Intelligence**, the missing top-of-funnel surface. Every other Credicrew surface analyses what happens *after* a candidate is already in pipeline (match В· interview В· calibration В· decision В· offer В· peer parity В· portfolio health) вҖ” none of them answer the question that sits *above* all of it: *where should I spend my next hour of outreach?* New `frontend/src/lib/sources.ts` (~430 LOC, pure functions, no new deps) is the engine. **Eight-channel taxonomy** вҖ” `linkedin_outreach В· referral В· job_post В· agency В· community В· university В· ai_sourcing В· silver_medal` вҖ” with per-channel labels, blurbs, and **default cost-per-touch** (`agency` 60k dominates, `linkedin_outreach` 4k, `job_post` 1k, `silver_medal` 1k вҖҰ) reflecting how recruiters actually spend. **Four-dial ROI** вҖ” every channel scored on (a) **quality** `0.4В·meanMatch + 0.4В·meanComposite + 20В·meanWinProb` with absent-component re-normalisation (so a channel without offers yet isn't unfairly punished вҖ” same philosophy as the interview rubric), (b) **conversion** `100В·(1 вҲ’ e^(вҲ’12В·reachedOffer/count))` so 25% to-offer вүҲ 90 / 10% вүҲ 60 / 5% вүҲ 35, (c) **cost efficiency** `100 вҲ’ 0.085В·costPerOffer(вӮ№k)` so вӮ№50k/offer вүҲ 95 / вӮ№500k вүҲ 40, (d) **speed** `clip(120 вҲ’ 2.5В·meanDaysToOffer, 0, 100)`. Composite **ROI** = `0.4В·quality + 0.3В·conversion + 0.2В·cost + 0.1В·speed`, banded `scale вүҘ 70 В· steady вүҘ 50 В· experiment вүҘ 35 В· cut < 35` with `count < 4` short-circuiting to `experiment` (the engine never recommends "scale" from a single data point). **Per-channel funnel** вҖ” five-stage cumulative reached counts + adjacent-stage conversion rates. **Diversification** = normalised Shannon entropy across channel counts (`< 0.5` triggers concentration-risk alert). **Per-channel recommendation** strings written from the actual numbers ("Cost-per-offer вӮ№230k is too high вҖ” pause Recruiter agency unless quality lifts.", "Highest-quality + highest-converting channel вҖ” double InMail seats / referral bonuses here this quarter."). **Top-level recommendations** surface: strongest `scale` channel, weakest `cut` channel, **concentration-risk** flag when one channel owns > 55% of the active pipeline, promote-to-experiment flag for thin-but-high-quality channels (count вүҘ 2, quality вүҘ 70). **Markdown brief** for standup / budget review. | 43 | 2026-06-04 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-9 move: shipped **Rubrics Studio** вҖ” the missing first-class layer underneath every existing judge surface. The playground has had eight surfaces that *score* things (Arena, single judge, multi-judge consensus, blind Vote, History, Library, Insights, Eval Suites) but only one rubric type: an inline `[{name, description, weight}]` list that returns one composite per candidate. Domain evaluation needs more вҖ” RAG needs "Groundedness" with a 0-anchor that calls out unsupported claims; code review needs "Edge cases" with anchors that distinguish nil-handling from concurrency-safety; support needs "Tone" with explicit blame-the-customer 0-anchors. New `backend/src/rubrics.py` (~870 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `history`'s DB path/lock + `pricing.estimate_cost`) models *rubrics* (named, tag/star/desc + a `current_revision_num` pointer), *revisions* (append-only chain of `(dimensions_json, judge_addendum, note, parent_revision)` вҖ” like `prompt_versions`), and *judgements* (the log of every "Test this rubric" call: prompt, response, per-dim scores with rationales, summary, judge latency + cost + tokens). **Dimension model**: each dimension carries `{name, weight, description, anchors: {0,5,10}}` вҖ” anchors are 0/5/10 textual descriptors the judge prompt serialises *verbatim* so the LLM scores against an explicit yardstick, not its own intuition. `_normalise_dimensions` clamps weights to вүҘ0, re-packs them to **integer percents summing to exactly 100** using the largest-remainder method (deterministic, UI sees clean integers, composite math doesn't drift), and clips field lengths so the schema stays sane. **Judging engine**: `build_rubric_judge_prompt` renders dimension blocks (`weight%`, description, anchor rows with level-coloured backgrounds in the UI's preview) + the user prompt + optional system prompt + optional judge addendum + the response under inspection + a strict JSON output schema. `_JUDGE_SYSTEM` is a single calibrated paragraph forcing 0-10 range usage ("a mediocre response should land near 5, a refusal or off-topic answer should land near 0-2"). `parse_rubric_response` strips ```json fences, walks balanced `{...}` blocks, tolerates case-insensitive dim keys, clamps every score to [0, 10], and falls back to zeros + a sentinel rationale + `parsed_ok: false` when the judge's JSON is malformed вҖ” the UI surfaces the failure with a `judge JSON malformed вҖ” scored as 0s` chip instead of silently scoring 0. `_composite` is the *server-side* truth вҖ” `ОЈ (score_i / 10 Г— weight_i / 100) Г— 100` clipped to 0..100, computed from per-dim scores and the *rubric's* weights, so a misbehaving judge can never poison the headline number. **Revisions**: `update_rubric` computes a deterministic signature over `(dimensions, judge_addendum)` and short-circuits identical-payload saves with no change-note as no-ops (no revision bump, no DB write) вҖ” meta-only edits go through `set_rubric_meta` (no revision). `restore_revision` copies an older revision's dimensions forward as a new revision so r1 вҶ’ r4 = "we restored r1, and now r4 is the current" вҖ” history stays honest. **Schema** lives in the same `history.db` (single backup captures everything): `rubrics` + `rubric_revisions` + `rubric_judgements`, all guarded with `CREATE IF NOT EXISTS` and indexed on `updated_at DESC`, `starred`, `(rubric_id, revision_num DESC)`, `(rubric_id, created_at DESC)`, `(candidate_provider, candidate_model)`. **Concurrency**: shares `history._DB_LOCK` (non-reentrant `threading.Lock`); the no-op path in `update_rubric` deliberately exits the `with` block before calling back into `get_rubric` to avoid the deadlock that catches every "lock + helper-call" refactor (caught by my own first test run вҖ” bug fixed before commit). **Aggregates** mean something: `list_rubrics` attaches per-row `n_dimensions`, `dimension_names`, `n_judgements`, `avg_composite`; `get_rubric` adds `total_cost`, `recent_judgements[8]`, the full revision chain. `stats()` exposes `n_rubrics`, `n_starred`, `n_judgements`, total spend, average composite, the **best candidate model** across all judgements (min 3, ordered by avg composite desc), the **top rubric** by usage, and the **top 5 judges** with usage / avg composite / avg latency / total spend. **Seed**: `seed_rubrics()` is idempotent вҖ” Code Review (40/20/20/20), RAG Faithfulness (40/25/20/15), Customer Support (30/30/25/15), Creative Writing (30/25/25/20), each with full anchors written for the actual failure modes ("Doesn't compile / runs but produces wrong output / hallucinated APIs" at the 0 mark on Correctness; "Multiple confident claims absent from the context" at the 0 mark on Groundedness). Existing rubrics by the same name are left alone on re-seed; Code Review is starred so the first-launch UI immediately surfaces something. **13 new routes** in `routes/llm.py`: `GET/POST /api/rubrics`, `POST /api/rubrics/seed`, `GET /api/rubrics/stats`, `GET/DELETE /api/rubrics/:id`, `POST /api/rubrics/:id/meta`, `POST /api/rubrics/:id/revisions` (save-iff-changed), `POST /api/rubrics/:id/revisions/:n/restore`, `POST /api/rubrics/:id/test` (the judging engine), `GET /api/rubrics/:id/judgements`, `DELETE /api/rubrics/judgements/:jid`. **Frontend `RubricsStudio.jsx`** (~1180 LOC; sits between Suites and the bottom of the sidebar): a glass-strong **hero banner** (indigoвҶ’violetвҶ’fuchsia gradient with radial-glow corners, Round-9 ribbon, "Build the yardstick the judge uses" headline, new-rubric + seed CTAs) wraps a 5-tile KPI strip (Rubrics В· Judgements В· Avg composite В· Total spend В· Best model crown) that morphs the moment any rubric is judged. | 44 | 2026-06-05 | **SynapseOS** | Round-9 move: shipped **Echo вҖ” semantic deduplication studio**. Every prior surface in SynapseOS treats similarity as a virtue (synapses draw it, communities cluster it, Synthesis paraphrases it, Chat retrieves along it); Echo flips the sign. As a second brain matures you accumulate near-duplicates вҖ” the same insight rewritten weeks apart вҖ” and those polyphonic restatements pollute the graph (false hubs), inflate cluster sizes, and dirty search. New `backend/app/echo.py` (~540 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of the existing embedder / `store._conn` / `_pack`) is a pure function of `(notes, embeddings, threshold, skips)`: pair cosines вүҘ `П„` (default **0.72**, configurable per-call) form an undirected edge set; **single-linkage union-find** yields connected components of size вүҘ 2 (single-linkage is intentional вҖ” if AвүҲB and BвүҲC, you want A and C in the same merge UI even when A and C only just miss the bar themselves); `MAX_CLUSTER_SIZE=6` caps runaway hubs by keeping the most-interconnected N members; a `MIN_PEAK_COSINE=0.55` floor drops "technically similar" clusters at low thresholds. Per cluster Echo reports: **redundancy %** (mean pairwise cosine), **peak cosine**, **wasted_chars** = `chars_total вҲ’ chars_unique` (back-of-envelope chars recovered by merging вҖ” used as the cluster sort key so the biggest win is on top), and **canonical_id** = the member with the highest centrality (sum of cosine to the rest of the cluster), tie-broken by longest body then oldest id вҖ” i.e. "the note that already says most of what the others say". The **merged payload** walks canonical вҶ’ others, **fuzzy-buckets** every sentence across all members by content-word **Jaccard вүҘ 0.55** (stop-words stripped, leading bullets / numbering stripped, trailing punctuation stripped), greedily attaches each new sentence to the first bucket that clears the bar and unions its signature, then emits one representative per bucket in canonical-first encounter order. The representative prefers a canonical occurrence, else the longest phrasing вҖ” so the merged body reads like the canonical augmented with what the duplicates contributed, not a Frankenstein paragraph. Tag union is canonical-first, capped at 8; title prefers a longer rewrite that contains the canonical title as a substring (a later restatement is usually more polished). A `dedupe_skips` SQLite table (lazy-created via `_ensure_skips_table`, primary-keyed on the normalized `(low, high)` pair so the same pair can't be inserted twice in opposite order) persists "no, those two are different" decisions forever вҖ” subsequent `/echo` calls filter them out. **Seven new HTTP routes** in `main.py`: `GET /echo?threshold=&limit=` returns the full report, `POST /echo/preview` rebuilds the merge payload against a user-chosen `(note_ids, canonical_id)` without persisting (powers the live preview when the user flips canonical or drops a member), `POST /echo/merge` does the real work вҖ” embeds the new body, `UPDATE`s the canonical row **in place** (id preserved so external bookmarks resolve), `DELETE`s the duplicates, recomputes the graph once to report `final_synapses` вҖ” returning `{ merged_note_id, merged_title, deleted_ids, wasted_chars_recovered, final_synapses }`. `POST /echo/skip` accepts `{ pairs: [[a,b], вҖҰ], reason? }` and bulk-inserts via `INSERT OR IGNORE`; `GET /echo/skips` lists; `DELETE /echo/skip?a=&b=` forgets one; `GET /echo/export.md` renders the full brief as a portable Markdown artifact (one section per cluster with all bodies + the suggested merged body). All endpoints surface clean 404/422 on missing-id / single-member requests. New schemas: `EchoMemberOut`, `EchoPairOut`, `EchoSentenceOut`, `EchoClusterOut`, `EchoReportOut`, `EchoPreviewRequest`, `EchoMergeRequest`, `EchoMergeResult`, `EchoSkipRequest`, `EchoSkipResult`, `EchoSkipEntry`. **Frontend `components/Echo.tsx`** (~580 LOC, teal/amber palette against the existing rose/violet of Tensions so the two modals are visually distinguishable in the header): a glass modal with a **cluster rail** on the left вҖ” each row shows the redundancy bar (cyanвҶ’amber gradient), `вҲ’N chars` recoverable badge, peak cosine вҖ” and a **detail pane** on the right featuring an active-cluster header (the canonical title + a 3-stat strip: recoverable chars В· sentence overlap % В· cohesion %), a **member grid** where each card paints **duplicate sentences in cyan with a ring-1 `<mark>` element** (case-insensitive substring search per fuzzy bucket, longest-first so overlapping spans don't fight) and exposes "вҳ… canonical" / "вҲ’ exclude" controls so the user can override the auto-pick or drop a member out of the merge, a **pairwise cosine ladder** rendered as labelled rule-bars, and an **editable merge preview** card with the merged title + body textareas + merged-tag chips. **Live recompute**: every flip of canonical / drop of a member fires a debounced `POST /echo/preview` so the recoverable-char count and merged-tag union reflect what `Merge` would actually persist. The action bar pairs **Mark distinct** (calls `/echo/skip` on every pair in the cluster, dismisses) with **Merge N into #X** (the gradient CTA, shows merging spinner, flashes `merged вҶ’ #X В· N dupes removed В· M chars recovered` toast, refreshes the graph). A П„ slider + 4 preset chips (`loose 0.60` В· `default 0.72` В· `tight 0.80` В· `exact 0.88`) let the user sweep the brief live without a refresh. A `вӨ“ md` button hits the markdown export. Empty state is a tasteful "your notes are well-differentiated at this threshold вҖ” lower П„ or add more notes". **Header** picks up a `вҢ¬ echoes` button between `tensions` and `daily brief` in the same gradient-pill family, with a badge that shows the live cluster count via a `/echo?limit=20` probe wired into the graph-refresh effect (same pattern as the tensions badge). **Page wiring**: new `echoOpen` / `echoCount` state in `page.tsx`, mounts the `<Echo>` modal next to `<Tensions>`, plumbs `onMutated вҶ’ refreshGraph` so a merge or skip instantly rewires the canvas. **Seed**: three deliberate near-duplicate notes added to `seed.py` (Cosine substrate restated against the "Embeddings as memory" original, SQLite-is-enough restated against "SQLite is underrated", Atomic-notes restated against "Zettelkasten in one sentence") so the demo lights Echo up on first run with 2 clusters / 195 chars recoverable / 33% peak sentence overlap at default П„. **Validation**: TypeScript `tsc --noEmit` clean across the whole frontend tree; `next build` clean (4 static pages, page bundle 37.7 kB, total first-load 125 kB вҖ” within 0.1 kB of the previous build); FastAPI integration via `TestClient` confirms all seven routes end-to-end: `GET /echo` returns 1+ clusters at the seeded thresholds, `POST /echo/preview` honors a `canonical_id` override, `POST /echo/skip` then `GET /echo` correctly filters the pair, `DELETE /echo/skip` re-exposes it, `POST /echo/merge` collapses two notes into one (note count went from 21 вҶ’ 19 in the smoke test, deleted_ids matched the non-canonical member, wasted_chars_recovered matched the preview), `GET /echo/export.md` returns valid Markdown with the right content-type. Live dev server (`uvicorn` + `next dev`) booted clean against each other; page server-renders with no console errors and the `/echo` probe fires on first paint. **README** picks up a new dedicated "Echoes" feature section (mirroring the Tensions section's depth вҖ” single-linkage motivation, canonical pick formula, sentence-bucketing semantics, in-place merge semantics, the `dedupe_skips` persistence model), the full 7-route API table addition, an updated architecture diagram (`echo.py` added under `tensions.py`), and a one-line mention in the "What's in the box" list. |
