| 58 | 2026-06-19 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-13 entry: shipped **Showdown Arena (`/showdown` tab)** вҖ” the missing *"should I ship this?"* surface every other tab punted on. Arena fans clean prompts to many models, Vote ranks them, Suites batches them across cases, Rubrics judges responses, Optimizer evolves prompts under tidy conditions, Adversary stress-tests how a prompt holds up under perturbation. None of them answer the single question every prompt engineer hits the moment they have a candidate revision: *"is this challenger actually better than the champion currently in production, or am I about to ship noise on a few cherry-picked cases?"*. New `llm_playground_backend/src/showdown.py` (~1100 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `pricing.estimate_cost`) is the engine. **Paired comparison model**: a *showdown* runs the same set of test cases through both prompts (Champion + Challenger) and produces a single per-case О” vector `delta_i = challenger.composite_i вҲ’ champion.composite_i`. **Real statistics** layered on the О” vector: (a) **mean О”** = `ОЈdelta_i / n`; (b) **paired bootstrap 95 % CI** вҖ” `5000` resamples (clipped to `[200, 20000]` via `n_bootstrap` request param), seed is `int(md5(showdown_id)[0:8], 16)` so re-runs are byte-for-byte reproducible, percentile bounds at `floor(0.025В·B)` and `ceil(0.975В·B)вҲ’1`, degenerate single-case CI returns `(value, value)` rather than NaN; (c) **sign-test p-value** вҖ” two-sided exact binomial on the win/loss vector with ties stripped, computed in **log-space** via `math.lgamma` for numerical safety even at `n=25`; (d) **Cohen's d** = `mean_О” / std_О”` (sample std with Bessel correction); (e) **win rate** = `n_wins / n_compared`; (f) **per-dimension О”** вҖ” when a rubric is attached, every rubric dim carries its own mean/worst/best О” aligned by name across the two sides. **Decision rule** (single formula reused across engine + UI + Markdown digest): `ship_challenger` if `mean_О” вүҘ +3.0 AND ci_low > 0 AND win_rate вүҘ 0.55` В· `keep_champion` if `mean_О” вүӨ вҲ’3.0 AND ci_high < 0 AND win_rate вүӨ 0.45` В· `tied` if `|mean_О”| < 1.0 AND ci_low вүӨ 0 вүӨ ci_high AND 0.40 вүӨ win_rate вүӨ 0.60` В· `no_decision` otherwise. **Dry-run scoring** mirrors the Adversary/Optimizer heuristic вҖ” token-overlap-with-expected (Г— 0.55) + length-sanity 80вҖ“800 chars (Г— 0.25) + structural-cue presence (Г— 0.20) вҖ” with a deterministic synthetic response generator that introspects the prompt for signals (few-shot examples, format constraints, step-by-step framing, tone words, constraint words) and emits a response with more scoring cues when the prompt is better engineered, so the challenger consistently wins on prompt quality rather than RNG. Side seed (`"champ"`/`"chall"`) partitions the per-side jitter so identical prompts wouldn't collide on identical text (the API rejects identical prompts anyway). **Live scoring** uses a 2 N task fan-out (both sides Г— every case, max 8 parallel workers via `ThreadPoolExecutor`) вҖ” candidate.make_request + `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` per response; the judge always sees the *original* user input so it rates against the legitimate ask. **Two new SQLite tables** in the shared `history.db` вҖ” `showdowns` (PK id В· champion_prompt В· challenger_prompt В· champion_label В· challenger_label В· rubric_id В· rubric_revision В· judge/candidate provider+model В· test_cases_json В· status В· dryrun В· n_bootstrap В· champion_composite В· challenger_composite В· mean_delta В· std_delta В· ci_low В· ci_high В· p_value_sign В· win_rate В· n_wins/losses/ties В· effect_size В· decision В· total_cost В· duration В· summary_json) + `showdown_runs` (FK showdown_id В· case_idx В· case_input/expected В· champion_response В· challenger_response В· champion_composite В· challenger_composite В· delta В· outcome В· champion_dim_json В· challenger_dim_json В· cost_usd В· latency В· error); 3 indices (updated_at DESC, status, decision); idempotently bootstrapped at import time via `init_db()`. **Seven new endpoints** in `routes/llm.py` (`GET /api/showdown` В· `POST /api/showdown` В· `POST /api/showdown/seed` В· `GET /api/showdown/stats` В· `GET /api/showdown/<id>` В· `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` В· `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run`) вҖ” live mode requires `{confirm_live: true}` to spend money, identical prompts return 400 with `"champion and challenger prompts are identical вҖ” nothing to compare"`. **Frontend** вҖ” new `ShowdownArena.jsx` (~1100 LOC) wired into App.jsx sidebar as a new `selectedMode='showdown'` radio after Adversary (`Swords` glyph + cyanвҶ’fuchsiaвҶ’emerald gradient `new` badge). **Hero** with `Swords` logomark in a 12 px gradient tile (cyan-500 вҶ’ fuchsia-500 вҶ’ emerald-500), "Champion vs Challenger вҖ” should you ship?" headline, 5-tile stats strip (Showdowns / Ship recs / Keep recs / Tied / Avg О”), each tile hue-coded by decision colour. **Two-pane layout**: **left rail** (320 px Card) with search-bar + plus-button + scrollable showdown list вҖ” each row a 52 px `MiniRing` (conic-gradient filled to win-rate% in decision hue), name, decision-tinted short label + signed О” + win-rate-as-% + rel-time, dry-run/live badge + status; **right pane** with two-tab switcher (`Setup` вҶ” `Results`, results tab disabled until `status === 'complete'`, with a small decision chip on the Results tab when present). **Setup tab** (3 sections): (1) header card with name + description + side-by-side **Champion** (amber-tinted) and **Challenger** (cyan-tinted) prompt panels each carrying their own editable label pill (defaults `Champion` / `Challenger` but the user can name them e.g. `v1 (terse)` / `v2 (structured)`); (2) bottom controls row with rubric select (defaults to "No rubric вҖ” heuristic scoring"), bootstrap-iterations numeric input clamped 200вҖ“20000 with a sub-caption explaining the precision/cost tradeoff, and a Mode toggle card with Switch + descriptive caption (Dry-run vs Live); (3) Test cases card with auto-add/remove case grid (input | expected side-by-side), trash button per row. **Results tab**: (1) **Decision hero** вҖ” full-width card with hue-lit gradient + 168 px `DecisionRing` (conic at win-rate%, decision glyph + label + signed О” in the centre; `Trophy`/`Crown`/`Scale`/`HelpCircle` for the four decisions), decision pill chip + dry-run badge + duration/cost eyebrow, headline narrative with `**bold**` вҶ’ `<strong>` and backtick вҶ’ `<code class="text-cyan-300">` parsing, 4-tile metric strip (Champion composite В· Challenger composite В· Win rate В· Cohen's d) hue-rim-lit by appropriate colour, vertical action stack (`Re-run` emerald-cyan gradient В· `Markdown digest` outline В· `Delete` rose-outlined). (2) **Effect-size forest plot** вҖ” centred bipolar `DeltaBar` with the 95 % CI band overlaid as a translucent rectangle (`opacity 0.22 of hue`), zero line, three-cell summary strip below (CI excludes 0? В· Sign test p-value with вң“ < .05 / вң— вүҘ .05 В· cases compared `n_compared/n_cases`). (3) **W/L/T pills** вҖ” emerald `n_wins challenger`, slate `n_ties ties`, amber `n_losses champion`. (4) **Per-dimension impact** вҖ” 2-column grid of rubric dim cards, each a label + weight + signed mean О” chip (hue-coded by `deltaHue(mean*5)`) + centred bipolar `DeltaBar` (absMax 3) + worst/best/n footer. (5) **Per-case results strip** вҖ” sorted ASC by delta (worst regressions first), every row a clickable accordion: `#i`, outcome glyph (`ArrowUp` emerald / `ArrowDown` amber / `Equal` slate) coloured by `deltaHue(delta)`, truncated input preview, champion вҶ’ challenger composite mini-chip pair, signed О” on the right (mono, decision-hue-coded), bipolar `DeltaBar` under the row. Expand reveals champion (amber) vs challenger (cyan) responses side-by-side with per-dim score grids and signed dim deltas in the challenger card, plus the expected-output reference and any per-case error. **Markdown export** вҖ” single click pulls a copyable digest (decision header + result-snapshot table + decision-rule appendix + per-dim table + per-case table) downloaded as `showdown-{id8}.md` for the PR description. **Visual primitives** local to the file: `DecisionRing` (168 px conic + glyph + label + О”), `MiniRing` (52 px), `DeltaBar` (centred bipolar with optional CI band + zero line + signed-label cap), `Tile` (metric card with inset bottom-edge hue rim), `WLTPills` (W/L/T strip), `EmptyState`. Two child panes split out: `SetupPane` and `ResultsPane` with `CaseExpanded` child for the accordion body. **Theme**: cyan-fuchsia-emerald accent throughout (the three decision-confidence-meter colours); `deltaHue` ramps emerald (+8) вҶ’ emerald (+3) вҶ’ lime (+1) вҶ’ slate (~tie) вҶ’ amber (вҲ’3) вҶ’ orange (вҲ’8) вҶ’ rose. **API client**: 7 new methods in `services/api.js` (`listShowdowns`, `createShowdown`, `seedShowdown`, `showdownStats`, `getShowdown`, `deleteShowdown`, `runShowdown`). **Validation**: `python3 -c "import ast"` clean on `showdown.py` and the updated `routes/llm.py`; engine end-to-end smoke вҖ” `seed_demo` returns deterministic id (idempotent on second call), `run_showdown` on the seeded 10-case `v1 (terse)` vs `v2 (structured)` showdown yields `decision='ship_challenger'`, `mean_delta=+3.95`, `ci=[+1.4, +6.2]` (excludes 0), `win_rate=0.80` (8/10), `p_signвүҲ0.039`, Cohen's d `0.94`, `n_wins=8 / n_losses=1 / n_ties=1`, `champion_composite=43.4`, `challenger_composite=47.35`; Flask `test_client` smoke pass on all 7 endpoints (`POST /api/showdown/seed` 201 В· `GET /api/showdown/<id>` 200 В· `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run` 200 ship_challenger В· `GET /api/showdown` 200 total=1 В· `GET /api/showdown/stats` 200 `n_ship_challenger=1` В· `POST /api/showdown` 400 on missing fields + 400 on identical prompts with explicit error message + 400 on live without `confirm_live` В· `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` 200 + subsequent GET 404). `npx vite build` clean: 1733 modules transformed, bundle `index-CqA13br3.js` **778.74 kB В· gzip 210.03 kB** (+40 kB raw / +9 kB gzip vs the pre-Showdown baseline, fully accounted for by the ~1100-LOC component), `index-B2bDzhQO.css` 187.78 kB / gzip 25.04 kB. README rewritten вҖ” opening paragraph extended with the "A/B test prompts head-to-head with Showdown Arena" close, new **"рҹҶ• What's new вҖ” Showdown Arena (Day 58)"** section (~110 lines: paired stats explainer + decision-rule formula block + dry-run vs live + seed demo numbers + visual surface walkthrough + 7-row endpoint table + engine architecture + validation), prior Adversary Lab "рҹҶ•" callout demoted to plain heading. |
| 57 | 2026-06-18 | **Credicrew** | Round-12 move: shipped **Crosswind вҖ” Cross-Role Candidate Router**, the *portfolio-level* layer that every other surface punted on. Up to Day 56, every Credicrew surface is **role-scoped**: Discover ranks the global pool against ONE role's plan, Forecast/Cadence are per-role velocity models, Decision/Offer are per-candidate-within-role. The HQ Command Center rolls them up but doesn't ask the question recruiters running ten reqs actually open Monday with вҖ” *"of all the candidates I've already paid sourcing cost on, are they each in the role that actually fits them best?"*. Crosswind makes that question first-class. New `frontend/src/lib/crosswind.ts` (~430 LOC, pure-TS, **zero new physics** вҖ” Crosswind has no engine of its own; it's a *composer* over the existing `matchCandidate` function from `match.ts` exactly the way Pulse composes WaySafe's engines) takes `(roles, candidates)` and emits a `CrosswindSummary`. **Physics**: for every active candidate (status вү  `passed`/`offer` вҖ” frozen statuses) sitting in some role's shortlist, compute `matchCandidate(role.plan, candidate)` against EVERY open role, producing a candidate Г— role grid of `CrosswindCell { score, matched, missing, isHome, isOnShortlist, locationState, seniorityMatch }`. A candidate's "home" role = the one whose shortlist holds them; if they appear in multiple, the home is whichever has the most recent `stageChangedAt` timestamp (recruiters move people, not history). **Four derived signals**: (1) **Routing moves** вҖ” `home_score < best_alternative_score` by вүҘ `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD=10` pts, sorted descending by delta; each move carries a `why` array deterministically composed from the diff between the home and target `MatchResult` (`+{n} matched skill{s} ({names})` В· `вҲ’{n} ({names})` В· `Location {home_state} вҶ’ {target_state}` В· `Seniority match вҶ’ mismatch / mismatch вҶ’ match`), with status preserved so the move card carries the candidate's current stage pill. (2) **Talent magnets** вҖ” score вүҘ `STRONG_FLOOR=80` in вүҘ `MAGNET_ROLES=3` distinct roles, ranked by hit count then top score; these are scarce portfolio-level assets (losing them costs N reqs not 1). (3) **Lonely roles** вҖ” own best match < 80 *and* a transplant exists вүҘ `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR=70` *and* the move doesn't hurt the candidate's home fit by more than 5 pts (don't poach down вҖ” that's what the Cadence Studio already polices on the velocity axis). (4) **Portfolio lift** вҖ” `ОЈ(best_alt_score вҲ’ current_score)` over all active candidates, with `lift_avg_per_move = lift_total / move_count`. Plus a per-role rollup with `(best, median, candidateCount, isTarget, isSource, crowdedRank)` and a 10-bucket score histogram across every (candidate Г— role) cell. **Band ladder**: `idle` if no moves, `urgent` if `lift вүҘ 60` or `вүҘ 5` moves, `meaningful` if `lift вүҘ 25` or `вүҘ 3` moves, `modest` otherwise вҖ” colour-coded slate/sky/violet/rose for the hero ring. **Surface** вҖ” dark glass page at `/crosswind`, sitting between Cadence and Pipeline in the nav. (a) **Hero** with a 168 px conic-gradient `Portfolio lift` ring (lift normalised to a notional `25 Г— candidate_count` max, band-tinted) flanked by two columns of metric tiles (Active candidates В· Open roles В· Routing moves В· Avg lift/move В· Talent magnets В· Lonely roles). (b) **Recommendations strip** вҖ” violet-tinted callout with a band-keyed first line (urgent / meaningful / modest copy that names the top move's candidate, from/to roles, and delta) plus a magnets line and a lonely-roles line, all rendered through a tiny `**bold**` parser so the numerics pop. (c) **Match matrix** вҖ” the centerpiece. Rows = active candidates (sorted by best-fit score desc), cols = open roles (sorted by `perRole` order, with target roles in emerald-300 header and source roles in rose-300 header, plus the role's own `best N` muted below the name). Cells are colour-tiered (`emerald вүҘ80 В· sky вүҘ70 В· amber вүҘ55 В· rose вүҘ35 В· slate <35`) with `alpha = 0.08 + score/100 Г— 0.6` so the cell intensity tracks score even within a tier; the **home cell** gets a white-40 ring, and any off-home cell scoring `+MISPLACE_THRESHOLD` or more over home gets a tiny emerald `вҶ‘` chip in the upper-right corner so the eye lands on routing opportunities immediately. Every cell is a button вҖ” click adds the candidate to that role's shortlist as `new` (calls `addToShortlist` from the existing roles lib, persists to localStorage, and re-runs the engine in the same render pass so the matrix re-tiers live). Sticky-left candidate column with avatar + name + home-role tag stays anchored when the matrix scrolls horizontally. (d) **Recommended moves** card with avatar + name + stage pill + from-role(score, rose) вҶ’ to-role(score, emerald) вҶ’ delta pill + multi-line `why` diff + Route button (toggles to "вң“ Routed" once applied). Top-4 by default, "Show all N" toggle. (e) **Routing flow** Sankey вҖ” left nodes are source roles (rose with `вҲ’N` count badges), right nodes are target roles (emerald with `+N`), bezier paths between them with `strokeWidth = max(1.5, delta/6)` so the eye reads "biggest single-move = thickest edge"; one glance tells you whether the portfolio is converging (1 target, many sources) or diverging. (f) **Talent magnets** panel вҖ” per-candidate card with score-tinted avatar + home tag + role-hit chips (вҳ…-marked when the chip IS the home, emerald otherwise). (g) **Lonely roles** panel вҖ” per-role card with own best/median/count + top-3 transplant rows (avatar + name + from-role + score in emerald + delta vs home) and an "Open вҶ’" link to the role page. (h) **Score histogram** across all (candidate Г— role) cells, 10-pt buckets, each bar tiered to its bucket's hue so the distribution is instantly legible. (i) **How Crosswind reasons** explainer footer with formal definitions of move / magnet / lonely / lift / frozen-statuses. Plus Copy brief / Download .md buttons that emit a markdown brief identical to the one the backend's `build_brief()` produces. **Backend mirror** вҖ” `backend/app/services/crosswind.py` (~340 LOC) is the byte-for-byte Python port using the existing `app.services.match.match_candidate` (same `WEIGHTS = {skill: 0.55, loc: 0.15, sen: 0.20, base: 0.10}` so client and server always agree). Same `STRONG_FLOOR`, `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD`, `MAGNET_ROLES`, `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR` constants. Same `_diff_why` builder. Same frozen-status filter. `backend/app/routers/crosswind.py` exposes `POST /crosswind/summary` (accepts both camelCase and snake_case via Pydantic aliases with `populate_by_name=True`, optional `includeBrief: true` to embed the markdown inline), `POST /crosswind/brief` (re-render from a cached summary dict), `GET /crosswind/defaults` (thresholds + frozen-statuses + formulas + match weights so a CLI client can render a what-if without hard-coding numbers). API version bumped `0.12.0 вҶ’ 0.13.0` in `main.py`. **Validation**: a 5-candidate Г— 3-role fixture run through the Python engine produces `current_total=390, optimal_total=500, lift=110`, two routing moves (Rohan Sharma: Frontend(45)вҶ’Backend(100) +55 because his bag contains fastapi/postgres/python; Sneha Patel: Backend(45)вҶ’Frontend(100) +55 because her bag contains react/next.js/tailwind), each move's `why` line correctly names the three skills gained, no magnets and no lonely roles (every role has a strong own match because of candidates 1/2/3), `band=urgent` (lift вүҘ 60), markdown brief renders end-to-end. **Frontend validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean across the whole `src/`; `npx next build` clean вҖ” `/crosswind` route emitted at 10.2 kB (smaller than `/cadence` at 9.65 kB despite carrying the matrix because the heatmap is pure CSS, no chart lib). **Navigation**: `Navbar.tsx` gets a `Crosswind` link inserted between Cadence and Pipeline. **CSS**: new `.cc-xw-hero`, `.cc-xw-ring`, `.cc-xw-tile`, `.cc-xw-matrix`, `.cc-xw-cell` (with `transform: scale(1.08)` + `box-shadow: inset white-18` on hover so the cell pops without breaking row alignment), and `.cc-xw-move` micro-animations added to `globals.css`. **README rewritten** вҖ” new "What's new вҖ” Crosswind (Day 57)" section at the top with the four signals, the surface walkthrough, the backend curl example, and the version bump callout. |
| 56 | 2026-06-17 | **WaySafe** | Round-12 move: shipped **Pulse вҖ” Today's Outlook**, the *morning-brief* composer that finally adds the **temporal-delta lens** WaySafe was missing. Every prior surface up to Day 55 is *forward-looking* (Compass picks where to go, StaySafe where to sleep, Plan Route how to get there, Tempo when to leave, Refuge where to flee, Sentinel which clusters are heating) вҖ” none of them answer the question a traveller actually asks the moment they wake up: *"what's different about my day vs 24 hours ago, and what should I do about it before lunch?"*. New `WaySafe/pulse.py` (~560 LOC, pure-stdlib, **zero new physics** вҖ” Pulse is the first WaySafe surface that has *no engine of its own*; it's a composer) is a pure function of `(watched, incidents, geofences, pois, forecaster, now, clusters?)` that treats the user's day as a small portfolio of **watched points** (typically the stay + 1вҖ“3 planned destinations) and re-runs every existing engine for each point *twice* вҖ” at `now` *and* at `now вҲ’ 24 h`. **Per-point pipeline**: (1) `safety.compute_safety(now, all_incidents)` and `safety.compute_safety(nowвҲ’24h, incidents_with_created_at вүӨ cutoff)` for a clean *signed* О”score + band-shift flag (the cutoff filter is the one trick вҖ” drop incidents created after `nowвҲ’24h` to get the world as it was, instead of double-counting today's news against yesterday's penalty); (2) `forecast.HazardForecaster.risk_curve` for **today's** DOW *and* **yesterday's** DOW so the per-point hour-ribbon also carries a day-over-day diff; (3) `sentinel.cluster_incidents` вҖ” clusters are computed once globally (reused from the Map / Sentinel tab via the new `clusters=вҖҰ` keyword so the two surfaces never disagree), each watched point picks up the clusters whose **halo edge** sits within **`CLUSTER_INTERSECT_KM=1.5`** km, escalating-first; (4) `refuge.find_refuge(max_results=1)` so the stay's refuge-readiness band rides on every report (caught in a try/except вҖ” refuge is context, never breaks the brief). **Per-point window math**: `best_window = argmin_h mean(curve_today[h:h+3])`, `worst_window = argmax_h ...` over a wrap-around 24-h ring (so `(22, 1)` is a valid 3-h window crossing midnight); also computed across all watched points as the **joint curve** `joint(h) = max_p curve_p(h)`. **Mood ladder** вҖ” first match wins: `Critical` if any watched point Danger or any intersecting cluster Critical; `Active` if any High Risk, any cluster Emerging, or вүҘ 2 watched points slipped вүҘ 10 pts; `Watch` if any Caution or any single point dropped вүҘ 5 pts; else `Calm`. **Biggest mover** is the snapshot with the largest *signal* score = `|О”score|В·1.0  +  new_incidents_24hВ·4.0  +  ОЈ_escalating-clusters(6 + 2В·(velocityвҲ’1))  +  6В·band_changed  +  4В·(refuge_band вҲҲ {High Risk, Danger})` вҖ” so a watched point that didn't shift in score but is touching a Critical cluster still surfaces. **Plain-English change log** deterministically composed from each snapshot's deltas (`"{label}: safety down **{О”} pts** overnight ({s24}вҶ’{s})"` В· `"{label}: band shifted **{old} вҶ’ {new}**"` В· `"{label}: **{n} new incidents** within 1 km in the last 24 h (mostly accident)"` В· `"{label}: **Cluster #X В· Accident** is Critical (Г—43.9) вҖ” edge 0.00 km"`), ranked by `signal + 0.01В·len(line)` so the biggest-mover's lines float to the top, capped at 8 bullets. **Plan-of-day** is the action layer вҖ” prioritised checklist that *references other WaySafe tabs by name when those are the right follow-ups*: a Critical cluster intersection produces *"Re-plan any leg through {cluster} вҖ” pick a corridor вүҘ 1.5 km away and prefer the **Tempo** winner over a now-departure"*; an Emerging cluster produces a wide-berth bullet; the best/worst outdoor windows produce front-load / avoid bullets quoting the joint risk number; a slipped biggest-mover produces a re-check bullet; a fresh-incident spike (вүҘ 3 in 24 h) produces a *"Skim the **Map** tab around {label}"* bullet; a stay whose refuge band вүҘ High Risk produces *"Memorise the nearest non-stay refuge before evening"*. Falls back to *"Day looks clean вҖ” no special precautions beyond the usual"* on a calm morning, so the brief is never spammy. **Serialisation**: `to_dict() вҶ’ waysafe.pulse.v1` JSON envelope (mood В· headline В· advisory_line В· joint_curve В· best_outdoor_window В· worst_outdoor_window В· biggest_mover В· per-snapshot block with hour curves today + yesterday + best/worst windows + refuge + changes В· de-duped sentinel intersections В· change_log В· actions); markdown digest is WhatsApp/email-shaped (headline > advisory line > best/avoid window > watched-points table > sentinel intersections > what-changed-since-yesterday > plan-of-day numbered list). **Frontend** вҖ” new `Pulse` tab inserted at `tabs[0]` (so it's what the user opens first), every other tab index bumped +1 in a single deterministic pass (`Map 0вҶ’1 В· Plan Route 1вҶ’2 В· вҖҰ  В· Trip Log 14вҶ’15`); `render_pulse` + `render_pulse_empty` added to `theme.py` (~470 LOC of `.ws-pulse-*` CSS + Python) вҖ” the render stack: (1) **hero card** with a 140 px conic-gradient `Pulse` ring (mean watched-point score as the fill %, mood-tinted hue, central mood eyebrow + score + band) + radial-gradient glow tinted by mood + headline + advisory + biggest-mover side card (delta-arrow + delta-pts + band arrow `{old} вҶ’ {new}` in band hue); (2) **four-tile strip** (overall band В· best 3-h window with joint risk В· total new incidents within 1 km in last 24 h with hue ramp В· refuge readiness at the stay with nearest POI + distance); (3) **24-hour joint risk ribbon** вҖ” one row of 24 cells with height + colour driven by `joint_curve(h)` (green вҶ’ amber вҶ’ orange вҶ’ rose at 0.20 / 0.40 / 0.66 risk thresholds), **best window outlined in green with glow shadow**, **worst window outlined in red**, **blue vertical now-line** marking the current hour, past hours dimmed to 35% opacity, hour labels below colour-coded by membership in best/worst windows; (4) **per-watched-point card** вҖ” 78 px score ring + kind eyebrow + glyphed title + band-tinted band chip + О”-chip (`в–ј вҲ’21 pts vs 24h ago` rose / `вҶ’ Вұ0` slate / `в–І +8 pts` emerald) + cluster pings (escalating ones rose-tinted) + band-shift chip + plain-English changes block + compact today-curve mini-ribbon + side panel with per-point best window and nearest refuge; (5) **Sentinel intersections** strip with status-coloured dot per cluster + escalating chip; (6) ranked **what-changed-since-yesterday** numbered list; (7) prioritised **plan-of-day** numbered list вҖ” both lists use a custom `data-i` CSS counter so they self-number even when partially filtered; (8) JSON + markdown export buttons. **App wiring**: a `Watched points` `data_editor` expander lets the user customise the roster (kind selectbox, label, lat/lon вҖ” NaN-guarded, defaults seeded from the user's `current_loc` as the stay + up to two nearest non-help POIs as destinations within 5 km), a primary `Compose Pulse` button that pulls in the cached `sent_clusters` from the existing Sentinel computation (so re-clustering is free), a `pulse_day` session-state slot that holds the result until re-composed, and graceful empty-state via `render_pulse_empty()`. **README rewritten** вҖ” new headline-feature bullet under the existing Tempo bullet describing every engine Pulse re-runs and what the surface looks like; new dedicated **"рҹ’“ Pulse вҖ” Today's Outlook (Day 56)"** section between StaySafe and Tempo with the "what gets re-run per watched point" table (engine В· what Pulse asks it twice В· new signal), the day-level summary equations (`joint_curve` В· `best_outdoor_window` В· `worst_outdoor_window` В· `overall_band` В· `overall_mood`), the explicit first-match-wins mood rules, the biggest-mover signal formula spelled out, an "what you see" surface walkthrough (hero В· four-tile strip В· joint ribbon В· per-point card В· Sentinel list В· what-changed list В· plan-of-day В· exports), and a closing "why this matters" passage tying it back to the rotation's central thesis ("a planner suite that only ever computes 'what is' leaves the traveller to track 'what changed' in their head вҖ” Pulse closes that loop"). **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; | 59 | 2026-06-20 | **SynapseOS** | Round-12 entry: shipped **Pulse вҖ” what changed in your second brain this week**, the cross-cluster, time-windowed diff every prior surface had left to the user. SynapseOS already had three "lens" surfaces but each looks at one slice вҖ” **Atlas** is the snapshot of *where every cluster sits right now* (cohesion Г— activity quadrant), **Chronicle** is the biography of *one* cluster (equal-time chapters + drift + pivot), **Daily Brief** is *today's* revisit picks. None of them ask the question a writer asks on a Friday afternoon: *"across my whole second brain, in the last N days, what got written, where did it land, what synapses formed, which clusters caught fire, what vocabulary appeared and what fell away?"*. New `backend/app/pulse.py` (~700 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `embed.cosine`) is a single deterministic function `compute_pulse(window_days, threshold, top_k) вҶ’ PulseReport`. **Per-cluster pulse** (mirrors `community.name_communities` for tokenizer alignment): for every cluster compute `new_count` (members with `created_at >= window_start`), `revisits_count` (members with `last_seen_at >= window_start` AND `created_at < window_start` so the two buckets are mutually exclusive), `share_new = new/size`, **centroid drift** = `1 вҲ’ cosine(centroid(prior_members), centroid(new_members))` *only* when both epochs have вүҘ 2 members (so a newborn cluster doesn't print a misleading 0), a **momentum** soft blend (`0.55В·share_new + 0.25В·(revisits/size) + 0.20В·density_proxy`), and a status badge вҖ” first-match-wins ladder: `new_count == size вҶ’ born` В· `share_new вүҘ 0.5 AND new_count вүҘ 2 вҶ’ emerging` В· `new_count вүҘ 3 вҶ’ hot` В· `new_count вүҘ 1 OR revisits вүҘ 1 вҶ’ warm` В· else `dormant`. Plus per-cluster **new vocabulary** (a chronicle-style `_delta_terms` with the same 0.5 forgiveness factor scoring in-window member tokens against the rest of the cluster вҖ” title Г— 3, tags Г— 2, body Г— 1) and the actual **hot titles** of the new notes ordered by `created_at desc`. **Library-wide signals**: (a) **bridges born** вҖ” current synapses where `cmap[u] != cmap[v]` *and* at least one endpoint is a new note, sorted by strength desc and capped at 16, with a `NEW` chip per new-side; (b) **hubs born** вҖ” new notes already pulling `degree вүҘ HUB_MIN_DEGREE=3` at the current graph parameters (instant centrality is rare and worth surfacing); (c) library-wide **vocab delta** (emerged vs faded) over the prior-vs-new TF tables with `VOCAB_MIN_COUNT=2` floor so single-mention typos don't slip in; (d) **daily activity** вҖ” per-day bins of created vs revisited across the window for a sparkline, oldest-first so the UI draws left-to-right time; (e) **streak** вҖ” longest run of consecutive days ending today (UTC) with вүҘ 1 note created, computed across *all* notes (extends beyond the requested window so a 60-day streak still shows in a 7-day pulse); (f) **words written** вҖ” `chars / 5` heuristic summed over new-note bodies (the standard word-proxy that doesn't trip on punctuation). **Recommendations**: priority-banded so the top-5 view shows a healthy mix (`synthesize 0.70+` *catch the hot topic before it scatters* В· `name 0.60` *the cluster doesn't have a meaningful label yet* В· `hub 0.50` *a new note grew structural importance fast вҖ” re-read while context is fresh* В· `bridge 0.40` *write a connector note for the freshest cross-cluster synapse* В· `revisit 0.20` *dormant cluster nudge*) вҖ” sorted priority desc with alpha tie-break so the panel doesn't jitter, capped at 14. **Headline** вҖ” one-liner narrative composed first-match-wins from the dominant shape (`No new notes` В· `Quiet writing week` В· the prose form with new/words/revisits/hot/bridges/hubs/streak). `serialize()` returns a plain-dict response; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-anywhere brief (headline + metrics table + vocab delta + active clusters + bridges + hubs + recommendations). Two new schemas (`PulseReportOut` + 5 child models) and two new routes in `main.py`: `GET /pulse?window_days=1\|7\|30\|90` (clamped 1..365 with 422 on out-of-range), `GET /pulse/export.md`. **Frontend** вҖ” new `frontend/src/components/Pulse.tsx` (~830 LOC) wired into `page.tsx` as `pulseOpen` modal sibling of Atlas/Chronicle, opens via a new header pill (`в©ҳ pulse` with a pinkвҶ’limeвҶ’cyan gradient ring) carrying a live badge of `new_notes + bridges_born` over the last 7d. **Visual identity**: distinct pink+lime ECG glyph (an actual heartbeat polyline in a gradient tile вҖ” `0,8 вҶ’ 6,8 вҶ’ 9,3 вҶ’ 12,13 вҶ’ 15,5 вҶ’ 18,11 вҶ’ 21,8 вҶ’ 32,8` for a clean PQRST shape) so it doesn't get mistaken for Atlas/Chronicle. **Layout**: dark glass dialog identical to Atlas вҖ” title strip with pinkвҶ’limeвҶ’cyan linear-gradient header band, window-picker pills (`1d / 7d / 30d / 90d`), вӨ“ md export, вң• close, headline echoed inline. Body sections: (1) **6-tile metrics strip** (new notes В· revisits В· bridges В· hubs В· streak В· hotВ·forming with dormant sub-label), each tile hue-rim-lit by signal colour (lime/amber/pink/violet/cyan/white). (2) **Daily activity sparkline** вҖ” a single SVG with two stacked area layers (`pulse-fill` lime gradient for created, `pulse-fill-rev` amber gradient for created+revisited stacked on top), a baseline + dashed midline, peak dots on every active day, deterministic month-day x-axis labels at first/mid/last via a hand-rolled `dayLabel`, max-value label at the y-axis top, viewBox stretched to width. (3) **Vocabulary delta** вҖ” two-column emerged (lime chips, "frequent now В· rare before") vs faded (slate chips, "frequent before В· rare now") with empty-state copy when no shift. (4) **Active clusters** (lg:7 col) вҖ” one `ClusterRow` per cluster: status pill with coloured dot (hot/lime В· born/pink В· emerging/cyan В· warm/amber В· dormant/slate), `вңҰ synth` + `вҠҷ isolate` action chips, **momentum bar** (1.5 px high, cluster-colour fill, percentage-tagged), pill row (`size`, `+N new` lime, `вҶ» R` amber, `S% new`, `drift X.XX` pink when populated, `quiet Nd` for fully-dormant), **new vocab chips** + **hot titles list** (first 3) with a left-side cluster-colour dot bullet. (5) **Recommendations** (lg:5 col) вҖ” priority-ranked card list with a kind glyph (`вңҰ synthesize` lime В· `вҢҒ name` cyan В· `вңә hub` violet В· `вҮ„ bridge` pink В· `вҳј revisit` amber), headline, detail, `p 0.XX` chip, clickable to act (synthesize/name вҶ’ opens Synthesis modal В· revisit/bridge вҶ’ isolates cluster on canvas В· hub вҶ’ opens note in Inspector). (6) **Hubs born** вҖ” grid of violet-ringed cards with `вңә` glyph, title, `Nx` degree pill, snippet, cluster name + dot + age in days. (7) **Bridges born** вҖ” list of pink-tinted rows: source-cluster chip вҮ„ target-cluster chip В· cosine, then source-title вҶ” target-title with `NEW` lime chips on whichever side is in-window; click opens the note. **Status colors** picked to be distinct from Atlas's quadrant palette (Pulse uses pink for born/bridges, lime for emerged/hot, cyan for emerging вҖ” Atlas uses lime/cyan/violet/slate by quadrant вҖ” so the two surfaces don't visually clash when stacked open). Type-clean `PulseReport` / `PulseCluster` / `PulseBridge` / `PulseHub` / `PulseRecommendation` types + 2 new API methods (`api.pulse({ windowDays })`, `api.pulseExportUrl({ windowDays })`). **Validation**: full backend round-trip via FastAPI `TestClient` вҖ” `GET /pulse` 200 across 1d/7d/30d/90d windows on the seeded 21-note graph, headline correctly switches from `"No new notes in the last 1d. | 60 | 2026-06-21 | **Titan** | Round-13 move: shipped **Pulse вҖ” the compliance officer's morning brief**, the *temporal-delta* lens every prior TITAN surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day 55 every TITAN engine measures *right now*: `risk` & `typology` score one batch, `profile` composites a customer's surfaces into one number, `cases` queues alerts, `network` propagates across counterparties, `peer` scores cohort outliers, `drift` catches *account-vs-self* change. None of them ask the question an MLRO opens Monday with вҖ” *"across my whole customer book, what's different since yesterday, and what should I look at FIRST before lunch?"*. New `apps/ai-aml/pulse.py` (~700 LOC, pure-stdlib, **zero new physics** вҖ” Pulse is a *composer* вҖ” same shape as WaySafe Day-56 Pulse and SynapseOS Day-59 Pulse) is a single deterministic function `compute_pulse(profiles, cases_index, all_cases, window_days, now) вҶ’ PulseReport`. **Per-customer pulse**: for every profile read the most recent `profile_history` row whose `refreshed_at < window_start` (the prior snapshot lives in the data model already вҖ” no separate cache), compute signed `composite_delta`, derive `band_shift_direction` (`up`/`down`/`""`) when buckets differ across the window, and tally the customer's owned-account cases via a flat `accounts_by_customer` reverse index вҖ” `open_case_count`, `new_case_count` (`opened_at >= window_start`), `new_case_critical`, `new_case_high`, `open_breach_count` (`status NOT IN cleared|sar_filed AND sla == 'breach'`). Per-customer **signal** = `abs(О”)В·1 + bucket_upgradedВ·8 + new_case_criticalВ·6 + new_case_highВ·4 + open_breachВ·5 + refresh_overdueВ·3 + critical_floorВ·4` вҖ” sorted desc with a `signal вүҘ 1` floor so trivially-recomputed customers don't flood the panel. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins across the entire portfolio): `critical` if any customer crossed INTO `critical` OR any case SLA == breach OR any composite вүҘ 90 В· `active` if any band-shift up OR new_cases вүҘ 3 OR вүҘ 2 customers up by вүҘ 10 pts В· `watch` if any composite up by вүҘ 5 OR any new high/critical case OR any KYC overdue В· `calm` otherwise. **Headline** вҖ” one-liner narrative composed first-match-wins from the dominant shape (`"Critical morning В· {biggest_mover} В· escalated to critical"`); **advisory** rolls up `"N new case(s) В· M SLA breach(es) В· K customer(s) moving"`. **Change-log** ranks per-customer change-lines by `(signal + line_kind_bonus)` вҖ” bucket-shift lines get +6, generic delta lines +1.5 вҖ” then deduplicates by `display_name` Г— kind, capped at 10. **Plan-of-day** is the action layer вҖ” *names the TITAN tab each action lives in* so the brief stays operational: (1) **breach triage** вҖ” top-3 customers by `(вҲ’breach_count, вҲ’signal)` вҶ’ "Triage **N breach case(s)** for **X** in the **Cases** tab"; (2) **critical escalations** вҖ” top-3 customers crossing INTO `critical` вҶ’ "Escalate **X** вҖ” crossed into critical (from `medium`). Freeze new-product onboarding pending MLRO review."; (3) **fresh case review** вҖ” top-3 unique customers with new critical/high cases not already covered above вҶ’ "Review **N fresh case(s)** for **X** in the **Cases** tab"; (4) **KYC overdue** вҖ” top-2 by `(days_overdue, вҲ’signal)` вҶ’ "Re-anchor **X** in the **Profile** tab вҖ” KYC overdue by 148d"; (5) **composite movers** вҖ” one rollup line naming up to 3 movers вҶ’ "Open the **Profile** tab for **A, B, C** вҖ” composite shifted by вүҘ 5 pts in the window"; fallback `"Portfolio quiet вҖ” skim the Profile tab for any due-soon KYC refreshes and call it a clean morning"` on a calm morning. Each `PulseAction` carries `kind В· priority В· body В· customer_id В· href` so the surface can deep-link straight into `/profile?customer_id=вҖҰ` or `/cases?account_id=вҖҰ`. **Daily activity sparkline** вҖ” per-day case-open counts across the window, oldest-first, with a separate breach overlay (SLA-breach interpretation as "incurred on the opening day" вҖ” same calendar-day bucketing as the existing case-stats panel). **Score histogram** вҖ” 10-bucket distribution across composites, tiered to the bucket palette. `to_dict() вҶ’ titan.pulse.v1` JSON envelope; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able brief (headline В· advisory В· vital-signs table В· bucket distribution before/after В· biggest movers list В· change-log В· plan-of-day, ~2.5 KB) for Slack / email. Four new routes in `main.py`: `GET /aml/pulse/rules` (window bounds, signal weights, mood ladder, signal formula coefficients вҖ” auditor-facing); `GET /aml/pulse/sample?window_days=1..30` (rich demo built from the bundled 12-customer CRP book + a deterministic synthetic "yesterday" snapshot вҖ” high-risk customers in the fixture back off by 18+ pts so the demo always lights up with realistic movement); `GET /aml/pulse` (LIVE composer over persisted profiles + cases вҖ” falls back to sample when the store is empty so the surface never renders a depressing "no data" state, payload carries `source: live|sample`); `GET /aml/pulse/export.md?source=auto|live|sample` (markdown brief, `text/markdown; charset=utf-8`). Mirror pass-throughs added to the gateway in `apps/api/main.py` so the frontend has one origin. | 61 | 2026-06-22 | **WaySafe** | Round-13 entry: shipped **Beacon вҖ” Group Safety Coordinator**, the first WaySafe surface that thinks in terms of a *group* instead of a single point. Every prior surface вҖ” Compass, StaySafe, Plan Route, Refuge, Sentinel, Tempo, Pulse вҖ” scores one location at a time; the moment two or more people are on the same trip, the question is no longer "am I safe?" but "are *we* safe, and what do *we* do together about it?". New `WaySafe/beacon.py` (~580 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `safety.compute_safety` and `safety.point_risk` вҖ” **zero new physics**, same composer family as Pulse Day 56 / SynapseOS Pulse Day 59 / TITAN Pulse Day 60) is a single deterministic function `compute_beacon(members, incidents, geofences, pois, now) вҶ’ BeaconReport`. **Per-member**: score each via the existing `compute_safety` (band, nearest help, incidents nearby, factors), plus a per-member **isolation** (min pairwise distance to any other member вҖ” a "loneliness" proxy). **Group composite** = `0.50В·min_score + 0.30В·kind-weighted_mean + 0.20В·spread_score` where `spread_score = 100В·(1 вҲ’ spread_penalty)`, `spread_penalty` falls linearly from 0.0 at вүӨ 0.8 km max-pairwise-distance to 1.0 at вүҘ 3.8 km вҖ” so a splintered group reads as *less coordinated* even if every member's individual score is fine; `KIND_WEIGHT` upweights `minor` (1.25), `elder` (1.20), downweights `guide` (0.90). **Meet-point candidates** from four sources: (1) the geometric **centroid** of all members, (2) **top-5 help POIs** within 4 km of centroid ranked by raw `compute_safety` score (so we don't waste a slot on a gated hospital next to a midnight roadblock), (3) **top-3 safe pockets** from a 5Г—5 grid sample centered on centroid (catches the off-beat safe corners that aren't near any institutional refuge), (4) **stable-member** fallback вҖ” a member already in a Safe band becomes a candidate (`"Stay with X"`), sometimes the best move is to *not* make everyone walk. Each candidate is evaluated by sampling **5 waypoints** from every member's position to the candidate, pricing each waypoint by `safety.point_risk`, then composing: `score = 100В·(0.40В·safety_at_point/100 + 0.25В·(1 вҲ’ max_path_risk) + 0.20В·(1 вҲ’ min(1, max_walk/4 km)) + 0.15В·(1 вҲ’ min(1, sum_walk/(4 kmВ·n))))` вҖ” the chain is only as strong as its riskiest member-walk, and the slowest member dominates a real-world rendezvous, so both make the blend. Also tracks `geofence_crossings` per member-arrival via point-in-polygon over the same 5 waypoints, fed into the alerts panel. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins): `Critical` if any member Danger or group_score < 35 or chosen worst corridor вүҘ 0.65 В· `Active` if any High Risk or group_score < 60 or spread > 2.5 km В· `Watch` if any Caution or group_score < 80 or spread > 1.2 km В· else `Calm`. **Biggest concern** = member maximising `band_weight + max(0, isolation вҲ’ 2.5)В·10 + max(0, 70 вҲ’ score)В·0.4 + 8В·(kind вҲҲ {minor, elder})`. **Rendezvous corridors** for the chosen meet-point sample **8 waypoints** per member (matching the great-circle line to within ~1 m at Goa-scale вүӨ 4 km), price each by `point_risk`, and emit `Corridor` with `mean_risk`, `peak_risk`, `distance_km`, and ETA at a `4.5 km/h` walking pace вҖ” `peak_risk вүҘ 0.55` flips the `risky` flag which feeds the alerts and paints the map `PathLayer` rose. **Alerts** ranked: per-member High Risk / Danger pull-lines first, then isolation lines (> 2.5 km from any other member), then corridor-risk lines, then geofence-crossing lines, then a group-spread fragmentation line (> 3.2 km), de-duped while preserving order. **Plan-of-action** is the action layer вҖ” prioritised checklist that *references other WaySafe tabs by name*: anchor action ("Converge at *{chosen.label}* вҖ” ETA {slowest} min for the slowest member ({name})"), lead-member departs-first line, per-Danger-member pull line, "Open the **Refuge** tab on the meet-point", "Enable **Live Trip** geofence pings on every member while corridors are in motion", "If a split happens en route, fall back to *{secondary.label}*", "Re-Beacon every **15 min**". **Serialisation**: `to_dict() вҶ’ waysafe.beacon.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at В· mood В· headline В· advisory_line В· group{score,band,spread_km,size,biggest_concern_id} В· members[] В· candidates[] В· chosen В· secondary В· corridors[] В· alerts В· plan_of_action); `to_json()`; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-anywhere brief (headline В· advisory В· vital-signs table В· members table В· alerts list В· candidates table В· plan-of-action numbered list, ~2.2 KB) for the squad chat. **Frontend** вҖ” new `Beacon` tab inserted at `tabs[1]` (right after Pulse вҖ” both are *composer* surfaces, Pulse asks "what changed?" and Beacon asks "where do we meet?"), every other tab index bumped +1 in a single deterministic pass (`Map 1вҶ’2 В· Plan Route 2вҶ’3 В· Itinerary 3вҶ’4 В· Live Trip 4вҶ’5 В· Forecast 5вҶ’6 В· Advisory 6вҶ’7 В· Compass 7вҶ’8 В· StaySafe 8вҶ’9 В· Sentinel 9вҶ’10 В· Refuge 10вҶ’11 В· Tempo 11вҶ’12 В· Report Hazard 12вҶ’13 В· Alerts 13вҶ’14 В· SOS 14вҶ’15 В· Trip Log 15вҶ’16`). `theme.py` gains a ~310-line `render_beacon` + `render_beacon_empty` block: (1) **hero card** with a 152 px conic-gradient ring (mood-tinted hue, breathing 4.6 s animation), mood eyebrow + group score + group band, headline + advisory + biggest-concern side card (member glyph + band pill + isolation/nearest-help sub); (2) **four-tile vital-signs strip** (group band hue-tinted В· group spread km hue-ramped at 0.5/1.2/2.5 km thresholds В· mood with alert/candidate count В· meet-at label with slowest ETA + max walk); (3) **per-member cards** in a responsive grid вҖ” 70 px ring + kind glyph + label + isolation chip + nearest-help chip (hue-ramped at 1.0/2.5 km) + corridor distance/ETA/risk chips (hue-ramped at 0.35/0.55 peak risk) + band chip; (4) **meet-point candidates table** вҖ” ranked 1вҖ“6 with chosen pick highlighted green (`rgba(83,227,166,0.06)` background + 2 px lime left rail) and secondary highlighted amber, each row carries source pill (help_poi=blue В· centroid=violet В· safe_pocket=lime В· stable_member=amber), composite score, safety at point, max walk, sum walk, worst corridor risk (rose-tinted at вүҘ 0.55); (5) **group map** (`pydeck`) вҖ” members as band-coloured `ScatterplotLayer` (radius 90, white outline 2 px), chosen meet-point as gold star `ScatterplotLayer` (radius 160, white outline 3 px), corridors as `PathLayer` painted blue / amber / rose by peak risk; (6) **alerts** as severity-banded cards (rose for Danger/High Risk lines, amber for isolation/geofence, yellow for corridor, blue informational) with mini `**bold**` markdown parser; (7) **plan-of-action** as a CSS-counter-numbered list with sky-blue index circles. **App wiring**: `data_editor` expander for the 3-default-member roster (kind selectbox: lead/traveller/minor/elder/guide, label, lat/lon вҖ” NaN-guarded, defaults seeded from `current_loc` + two perturbations so the demo always has a meaningful group), primary `Compose Beacon` button, `beacon_report` session-state slot, `Snap all to me` utility button for when the group has just regrouped, JSON + markdown download buttons. **Validation**: pure `ast.parse` clean on `beacon.py`, `theme.py`, `app.py`; | 62 | 2026-06-23 | **Credicrew** | Round-13 move: shipped **Revive вҖ” Silver Medalist Reactivation Engine** (`/revive`), the first Credicrew surface that works the *dormant* pool instead of the *active* one. Every other cross-cutting surface вҖ” Crosswind (Day 57), Cadence, HQ, Pipeline вҖ” explicitly filters `passed` and `offer` statuses out (`FROZEN_STATUSES = {'passed','offer'}` in `crosswind.ts`), because re-routing rejected candidates is a different problem from re-routing active ones. The side effect: every **already-sourced** candidate the recruiter ever marked Passed becomes invisible to every cross-role surface in Credicrew. That dormant pool вҖ” silver medalists вҖ” is the highest-ROI sourcing channel a recruiter has, and Credicrew had no surface for it. New `frontend/src/lib/revive.ts` (~500 LOC, pure functions, deterministic, browser-first) walks every role's shortlist, lifts every `passed` entry into a `SilverEntry` (carrying the candidate's *original* match score against the from-role for the О” baseline), and re-scores each one against every *other currently open role's* plan via the same `matchCandidate` engine that powers Discover and Crosswind. From the resulting candidate Г— role grid it computes a single **reactivation score** per opportunity: `reactivation = matchScore Г— (RECENCY_FLOOR + (1 вҲ’ RECENCY_FLOOR) Г— recency)` where `recency = 2^(вҲ’daysDormant / RECENCY_HALF_LIFE_DAYS)` is exponential decay with a default 90-day half-life and `RECENCY_FLOOR = 0.5` so a year-old silver medalist never falls below half their fit weight вҖ” match quality dominates the queue, recency tilts it. Opportunities below `REVIVE_MATCH_FLOOR=65` (raw match) and below `REVIVE_COMPOSITE_FLOOR=55` (reactivation composite) are pruned so the queue stays honest. The engine also derives the supporting surfaces: a per-candidate roll-up that collapses each silver to their single best alternative role (sorted by reactivation score desc), a per-role roll-up that ranks every open role by its best available reactivation pick (capped at PER_ROLE_LIMIT=8), a histogram of reactivation scores in 10-pt buckets, a per-candidate `stale` flag at вүҘ 180 days dormant, and a `lift_band` that reads the revivable/silver ratio (high-yield вүҘ 50% В· healthy вүҘ 25% В· niche вүҘ 10% В· low-yield) so the headline tells the recruiter whether today's queue is worth working. Distinct-candidate cost-saved estimate is `|distinct_revivable_candidates| Г— $1500` so two opportunities for the same silver don't double-count. A `whyLines` generator emits readable lines per opportunity (О” vs original role bucketed at Вұ5/Вұ15 pts, matched-skills count + sample for the new role, location alignment, recency or staleness call-out) вҖ” same `MatchResult.matchedSkills`/`missingSkills`/`location.match` it always speaks. **Frontend surface** (`frontend/src/app/revive/page.tsx`, ~940 LOC): hero with eyebrow + 4-tile stat strip (silver pool size В· revivable count В· est. cost saved В· top-pick reactivation score, each tinted by its tier) and a one-line band advisory ("High-yield pool вҖ” More than half of your silver medalists are revivable вҖ” work the queue") tinted by the same band hue. Filter strip: min-reactivation slider, hide-stale toggle, by-candidate / by-open-role view toggle. **Opportunity card** (the centrepiece) вҖ” for each silver medalist with a passing fit: 12-px gradient seam tinted by tier, 48-px initials avatar tinted by tier, from-role pill (rose В· with original score) вҶ’ to-role pill (emerald В· with new score), О” pill (emerald if positive, rose if negative), a 108-px conic reactivation ring with hex tinted by tier (hot вүҘ 78 emerald В· warm вүҘ 65 sky В· tepid вүҘ 55 amber В· cold slate) and the inner well showing `Reactivation В· NN В· Hot/Warm/Tepid pick`, a two-pane matched-vs-missing skill diff (emerald chips matched, slate chips missing) for the *new* role, an animated recency bar (width = recency%, hue ramping green вҶ’ amber вҶ’ rose at staleness), 1вҖ“4 lines of "why now" reasoning, then the action row: emerald `Reactivate to <role>` primary button + `Show N other fits` expander toggle + a footer link to the original role. The expander shows every other open role that cleared the floor for this candidate, with per-row inline `Reactivate` buttons so a recruiter can pick the second-best fit if the first feels wrong. **By-role view** swaps to a 2-column grid of role cards each carrying a tier-tinted left rail, the role's best reactivation chip, and a stacked list of top picks (candidate name В· from-role В· days dormant В· reactivation chip В· per-row reactivate button). One-click **Reactivate** is the punch-line: adds the candidate to the new role's shortlist as `new` via the existing `addToShortlist`, writes a provenance note ("Reactivated from *original role* (silver medalist)") via `setNote`, then removes the candidate from the original role's `passed` bucket via `removeFromShortlist` so the queue doesn't re-surface the same person, then refreshes the engine on the same tick. **Empty state** for users with no `passed` entries yet: an inviting "рҹҘҲ No silver medalists yet" card with a one-click `вңЁ Seed demo pool` that drops 8 currently-unused candidates across the roles as `passed` entries with a synthetic dormancy spread (5d / 27d / 49d / 71d / вҖҰ) вҖ” uses raw localStorage round-trip to write `stageChangedAt` (the public `addToShortlist` API doesn't expose it directly). **Copy briefing** pours a markdown summary (pool size В· revivable В· cost saved В· pool quality band + blurb В· top pick with fromвҶ’to scores + first why line В· top 5 per-role best-pick lines) to the clipboard via the same `copyToClipboard` helper Crosswind uses. Polished CSS-in-JSX hover state on cards: `transform: translateY(-1px)` and a tier-coloured shadow via `box-shadow: 0 12px 40px -16px var(--rv-accent)` plus a `color-mix` border that picks up the tier hue. Navbar updated вҖ” both `components/Navbar.tsx` and the Discover-page inline header get a `Revive` link; the page's own header carries the full nav across 8 surfaces (Discover В· Roles В· HQ В· Crosswind В· **Revive** В· Cadence В· Channels В· Pipeline). **Backend mirror** (`backend/app/services/revive.py` ~360 LOC, `routers/revive.py` ~210 LOC) is the byte-for-byte Python port вҖ” same thresholds (`RECENCY_HALF_LIFE_DAYS=90`, `RECENCY_FLOOR=0.5`, `REVIVE_MATCH_FLOOR=65`, `REVIVE_COMPOSITE_FLOOR=55`, `STALE_DAYS=180`, `SOURCING_COST_PER_HIRE_USD=1500`, `PER_ROLE_LIMIT=8`), same per-candidate de-dupe (most-recent `passed_at_ms` wins for the canonical silver record), same recency math (`2^(вҲ’d/90)`), same composite formula, same "why" generator, same `lift_band` mapping. Pydantic models accept both `camelCase` (TS-client style) and `snake_case` payloads via `populate_by_name=True` and field aliases just like the Crosswind router does. New routes: `POST /revive/summary` (full engine, optionally inlining a `brief`), `POST /revive/brief` (re-renders a markdown brief from a posted summary dict вҖ” same fast path Crosswind uses), `GET /revive/defaults` (publishes the thresholds + formulas so clients stay in sync). API version bumped `0.13.0 вҶ’ 0.14.0`; main.py registers `revive_router` after `crosswind_router` and the root manifest enumerates the three new endpoints. **Validation**: `next build` clean вҖ” type-check passes, lint clean after killing four unused-import / unused-vars / unescaped-quote findings, `/revive` builds at **8.41 kB** (109 kB First Load JS, comparable to `/crosswind` at 10.2 kB / 112 kB and lighter than `/hq` at 13.3 kB / 121 kB); backend `python3 -c "from app.routers.revive import router"` imports cleanly; end-to-end smoke against a 3-role Г— 3-candidate fixture (2 silver medalists at 20 days and 200 days dormant, 1 unrelated candidate) returns `silver=2, opportunities=2, revivable_count=2, cost_saved=$3.0k, top=Asha P В· Senior Backend вҶ’ Mid Python Remote В· reactivation=80 at 20 days dormant`, brief composes correctly with the High-yield-pool band, recency decay visibly demoting the 200-day entry below the 20-day one. README updated вҖ” top-level intro paragraph extended with the Revive sentence ("reactivates the silver-medalist pool with **Revive** вҖ” the candidates you already paid to source but passed on, re-scored against every other open role with a 90-day recency-decay so the queue stays fresh and sunk-cost talent never falls out of the funnel quietly"); new **"What's new вҖ” Revive (Day 62)"** section above Crosswind with the gap-analysis framing, the reactivation formula, every UI surface explained, the backend-mirror parity claim, the verified fixture numbers, and a `curl` example for `POST /revive/summary`. |

| 63 | 2026-06-24 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-14 move: shipped **Drift Lab вҖ” Output Stability & Variance Tester** (`/api/drift` + the **Drift** tab). Every prior quality surface in the playground perturbs *something* about the call вҖ” Adversary changes the *input*, Showdown changes the *prompt*, Suites/Rubrics/Judge change the *test case*. None of them answered the question every engineer who ships at `temperature > 0` eventually asks: *if I call this exact prompt eight times in a row against this exact model, how non-deterministic is the answer?* Drift Lab is that surface. New `backend/src/drift.py` (~880 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `pricing.estimate_cost`, mirrors the adversary/showdown engine pattern вҖ” sqlite + `ThreadPoolExecutor` parallel fan-out + dryrun fallback path so the demo lights up with zero API keys) is a single deterministic function `run_drift(drift_id) вҶ’ (DriftReport, status)`. **Replay batch**: fires `n_replays` (default 8, clamped 3вҖ“16) parallel calls to `(provider, model)` at the same `temperature` + `top_p`, captures `(response, in/out tokens, cost via pricing.estimate_cost, wall-clock latency)` per replay, with per-call try/except so a single transient 5xx never kills the batch. **Composite Stability Score** (0вҖ“100) = `0.55В·lexical + 0.30В·length + 0.15В·latency`, weights renormalised over whichever axes have data so a single missing axis doesn't collapse the score to 0. `lexical = 100 В· mean_pairwise_jaccard(3-gram word shingles)` (unigram fallback when responses are too short to form a 3-gram set so a one-sentence reply still gets a meaningful similarity number); `length = 100В·(1 вҲ’ clip(Пғ/Ој, 0, 1))` on output-token counts (penalises models whose verbosity changes call-to-call); `latency = 100В·(1 вҲ’ clip(Пғ/Ој, 0, 1))` on wall-clock time. Bands: **Steady вүҘ 80 В· Consistent вүҘ 60 В· Drifty вүҘ 40 В· Wild < 40**. **Variance type** classifier (first-match-wins ladder, *order matters*): `Steady` (lex вүҘ 90 AND length-CV вүӨ 0.08) вҶ’ "boringly stable" В· `Substantive` (lex < 50) вҶ’ "replies disagree on substance, not just wording" В· `Verbose` (length-CV вүҘ 0.20) вҶ’ "same gist, verbosity drifts" В· `Cosmetic` (else) вҶ’ "same answer, slightly reworded". Drives a calibrated advisory ladder so the headline isn't just flatter вҖ” `Drifty + Substantive` recommends *"add explicit constraints вҖ” scope, format, refusal rules"*, `Drifty + Verbose` recommends *"add an explicit length constraint"*, `Wild` (any type) says *"unsafe to ship at this temperature, either pin to T=0 or rewrite with hard constraints"*. **Cluster surface**: full nГ—n Jaccard similarity matrix + **single-link clustering** at a tunable `П„` (default 0.55, slider 0.2вҖ“0.95) вҶ’ connected components on the thresholded similarity graph, stable first-touch labelling so cluster 0 always contains sample 0. `n_clusters = 1` means *the model always says basically the same thing*, `n_clusters = N` means *total chaos, every reply is its own cluster*. **Medoid pick** вҖ” single response with the highest mean-similarity to every other reply ("the canonical answer most users will actually see") вҖ” crowned across the heatmap, cluster columns, and per-reply grid. **Persistence**: two tables (`drift_runs` + `drift_samples`, shared sqlite lock with `history._DB_LOCK`), runs are re-runnable in place (wipes prior samples on each `/run`), samples carry their assigned `cluster_id` + per-row mean-sim so the UI never re-derives. Eight HTTP endpoints proxied through `routes/llm.py`: `GET /defaults В· GET /stats В· GET / В· POST / В· POST /seed В· GET /<id> В· POST /<id>/run В· DELETE /<id>`, live mode gated behind `{confirm_live: true}` like adversary/showdown so the user never accidentally spends credits. **Dryrun synthesis** вҖ” deterministic per-`(prompt, idx)` seed picks one of two baseline answers, applies `temperature`-scaled synonym swaps (8 wordвҶ’3 options map: answerвҶ’reply/response/message, issueвҶ’problem/concern/matter, etc.), `temperature`-scaled length jiggle (appends 0вҖ“5 extra clauses from a pool of 5), and at `T вүҘ 0.9` even reorders clauses вҖ” so the demo produces a meaningful **Drifty (59/100) вҖ” Substantive drift** signature on the customer-support seed without any API keys. **Frontend** (`llm_playground_frontend/src/components/DriftLab.jsx`, ~1100 LOC, mirrors AdversaryLab/ShowdownArena layout DNA вҖ” same dark slate palette + shadcn/ui primitives + same Setup/Results tab split + same RunRail left rail): full surface in five layers. (1) **Header band** with a `Waves` icon in a gradient cyanвҶ’fuchsia tile, title + "new" gradient pill, 5-tile `StatsStrip` (Runs В· Avg stability В· Best stability В· Steady runs В· Wild runs, each hue-ramped). (2) **Setup tab** вҖ” name + description + system_prompt + user_prompt (Textareas, mono font, identical-across-replays caption on the user prompt to make the held-constant axis explicit) + provider/model picker (dryrun-gated, hidden when dryrun is on) + a **4-slider tile strip** (`Replays В· Temperature В· Top-p В· Cluster П„`, each tile carries its own icon + hue-tinted inset shadow + live mono value chip + a native `<input type="range">` with `accentColor` set to the tile hue) + dryrun toggle + a "How Drift Lab scores stability" explainer card that walks through the composite formula with the current `n_replays` and `П„` interpolated inline. (3) **Hero results card** вҖ” 168 px `StabilityRing` (conic-gradient, breathing glow, hue-ramped redвҶ’emerald via `hsl(valueВ·1.25, 78%, 48%)`) carrying composite/band/variance, the run name + band chip + variance chip + dry-run/live pill, headline + advisory (italic, with a `TrendingUp` icon tinted to the band hue), three `ScoreBar` mini-charts (lexical/length/latency, hue-ramped on the same scale as the ring so the eye trains), and a vertical action stack (Re-run В· Copy all В· Export JSON В· Delete). (4) **Heatmap card** вҖ” full nГ—n grid painted by `simHue` (`hsl(jaccardВ·125, 70+simВ·10%, 36+simВ·14%)`, so 0.0вҶ’deep red, 0.5вҶ’amber, 1.0вҶ’bright emerald), cell labels in tabular-nums when вүҘ 28 px, the medoid's row + column gain a 1-px amber inset outline (`rgba(250,204,21,0.65)`), every cell has a tooltip `"#i вҶ” #j вҖ” Jaccard 0.XX"`, vertical gradient legend on the right with a `Crown В· medoid #N` caption. (5) **Cluster columns** (side-by-side with the heatmap on `xl` screens) вҖ” one card per cluster, tinted by an 8-colour `distinctClusterPalette` (emerald/cyan/violet/amber/rose/pink/lime/sky), inset 3-px left rail, each member listed with `#index В· Ој-sim В· token-count`, medoid crowned. (6) **Per-replay grid** (responsive 1/2/3 cols) вҖ” every reply as its own card: replay-index pill in the cluster's hue, `ClusterChip`, a 36 px `SimRing` (0вҖ“1 conic gradient) for that reply's Ој-sim, a 3-tile mini-strip (`Tokens В· Latency В· Cost`), then the response body truncated to 240 chars with show-full/copy controls; the medoid card gets an amber ring + amber-rail + `Crown` badge. (7) **Run-config foot** вҖ” 5-pill row (Model В· Provider В· Temperature В· Top-p В· Duration) so the page is self-describing for screenshots. New API helpers in `services/api.js` (`listDrifts В· createDrift В· seedDrift В· driftStats В· driftDefaults В· getDrift В· deleteDrift В· runDrift`), new `Drift` radio tab in App.jsx (after Showdown, with the same "new" gradient pill), new dispatch branch in the main mode-switch. **Validation**: backend smoke via `python3 -c` end-to-end вҖ” seedвҶ’runвҶ’getвҶ’listвҶ’statsвҶ’defaultsвҶ’delete all green, the canonical seed produces `score=59.21, band=Drifty, variance=Substantive, lex=47.84, len=68.91, lat=81.51, mean_sim=0.4783, min_sim=0.3107, length_cv=0.31, n_clusters=1 (8 in one cluster), medoid=replay #4`; HTTP smoke via Flask `test_client` against the live `src.main:app` вҖ” all 8 endpoints return correct status codes (defaults 200, seed 201, run 200, list 200, get 200, stats 200, delete 200, create-live + run-without-confirm correctly 400s with the credits-warning message); HTTP smoke via `curl` against a real `python3 src/main.py` boot вҖ” `/api/health` 200, `/api/drift/defaults` returns the expected band catalogue, `/api/drift/seed` returns a fresh drift id. | 64 | 2026-06-25 | **SynapseOS** | Shipped **Spark вҖ” the first generative surface in SynapseOS.** Every prior surface (Atlas / Pulse / Chronicle / Tensions / Echoes / Synthesis) is observational вҖ” it describes what's *already* in your graph. Spark inverts that: it reads the *holes* and proposes the next note that would fill each one вҖ” title + opener + tags + cited evidence + predicted cluster + predicted synapses вҖ” so the canvas stops being a snapshot and starts being a queue. Click вңҰ on a spark and the NoteComposer pre-fills; you skim, edit, save. **Five spark kinds**, each tuned to a specific graph pathology: (1) **bridge** вҖ” two clusters with centroid cosine вүҘ 0.18 but no synapse (OR вүҘ 0.20 with strongest cross-edge < 0.22 = fragile link); drafts "X вҶ” Y" with one anchor sentence from each cluster's highest-centrality member. (2) **distill** вҖ” cohesive cluster with `max_weight < 0.55` (un-anchored) OR `size вүҘ 6` with `mean_centrality < 0.45` (large+loose); drafts "What X really is" stitching the leading sentences of the three highest-centrality members. (3) **counter** вҖ” hub note with `weight вүҘ 0.45` whose cluster carries no opposing-stance signal (no antonyms over an explicit pair map: simple/complex, fast/slow, centralized/decentralized, вҖҰ, AND no strong-stance markers like "against / rebuttal / overrated / fallacy"); drafts "Against [hub title]" opening with the hub's leading claim. (4) **frontier** вҖ” a 6+ char concept-shaped term that appears in only the cluster's newest note (вүӨ 30d) and nowhere else in your graph (with `-ly` adverbs and pure-digit/stopword tokens filtered); drafts "On 'term'" before the concept slips away. (5) **revive** вҖ” a vault: cohesion вүҘ 0.45, activity вүӨ 0.20, dormancy вүҘ 30d; drafts "Returning to X" framed around the cluster's distinctive vocabulary. **Every spark carries**: a deterministic `sha1` 6-char id (so reloads return stable cards), a `priority` (kind base + predicted-synapse bonus + per-kind signal strength), a one-sentence `rationale`, a draft `title`, a draft `body`, slugified `tags` (cluster terms first then distinctive draft terms, deduped, capped at 4), the `cited_evidence` it draws from with cluster pills, **`predicted_cluster`** (best-matching community centroid for the embedded draft + a strength score 0вҖ“1), and **`predicted_synapses`** вҖ” the top-K notes the draft would synapse to if committed, computed by running the *same* cosine + top-K cap the live `/graph` uses against the hypothetical draft vector. Sparks that would land outside the graph's gravity well (zero predicted synapses) are dropped. New `backend/app/spark.py` (~880 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic, reuses the graph/community/embed stack, two-phase: per-kind candidate selection вҶ’ enrichment with predicted cluster + synapses вҶ’ global priority re-rank). New schemas (`SparkOut`, `SparkReportOut`, `SparkEvidenceOut`, `SparkPredictedSynapseOut`). New endpoints `GET /spark?threshold&top_k&limit&per_kind&kinds=bridge,вҖҰ` and `GET /spark/export.md` for paste-anywhere planning. Frontend: new `Spark.tsx` modal (~570 LOC) вҖ” glowing вҡЎ header tile with pulsing animation, gradient header band (violet вҶ’ cyan вҶ’ lime вҶ’ amber), filter chips with live per-kind counts and kind-specific tinting + glow, stats strip on the right (avg synapses / notes / clusters), 2-column responsive card grid where each card carries its kind glyph in its tint colour, a 36px circular priority ring (hue-matched), the drafted title + italic rationale, body preview with show-full toggle for long openers, hue-tinted tag chips, a "**if you commit this**" panel listing predicted-cluster (with the cluster's dot colour + landing strength) and predicted-synapses (each with a cyanвҶ’violet hue-ramped strength bar and the target note's title clickable to jump on canvas), a "**cites**" panel showing each evidence note with cluster pills + quoted snippet, and an action row with **вңҰ use this draft** (sends to NoteComposer via the same `NoteDraft` channel Tensions's Reconcile uses) + a details toggle. Empty state for "no sparks of kind X." Header pill in violetвҶ’cyanвҶ’amber gradient with a pulsing вҡЎ glyph, a "new" badge, a live count of queued sparks, and a 20вҶ’28px shadow halo that brightens on hover. ## Next pick

After **SynapseOS** вҶ’ next is **Titan** (round 14, day 65 of the
