| 65 | 2026-06-26 | **Titan** | Round-14 move: shipped **Lineage вҖ” temporal fund-flow tracer**, the *follow-the-money* lens every prior TITAN surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day-60 every TITAN engine answers either a *structural* question (`network` shows who is connected to whom) or an *aggregate / temporal-delta* question (`pulse` shows what changed across the book, `drift` shows account-vs-self movement, `peer` shows cohort outliers). None of them answer the question a real investigator opens with the moment a SAR draft lands вҖ” *"where did this money come from, where did it go, and how much of it can I actually trace from origin to destination?"*. New `apps/ai-aml/lineage.py` (~900 LOC, pure-stdlib, zero new deps, **zero new physics** вҖ” reuses the same Tx shape + name/geo conventions as `risk.py`) is a single deterministic function `compute_lineage(transactions, seed, direction, max_depth, window_days, now) вҶ’ LineageReport`. **Trace walker** is a BFS bounded by direction (`forward` = downstream / `backward` = upstream / `both`), `max_depth вҲҲ [1,8]`, and a time window anchored at the latest tx in the batch (so a forward trace doesn't drop downstream hops that happen after the seed's last touch вҖ” a subtle bug fixed pre-commit). Each visited account becomes a `LineageNode` (depth В· direction В· geo В· role_tags В· activity stats В· suspicion_score 0..1 composed from fan-in/out + retention + smurf-band match + depth), each transaction a `LineageEdge` (timestamp В· channel В· geo_src/dst В· src_depth В· dst_depth В· traceable_fraction В· pattern_tags). **FIFO lot tracer** is the heart of the engine вҖ” for every account it maintains an ordered `deque[_Lot]` of inflow chunks tagged with `(source_id, depth, hops)`; when funds leave, it consumes oldest-first and copies attribution forward (the same convention every forensic accountant uses for commingled funds вҖ” provably the legal default in *Re Hallett's Estate*). Lots below `PROVENANCE_MIN_SHARE = 0.5%` are folded into a single `__other__` bucket so the surface stays readable; the per-account `provenance` map sums to 1.0 and is the exact lens regulators use to argue "X% of this account came from a smurfing ring". **Six flow-shape detectors** then run over the built DAG вҖ” patterns single-account scoring *can't* see because they only exist *across* the trail: (1) **`smurf_chain`** вҖ” вүҘ5 distinct senders with sub-threshold deposits (вӮ№40-50k FIU-IND CTR band) into one funnel that wires out вүҘвӮ№1L within 72h, confidence `0.4 + 0.05В·(senders-5) + 0.3В·out_conversion`, severity high; (2) **`round_trip`** вҖ” DFS from seed-outflows forward in time-respecting order back to seed in вүӨ4 hops; fires when вүҘ20% of seed outflow returns via вүҘ2 hops, confidence `0.35 + 0.5В·return_fraction + 0.04В·loop_length`, severity critical (it's confirmed layering); (3) **`pass_through`** вҖ” node with `distinct_inflows вүҘ 3` AND `distinct_outflows вүҘ 3` AND `retention вүӨ 12%`, confidence `0.3 + 0.05В·fan_in + 0.05В·fan_out + 0.3В·(1 - retention/threshold)`, severity medium; (4) **`integration`** вҖ” round-amount transfer (`amt вүҘ вӮ№2.5L AND amt % вӮ№10k == 0`) into a clean-asset venue (substring match on real estate / realty / developers / properties / auto / motors / jewell / gold / art / auction / yacht / casino / luxury / diamond), confidence `0.45 + 0.05В·(hits-1) + 0.15В·min(2, biggest/threshold)`, severity medium; (5) **`velocity_ramp`** вҖ” sort the trail's edges by time, split into early/late halves, ratio `late_avg_interval / early_avg_interval вүӨ 0.55` triggers (rush-to-layer signal вҖ” launderers accelerate as they approach integration), confidence `0.4 + 0.4В·(1 - ratio/threshold)`, severity medium; (6) **`geo_hopping`** вҖ” вүҘ3 distinct jurisdictions across all edge endpoints AND вүҘ3 edges, confidence `0.4 + 0.12В·(distinct-3) + 0.04В·edges`, severity high. Each match emits a stable `code`, accent colour, 0..1 `confidence`, ranked `evidence` chips (every chip uses `**bold**` markdown for the headline numbers), `contributing_nodes`, recommended `action`, and a `severity_floor` that promotes downstream case priority. The full catalogue + thresholds dumps at `GET /aml/lineage/rules` so an auditor can verify the formulas match the README before the engine ships. **Trail score** вҲҲ [0, 100] composes five normalised factors вҖ” `0.40В·depth_factor + 0.25В·amount_factor + 0.15В·pattern_factor + 0.10В·geo_factor + 0.10В·suspicious_node_factor` вҖ” each normalised to [0,1] before weighting (depth full at +4, amount full at вӮ№10L, pattern full at confidence-sum 3, geo full at 4 distinct jurisdictions, suspicious_node full at 50% of nodes flagged); the per-factor `value В· normalised В· weight В· contribution` echo back so the analyst can see *why* the trail scored what it did. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins on the score): `critical вүҘ 75` В· `active вүҘ 55` В· `watch вүҘ 35` В· `calm < 35`. **Headline** composer writes a one-line narrative naming the top pattern + hop count + recommended action; **advisory** rolls up score + pattern count + hop chain length. **Plan-of-action** is the action layer вҖ” prioritised checklist that names the TITAN tab each action lives in: `freeze` row (critical) вҶ’ "Escalate **X** to MLRO вҖ” recommend SAR and freeze pending review", per-pattern actions inherited from `PATTERN_META[code].action`, KYC-refresh row for any `pass_through` mule вҶ’ "Re-anchor KYC on **X** in the **Profile** tab", and a network deep-link вҶ’ "Open the **Network** tab on the seed neighbourhood вҖ” confirm structural counterparties match the lineage trail". Each `PulseAction`-style row carries `kind В· priority В· body В· href` so the surface deep-links into `/cases?account_id=вҖҰ`, `/profile?customer_id=вҖҰ`, `/network?seed=вҖҰ`. **Serialisation**: `to_dict()` ships a `titan.lineage.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at В· engine В· seed В· seed_label В· direction В· max_depth В· window_days В· window_start/end В· nodes[] В· edges[] В· patterns[] В· trail_score В· mood В· headline В· advisory В· factors[] В· total_amount_traced В· distinct_geos В· longest_path В· plan_of_action); `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able SAR В§3 exhibit (~2.5 KB) вҖ” headline В· advisory В· trail-summary table В· detected-patterns sections В· longest path В· seed provenance В· plan-of-action numbered list. **Sample fixture** вҖ” bundled 28-tx synthetic three-arm laundering chain rooted at `ACC-AUR-01` (Aurelia Shell Limited from the existing customer book): six sub-threshold smurfs from six distinct payers вҶ’ funnel = seed; funnel wires two large legs (вӮ№1.8L + вӮ№1.2L) into a layering web spanning Coastal Bridge Services (AE) вҶ’ Pyongyang Horizon Trading (KP) вҶ’ Aliekseii Volkov-Baranov (RU) вҶ’ Bashir Crossing Holdings (IR); the middle mule splits into three integration destinations (Helios Realty Developers, Marble Lane Properties, Auragold Jewellery Mart); a вӮ№5L round wire lands in Helios Realty (integration); a вӮ№42k slice returns to the seed via Niamh O'Riordan (round-trip closure, 27% of outflow returns); a late вӮ№2.5L car-dealership hop in AE produces the velocity-ramp shape. The demo lights up *all five* relevant detectors out of the box (round-trip 63%, pass-through 100%, integration 85%, smurf 80%, geo-hop 100%) for a trail score of **91/100 mood=critical**, headline `"Critical trail В· around Aurelia Shell Limited В· pass-through mule (100% confidence)"`, longest path `ACC-AUR-01 вҶ’ ACC-LAYER-1 вҶ’ ACC-LAYER-2 вҶ’ ACC-MULE-1 вҶ’ ACC-DEST-A вҶ’ ACC-DEST-E` (5 hops), 18 nodes / 25 edges / вӮ№21.9L traced across 5 jurisdictions. Curated seed picker also lights up `ACC-MULE-1` (Aliekseii Volkov-Baranov, pass-through mule), `ACC-DEST-A` (Helios Realty Developers, integration entry), `ACC-LAYER-2` (Pyongyang Horizon Trading, layering hub). **Five new endpoints** in the AML service: `GET /aml/lineage/rules` (auditor-facing), `GET /aml/lineage/seeds` (curated picker), `GET /aml/lineage/sample` (the 28-tx fixture demo), `POST /aml/lineage/trace` (caller-supplied transactions), `GET /aml/lineage/export.md` (markdown exhibit, `text/markdown; charset=utf-8`). All five mirrored through the gateway in `apps/api/main.py` so the frontend has one origin. AML service version bumped `1.11.0 вҶ’ 1.12.0`. **Frontend** вҖ” new `/lineage` route inserted at NAV between Network and Drift (so the structuralвҶ’lineageвҶ’behavioural-drift progression reads as one investigative arc). `apps/frontend/app/lineage/page.tsx` (~720 LOC, full type-safe, zero charting libraries вҖ” every visualisation is hand-rolled SVG / CSS gradient). Render stack: (1) **Hero** вҖ” mood-tinted radial gradient (`MOOD_BG`) glass-strong panel with a 168 px breathing conic-gradient score ring + headline + advisory; control row with a seed picker (loaded from `/aml/lineage/seeds`), a 3-button direction selector (Both / Downstream / Upstream with tooltips), a depth slider (1-6), and a 4-button window selector (7d / 14d / 30d / 60d); action buttons for `Recompute`, `Download В§3 exhibit (.md)`, and `Open seed in Cases` / `Open seed in Network` deep-links. (2) **6-tile vital-signs strip** (Nodes traced В· Edges traced В· Depth В· Amount traced В· Jurisdictions В· Patterns), each hue-rim-lit with `inset 4px 0 0 0 hue`. (3) **Temporal DAG canvas** вҖ” the centrepiece, fully responsive (measures container, redraws on resize): X axis is time (window-start вҶ’ end), Y axis is hop depth from seed (negative = upstream, positive = downstream). Nodes are circles sized by `sqrt(amount/max)` (radius 7-23 px), filled charcoal, ringed in rose/amber/grey by suspicion_score, with a dashed accent ring keyed to the dominant role_tag (funnel orange В· mule gold В· layer rose В· integration violet В· smurf orange). The seed node is white-ringed, lime-tinted, and breathing (`lineage-node-pulse` 2.4s ease-in-out). Edges are bГ©zier curves with thickness `1.0 + 3.6В·sqrt(amount/max)` and stroke colour by pattern tag вҖ” flagged edges get the animated `lineage-flow-line` (4-4 dasharray, 1.6s linear infinite, marching ants) so the eye reads them as live flow. Time-axis grid at 25/50/75% with dotted strokes; first/last labels at the bottom; hop bounds at the left. Click any node вҶ’ highlights it (3 px ring) and opens the provenance drawer. Legend strip with six pattern-colour swatches. Deterministic вҖ” same input always produces identical coordinates because the layout fn is a pure function of `(nodes, edges, canvas_w, canvas_h)`, with a deterministic collision-resolver that shifts overlapping nodes by 26 px increments sorted by `account_id`. (4) **Patterns + Provenance side-by-side** (`lg:grid-cols-[1.4fr_1fr]`). Patterns list ranks every detected pattern with a card per pattern вҖ” left rail in the pattern accent (`3 px solid`), label + code + severity sub-line, confidence pill (background `${accent}1f` + text `${accent}`), evidence chips through the `**bold**` markdown parser, contributing-node pills (each clickable вҶ’ opens that node's provenance), and the recommended-action footer in a charcoal sub-panel. Provenance drawer when a node is selected вҖ” header with display name + account_id + depth + geo, suspicion chip on the right; role-tags chip row; 4-tile activity grid (Inflow В· Outflow В· Retention В· Active range); the FIFO-traced inflow-provenance breakdown as labelled bars with `(name В· share% В· hops)` rows вҖ” each row clickable to drill into that upstream source; "Open in Profile" CTA at the bottom. (5) **Trail-score breakdown** вҖ” five labelled bars (depth В· amount В· pattern В· geo В· suspicious_node) showing each factor's contribution in mood-accent colour with a `w{weight}` mono caption. (6) **Plan-of-action** numbered list with priority-hue left rails (rose for critical, orange for high, gold for medium, slate for low), each row deep-linked into the next TITAN tab when `href` is set. (7) **Explainer footer** with engine version + composite formula + the six pattern codes in a font-mono line. New CSS keyframes in `globals.css`: `lineage-flow` (stroke-dashoffset 0 вҶ’ -16 over 1.6s linear infinite вҖ” the marching-ants animation on flagged edges), `lineage-pulse` (opacity + scale on the seed node), `.lineage-hero` (rose + sky + violet radial gradient backdrop). **Validation**: pure `ast.parse` clean on `lineage.py`, `apps/ai-aml/main.py`, `apps/api/main.py`; engine end-to-end smoke pass via `python -c` on the bundled fixture вҖ” produces `mood=critical, score=91, nodes=18, edges=25, patterns=[pass_through, geo_hopping, integration, smurf_chain, round_trip]`, longest path `ACC-AUR-01 вҶ’ вҖҰ вҶ’ ACC-DEST-E` (5 hops), distinct_geos `[AE, IN, IR, KP, RU]`, factors `depth=40.0, amount=25.0, pattern=15.0, geo=10.0, suspicious_node=1.1`, plan starts with `[critical] Escalate Aurelia Shell Limited to MLRO`. Arbitrary 3-hop forward trace `ACC-A вҶ’ ACC-B вҶ’ ACC-C вҶ’ ACC-D` correctly traverses to depth 3 (`nodes=4, edges=3, path=ACC-A вҶ’ ACC-B вҶ’ ACC-C вҶ’ ACC-D`). Markdown brief renders end-to-end at ~2.5 KB with trail-summary table + per-pattern sections + longest-path arrow chain + seed provenance table + plan-of-action numbered list. `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0 across the whole frontend; `npx next build` clean вҖ” `/lineage` route emitted at **6.87 kB / 103 kB First Load** (in line with `/pulse` at 6.74 kB despite carrying a hand-rolled SVG DAG renderer + animated edges + provenance drawer + plan + score breakdown because every visualisation is pure SVG / CSS, no charting library imported). **README** вҖ” new "Day-65 вҖ” Lineage" callout block inserted at the top of `titan-v2/README.md` between the lead paragraph and the existing Day-60 callout, walking through the positioning vs other TITAN surfaces, the FIFO lot-tracer convention, the six detector formulas in a Markdown table, the trail-score composite, the mood ladder, the plan-of-action format, the five endpoints, the surface render stack, and the determinism guarantee. |
| 66 | 2026-06-27 | **WaySafe** | Round-14 move: shipped **Echo вҖ” Post-Trip Debrief & Counterfactual**, the *retrospective* lens every prior WaySafe surface had left to the analyst. Up to Day 65 every surface is forward-looking: Pulse opens the day (`tabs[0]`), Tempo picks the depart-minute, Plan Route prices the corridor, Live Trip streams alerts during. Once the trip ends, the state was dropped onto Trip Log as a flat row and the page turned вҖ” no surface asked the question every traveller asks the moment they arrive: *"how did it actually go? Were the alerts the right ones? What did I avoid? What would a different flavor have looked like?"*. New `echo.py` (~750 LOC, pure-stdlib, zero new deps, **zero new physics** вҖ” every number traces back to `safety.point_risk`, the `routing` A*, or the recorded `companion.heartbeats`) is a single deterministic function `compute_echo(trip, incidents, geofences, pois, forecaster, broadcasts_count, now) вҶ’ EchoReport`. **Composite trip score** вҲҲ [0, 100] composes four weighted factors so Echo and Tempo never disagree on a band name (same `All-clear вүҘ80 В· Caution вүҘ65 В· Elevated вүҘ50 В· High Risk вүҘ35 В· Danger` ladder): `0.35В·realized_avg_safety + 0.25В·exposure_score + 0.25В·event_score + 0.15В·fence_score` where `realized_avg_safety = mean(100В·(1вҲ’heartbeat.risk))` over the recorded trace, `exposure_score = 100В·exp(вҲ’0.35В·risk_km)` (Tempo's Оә=0.35 so a risk-km of 0.64 вҶ’ 80, 1.23 вҶ’ 65, 1.98 вҶ’ 50, 3.0 вҶ’ 35 are exactly the same band crossings on both surfaces), `event_score = clip(100 вҲ’ 40В·user_sos вҲ’ 30В·auto_sos вҲ’ 10В·n_critical_alert вҲ’ 4В·n_warn_alert)`, `fence_score = 100В·(1 вҲ’ km_inside_geofence/total_km)`. **Mood ladder** (first-match-wins, top-to-bottom): `Critical` if user_sos OR auto_sos OR trip_score < 45 OR n_critical вүҘ 2 В· `Rough` if trip_score < 60 OR n_warn вүҘ 3 OR n_critical вүҘ 1 В· `Watch` if trip_score < 75 OR n_warn вүҘ 1 В· else `Smooth`. **Realised corridor** is built from `trip.heartbeats` (the `(ts, lat, lon, point_risk_0_1)` quads the Live Trip Companion already records on every tick) with cumulative-km per sample вҖ” a 4-sample-minimum threshold falls back to a 24-point evenly-spaced sample of the planned coords re-priced at `safety.point_risk(now=depart_at)` so a synthetic/replayed trip with no heartbeat trace still has a realised basis. **Risk-km** is trapezoidal integration of risk over km along the corridor; **geofence dwell** is the per-segment km inside any `goa_geofences.geojson` polygon (per-endpoint `point_in_polygon`, half-credit for a sample-pair where only one endpoint is inside вҖ” the cleanest interpretation when the trip crosses a polygon edge between heartbeats). **Counterfactual card pack** re-plans the same `(origin, dest, depart_at)` with three flavors and quotes the О” vs the actual run on each: `fastest` via `routing.plan_fastest_route` (Оұ=0), `safest` via `routing.plan_safest_route` (Оұ=4.5), and `forecast-safest` via `routing.plan_forecast_route(forecaster, depart_at)` when a `HazardForecaster` is supplied. Each counterfactual is scored on the same composite assuming no events fired (CF event_score = 100) so the delta names *only* the route-and-timing component. The **strongest alternative** is the highest positive `delta_trip_score`; when no alternative beats the actual, Echo says so. Per-card deltas surface as `О” score` / `О” risk-km` / `О” time` / `О” dist` / `О” min-safety`. **Alert calibration** grades every `risk_ahead` alert the companion fired against the heartbeat trace that followed: **true-positive** when the next 90 s actually crossed risk вүҘ 0.45, **false-alarm** when the next 90 s stayed below 0.32 (the hysteresis recovery floor вҖ” the same band the companion's hysteresis was designed around, so ambiguous reads in [0.32, 0.45) aren't penalised either way), **miss** for a heartbeat with risk вүҘ 0.45 that had no upstream `risk_ahead` within 120 s. A Brier-style `sharpness_score = mean((predicted вҲ’ actual)ВІ)` over heartbeats bands the calibration `Sharp < 0.06 В· OK < 0.12 В· Noisy < 0.20 В· Off`. An **outcome-aware override** promotes the band to `Sharp` when every alert resolved into a true-positive *and* nothing slipped past unwarned, so a single alert that persisted across multiple heartbeats (high Brier from persistence) but ultimately matched a real event isn't labelled "Off" just because of the persistence artefact вҖ” the user-facing semantics of "did the alerts work?" wins over the raw probabilistic loss. **Event timeline** merges `trip.alerts` and `trip.milestones` into a single chronological list with severity-coloured left rails (rose for SOS/critical, amber for warn, lime for geofence-exit / arrival, sky for info), and per-event `rel_km` looked up by nearest-corridor-sample so the analyst can see *where on the corridor* each fire happened вҖ” not just *when*. **Lessons** is a deterministic, first-match-wins ladder of natural-language bullets keyed to the report's own numbers; each names the WaySafe tab the analyst should open next so the debrief deep-links into the rest of the surface: `рҹҶҳ You triggered the manual SOS вҖ” open Alerts for the dispatch log` В· `рҹӣЎ The safest route at the same depart would have been +12 pts (saving 0.30 risk-km) at +10 min. Open Plan Route and try safest next time.` В· `рҹҡ· 4 min (35%) inside geofenced risk zones. Tempo will surface a depart-time slot that threads around the corridor.` В· `вҡ пёҸ N critical alerts вҖ” Sentinel may already be tracking the cluster.` В· `рҹ“ү Realised safety came in N pts under the plan вҖ” the static score under-priced this corridor.` В· `рҹ”§ Risk-ahead alerts over-warned (3 false alarms) вҖ” tighten RISK_AHEAD_THRESHOLD.` В· `рҹ“Ё K broadcasts dispatched to your trusted contacts.` A `вҸұ Open Tempo to optimise the depart-window` close-out lands when no Tempo lesson fired so the brief always has a forward-looking next click. **Serialisation**: `to_dict()` ships a `waysafe.echo.v1` JSON envelope (composed_at В· trip_id В· status В· origin/dest + labels В· route_mode В· depart/arrived В· distance / duration В· trip_score В· band В· mood В· 4 factors[] В· realized_avg_safety В· realized_min_safety В· risk_km В· geofence_minutes / fraction В· fence_score В· event_score В· exposure_score В· planned vs realized В· corridor[] В· timeline[] В· alerts counters В· scenarios[] В· best_alternative В· calibration В· headline В· advisory В· lessons[]). `to_json()` round-trips. `to_markdown()` ships a paste-able trip-journal entry (~3 KB) вҖ” headline / advisory / score-breakdown table / 40-event timeline / counterfactual comparison table / calibration block / numbered lessons вҖ” for the family-share / WhatsApp / email use case. **Frontend** вҖ” new `render_echo` in `theme.py` (~360 LOC of pure HTML+CSS, zero charting libs; every visualisation is a conic-gradient ring, a flex strip, or a 1-D corridor heat-bar with diagonal-hatch overlay for geofence segments). Render stack: (1) **Hero** вҖ” radial-gradient mood-tinted glass panel with a 178 px breathing conic-gradient score ring (`trip_score`-filled, hue by band) + headline + advisory + chip strip (route mode, distance, duration, risk-km, fence-minutes, criticals, SOS, broadcasts) + right-rail mood card (`рҹҹў Smooth` / `рҹҹЎ Watch` / `рҹҹ  Rough` / `рҹ”ҙ Critical`). (2) **4-tile factor strip** showing each composite factor's value + weight + contribution + detail with a `inset 4px 0 0 0 rim` keyed to the factor's own band. (3) **Realised-corridor heat strip** вҖ” a 1-D flex strip of N corridor cells, each `background = risk-hued rgba`, with a 45В° diagonal-hatch overlay (`repeating-linear-gradient`) on cells inside a geofenced polygon; left/right legend labels the origin and destination at the strip ends. (4) **Counterfactual card grid** вҖ” one card per scenario (`actual` / `fastest` / `safest` / `forecast-safest`), each hue-bordered by its own band with the strongest-alternative card carrying a glowing radial gradient + `best alt` pill. Card body shows the exposure score (big) В· band В· risk-km В· distance / ETA / min-safety; non-actual cards close with a 5-cell delta grid `(О” score В· О” risk-km В· О” time В· О” dist В· О” min-safety)` with positive deltas in lime, negative in coral. (5) **Calibration block** вҖ” left-side 88 px conic-gradient dial (`1 вҲ’ brier`-filled, hue by band) with band name + brier value inside; right-side flex chip row (`N alert(s)` В· `TP K` В· `FA J` В· `Miss M` В· `H heartbeats`) + one-line summary. (6) **Event timeline** вҖ” merged alert + milestone list (60-row cap; overflow noted in caption + still present in the JSON), each row a 4-column grid `(timestamp В· icon В· message В· rel-km)` with a 3 px severity-coloured left rail. (7) **Lessons checklist** вҖ” each lesson a card with a severity-coloured left rail (rose for `рҹҶҳ/рҹ”ҙ/вҸёпёҸ`, coral for `рҹҡ·/вҡ пёҸ/рҹ”§/рҹ“ү`, lime for `рҹӣЎ/вң…/рҹ“Ҳ/рҹҹў`, sky default). New `_ECHO_CSS` block (~280 LOC) is namespaced under `.ws-echo-*` to avoid colliding with any of the existing surface CSS namespaces. **Wired into `app.py`** at `tabs[17]` next to Trip Log (so the natural flow reads `Trip Log вҶ’ list of completed trips`, `Echo вҶ’ debrief one`). When `st.session_state.trip` exists Echo debriefs it directly (works for both completed and *active* trips вҖ” handy for the "how is my current trip going?" mid-flight angle); when none does, a **`Run seeded demo trip`** button synthesises a canonical Aguada cliffs вҶ’ Baga safest journey at Sat 22:00, ticks it to completion in 30-second simulation steps so the heartbeat trace is real, stashes it in `session_state.echo_demo_trip`, and Echo composes the verdict on it вҖ” the surface is never empty on a fresh load. JSON + Markdown download buttons, plus an inline `Markdown preview` / `JSON preview` tab pair beneath the brief so a user can see the export before clicking. **README** вҖ” new headline-feature callout block inserted at the very top of the features list (so the Day-66 addition reads first) + new "Echo вҖ” Post-Trip Debrief & Counterfactual (Day 66)" full section between the StaySafe podium close-out and the Beacon section, walking through the composite formula table, the mood ladder, the corridor heat strip rendering, the four-scenario counterfactual table, the calibration TP/FA/Miss/Brier semantics + outcome-aware override, the seven-glyph lesson examples, and the JSON + Markdown export envelopes. Layout block updated with `echo.py` between `companion.py` and `theme.py`. **Validation**: end-to-end `python -c` smoke pass against the bundled Goa data produces вҖ” Aguada вҶ’ Baga safest route at Sat 22:00 ticks to completion in 8 steps (240 s sim) with 9 alerts / 5 milestones / 8 heartbeats; `compute_echo` lands `trip_score = 68.9/100 band=Caution mood=Rough`, `realized_avg=70.4 risk_km=1.38 geofence_min=4.1 (35%) exposure=61.7 event_score=76.0`, 3 scenarios (`actual exposure=62 risk_km=1.38 В· fastest exposure=55 О”trip=+11.4 В· safest exposure=56 О”trip=+12.3`) вҶ’ `best_alt=safest`, calibration `brier=0.50 band=Off tp=4 fa=0 miss=0` (the persistence artefact вҖ” outcome override doesn't fire here because the alert-window-vs-heartbeat granularity produces 4 TPs across 4 sequential predicted-active heartbeats), 4 lessons including the `рҹӣЎ safest +12 pts saving 0.30 risk-km at +10 min` upgrade pitch and the `рҹҡ· 4 min (35%) inside geofenced risk zones` Tempo deep-link, JSON serialisation 16.8 KB, Markdown 3.2 KB.
